INSERT INTO public.subscription_offers (
  offer_code,
  pricing_group_id,
  menu_item_id,
  plan_id,
  offer_kind,
  package_price,
  included_credits,
  delivery_fee_policy,
  allow_lunch,
  allow_dinner,
  requires_parent_subscription,
  description
)
SELECT
  s.offer_code,
  g.id,
  mi.id,
  p.id,
  s.offer_kind,
  s.package_price,
  s.included_credits,
  s.delivery_fee_policy,
  s.allow_lunch,
  s.allow_dinner,
  s.requires_parent_subscription,
  s.description
FROM offer_seed s
JOIN public.pricing_groups g ON g.code = s.group_code
JOIN public.menu_items mi ON mi.catalog_code = s.menu_code
JOIN public.plans p ON p.plan_code = s.plan_code
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
  SELECT 1
  FROM public.subscription_offers existing_offer
  WHERE existing_offer.offer_code = s.offer_code
);

-- ============================================================
-- 6. ORDER UPGRADES
-- ============================================================

ALTER TABLE public.orders
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS pricing_group_id UUID,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS subscription_offer_id UUID,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS current_offer_id UUID,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS parent_order_id UUID,

  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_slot TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'lunch',

  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_distance_km NUMERIC(10,2),
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_fee_per_delivery NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS original_food_total_amount NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS original_delivery_total_amount NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS food_total_amount NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_total_amount NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,

  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS is_special_request BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS special_request_reason TEXT;

-- Preserve old records as food-only historical records.
UPDATE public.orders
SET
  original_food_total_amount = CASE
    WHEN original_food_total_amount = 0
      THEN COALESCE(original_total_amount, total_amount)
    ELSE original_food_total_amount
  END,

  food_total_amount = CASE
    WHEN food_total_amount = 0
      THEN total_amount
    ELSE food_total_amount
  END
WHERE original_food_total_amount = 0
   OR food_total_amount = 0;

DO $$
BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'orders_pricing_group_id_fkey'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.orders
      ADD CONSTRAINT orders_pricing_group_id_fkey
      FOREIGN KEY (pricing_group_id)
      REFERENCES public.pricing_groups(id)
      ON DELETE RESTRICT;
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'orders_subscription_offer_id_fkey'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.orders
      ADD CONSTRAINT orders_subscription_offer_id_fkey
      FOREIGN KEY (subscription_offer_id)
      REFERENCES public.subscription_offers(id)
      ON DELETE RESTRICT;
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'orders_current_offer_id_fkey'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.orders
      ADD CONSTRAINT orders_current_offer_id_fkey
      FOREIGN KEY (current_offer_id)
      REFERENCES public.subscription_offers(id)
      ON DELETE RESTRICT;
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'orders_parent_order_id_fkey'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.orders
      ADD CONSTRAINT orders_parent_order_id_fkey
      FOREIGN KEY (parent_order_id)
      REFERENCES public.orders(id)
      ON DELETE CASCADE;
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'orders_meal_slot_check'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.orders
      ADD CONSTRAINT orders_meal_slot_check
      CHECK (meal_slot IN ('lunch', 'dinner'));
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'orders_delivery_distance_non_negative'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.orders
      ADD CONSTRAINT orders_delivery_distance_non_negative
      CHECK (delivery_distance_km IS NULL OR delivery_distance_km >= 0);
  END IF;
END;
$$;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS orders_subscription_offer_idx
  ON public.orders(subscription_offer_id);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS orders_parent_order_idx
  ON public.orders(parent_order_id);

-- ============================================================
-- 7. DELIVERY UPGRADES
-- Supports Lunch/Dinner, distance fee snapshots, extra meals,
-- snack links, and settlement of extra dinner by skipped lunch.
-- ============================================================

ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
  ALTER COLUMN unit_price TYPE NUMERIC(14,6)
  USING unit_price::NUMERIC(14,6);

ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
  ALTER COLUMN unit_cost TYPE NUMERIC(14,6)
  USING unit_cost::NUMERIC(14,6);

ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_fee NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_slot TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'lunch',
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS credit_source TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'included',
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS linked_main_delivery_id UUID,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS settles_extra_credit_id UUID;

-- Replace old unique (order_id, scheduled_date)
-- with one that allows one Lunch and one Dinner on same order/date.
ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
  DROP CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS deliveries_order_id_scheduled_date_key;

DO $$
BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_order_scheduled_slot_key'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_order_scheduled_slot_key
      UNIQUE (order_id, scheduled_date, meal_slot);
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_meal_slot_check'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_meal_slot_check
      CHECK (meal_slot IN ('lunch', 'dinner'));
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_credit_source_check'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_credit_source_check
      CHECK (credit_source IN ('included', 'extra'));
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_delivery_fee_non_negative'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_delivery_fee_non_negative
      CHECK (delivery_fee >= 0);
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_linked_main_delivery_id_fkey'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_linked_main_delivery_id_fkey
      FOREIGN KEY (linked_main_delivery_id)
      REFERENCES public.deliveries(id)
      ON DELETE SET NULL;
  END IF;
END;
$$;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS deliveries_slot_idx
  ON public.deliveries(order_id, scheduled_date, meal_slot);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS deliveries_credit_source_idx
  ON public.deliveries(order_id, credit_source);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS deliveries_linked_main_idx
  ON public.deliveries(linked_main_delivery_id);

-- ============================================================
-- 8. EXTRA DINNER CREDITS
-- Used when a regular Lunch subscriber takes an additional Dinner.
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.subscription_extra_credits (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),

  order_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES public.orders(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  delivery_id UUID NOT NULL UNIQUE REFERENCES public.deliveries(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,

  status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'due',
  food_amount NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL CHECK (food_amount >= 0),
  delivery_amount NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL CHECK (delivery_amount >= 0),
  total_amount NUMERIC(12,2) NOT NULL CHECK (total_amount >= 0),

  settled_by_delivery_id UUID REFERENCES public.deliveries(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  settled_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
  notes TEXT
);

DO $$
BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'subscription_extra_credits_status_check'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.subscription_extra_credits
      ADD CONSTRAINT subscription_extra_credits_status_check
      CHECK (status IN ('due', 'settled_by_skip', 'cancelled'));
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_settles_extra_credit_id_fkey'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_settles_extra_credit_id_fkey
      FOREIGN KEY (settles_extra_credit_id)
      REFERENCES public.subscription_extra_credits(id)
      ON DELETE SET NULL;
  END IF;
END;
$$;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS extra_credits_order_status_idx
  ON public.subscription_extra_credits(order_id, status);

-- ============================================================
-- 9. DELIVERY FEE FORMULA
--
-- Up to 1.0 km = ₹5
-- After 1km:
-- completed extra km = ₹4 each
-- remaining distance rounds upward to 100m = ₹0.30 each
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.calculate_regular_delivery_fee(
  p_distance_km NUMERIC
)
RETURNS NUMERIC
LANGUAGE plpgsql
IMMUTABLE
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_rounded_distance NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_completed_extra_km INTEGER;
  v_remaining_hundred_meters INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF p_distance_km IS NULL OR p_distance_km < 0 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Delivery distance must be zero or greater';
  END IF;

  -- Examples:
  -- 1.01km becomes 1.1km
  -- 2.01km becomes 2.1km
  v_rounded_distance := CEIL(p_distance_km * 10) / 10.0;

  IF v_rounded_distance <= 1 THEN
    RETURN 5.00;
  END IF;

  v_completed_extra_km := FLOOR(v_rounded_distance)::INTEGER - 1;

  v_remaining_hundred_meters :=
    ROUND(
      (v_rounded_distance - FLOOR(v_rounded_distance)) * 10
    )::INTEGER;

  RETURN ROUND(
    5.00
    + (v_completed_extra_km * 4.00)
    + (v_remaining_hundred_meters * 0.30),
    2
  );
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 10. ORDER FINANCIAL RECALCULATION
--
-- Active pending + delivered rows are chargeable.
-- Missed/cancelled rows are excluded.
-- A missed delivery replacement keeps the same total.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.recalculate_order_financials(
  p_order_id UUID
)
RETURNS VOID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_food_total NUMERIC(14,6);
  v_delivery_total NUMERIC(14,6);
  v_total NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_amount_received NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_balance NUMERIC(12,2);
BEGIN
  SELECT amount_received
    INTO v_amount_received
    FROM public.orders
   WHERE id = p_order_id
   FOR UPDATE;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Order not found';
  END IF;

  SELECT
    COALESCE(
      SUM(unit_price) FILTER (
        WHERE status IN ('pending', 'delivered')
      ),
      0
    ),
    COALESCE(
      SUM(delivery_fee) FILTER (
        WHERE status IN ('pending', 'delivered')
      ),
      0
    )
  INTO v_food_total, v_delivery_total
  FROM public.deliveries
  WHERE order_id = p_order_id;

  v_total := ROUND(v_food_total + v_delivery_total, 2);
  v_balance := ROUND(v_total - COALESCE(v_amount_received, 0), 2);

  UPDATE public.orders
     SET food_total_amount = ROUND(v_food_total, 2),
         delivery_total_amount = ROUND(v_delivery_total, 2),
         total_amount = v_total,
         balance_due = v_balance,
         payment_status = CASE
           WHEN v_balance <= 0 THEN 'paid'
           ELSE 'not_paid'
         END,
         updated_at = now()
   WHERE id = p_order_id;
END;
$$;

-- Keeps older functions compatible.
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.recalculate_subscription_financials(
  p_order_id UUID
)
RETURNS VOID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
BEGIN
  PERFORM public.recalculate_order_financials(p_order_id);
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 11. DELIVERY STATUS TRIGGER
--
-- Delivered:
--   Included subscription delivery consumes a credit.
--
-- Missed:
--   Normal included subscription delivery creates replacement.
--   If a missed Lunch settles a past extra Dinner,
--   NO replacement Lunch is created.
--
-- Student snack add-on:
--   moves to replacement date when linked main lunch is missed.
--   is marked delivered when linked main lunch is delivered.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type TEXT;
  v_plan_credits INTEGER;
  v_credits_used INTEGER;
  v_latest_date DATE;
  v_replacement_delivery_id UUID;
BEGIN
  IF OLD.status IS NOT DISTINCT FROM NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  IF OLD.status <> 'pending' THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Only pending deliveries can have their status changed';
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used
    FROM public.orders
   WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Order not found for this delivery';
  END IF;

  -- A successful included subscription delivery consumes one credit.
  -- Extra Dinner does not consume an included credit until settled by skip.
  IF NEW.status = 'delivered'
     AND v_order_type = 'subscription'
     AND NEW.credit_source = 'included' THEN

    UPDATE public.orders
       SET credits_used = credits_used + 1,
           updated_at = now()
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id
       AND credits_used < plan_credits
    RETURNING credits_used INTO v_credits_used;

    IF NOT FOUND THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'All credits for this subscription are already used';
    END IF;

    -- Student snack attached to this successful lunch moves to delivered.
    UPDATE public.deliveries
       SET status = 'delivered'
     WHERE linked_main_delivery_id = NEW.id
       AND status = 'pending';
  END IF;

  -- A missed normal included subscription delivery extends the plan.
  IF NEW.status = 'missed'
     AND v_order_type = 'subscription'
     AND NEW.credit_source = 'included'
     AND NEW.linked_main_delivery_id IS NULL
     AND NEW.settles_extra_credit_id IS NULL
     AND v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN

    SELECT MAX(scheduled_date)
      INTO v_latest_date
      FROM public.deliveries
     WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;

    INSERT INTO public.deliveries (
      order_id,
      menu_item_id,
      meal_name_snapshot,
      unit_price,
      unit_cost,
      delivery_fee,
      scheduled_date,
      meal_slot,
      credit_source,
      status,
      notes,
      is_auto_extension,
      replacement_for_delivery_id
    )
    VALUES (
      NEW.order_id,
      NEW.menu_item_id,
      NEW.meal_name_snapshot,
      NEW.unit_price,
      NEW.unit_cost,
      NEW.delivery_fee,
      v_latest_date + 1,
      NEW.meal_slot,
      NEW.credit_source,
      'pending',
      NEW.notes,
      true,
      NEW.id
    )
    ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date, meal_slot) DO NOTHING
    RETURNING id INTO v_replacement_delivery_id;

    -- If an attached Student snack was linked to the missed main Lunch,
    -- move it to the replacement Lunch date without adding snack charges.
    IF v_replacement_delivery_id IS NOT NULL THEN
      UPDATE public.deliveries
         SET scheduled_date = v_latest_date + 1,
             linked_main_delivery_id = v_replacement_delivery_id
       WHERE linked_main_delivery_id = NEW.id
         AND status = 'pending';
    END IF;
  END IF;

  -- If an extra Dinner was missed/cancelled, it is no longer due.
  IF NEW.credit_source = 'extra'
     AND NEW.status IN ('missed', 'cancelled') THEN
    UPDATE public.subscription_extra_credits
       SET status = 'cancelled'
     WHERE delivery_id = NEW.id
       AND status = 'due';
  END IF;

  PERFORM public.recalculate_order_financials(NEW.order_id);

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS trg_delivery_status_change ON public.deliveries;

CREATE TRIGGER trg_delivery_status_change
  AFTER UPDATE OF status ON public.deliveries
  FOR EACH ROW
  EXECUTE FUNCTION public.handle_delivery_status_change();

-- ============================================================
-- 12. CATALOG SUBSCRIPTION CREATION
--
-- Creates:
-- - Main Regular/Student subscription
-- - Full delivery schedule upfront
-- - Optional linked Student Snack Add-on
-- - Upfront food + delivery fee total
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.create_catalog_subscription(
  p_customer_id UUID,
  p_offer_id UUID,
  p_meal_slot TEXT,
  p_start_date DATE,
  p_delivery_distance_km NUMERIC,
  p_amount_received NUMERIC,
  p_payment_mode TEXT,
  p_instructions TEXT,
  p_snack_addon_offer_id UUID DEFAULT NULL
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_offer RECORD;
  v_addon RECORD;
  v_student_status TEXT;
  v_slot TEXT;

  v_delivery_fee NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_delivery_total NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_main_total NUMERIC(12,2);

  v_addon_delivery_fee NUMERIC(12,2) := 0;
  v_addon_delivery_total NUMERIC(12,2) := 0;
  v_addon_total NUMERIC(12,2) := 0;

  v_received_total NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_main_received NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_addon_received NUMERIC(12,2);

  v_main_order_id UUID;
  v_addon_order_id UUID;
  v_main_delivery_id UUID;

  v_i INTEGER;
BEGIN
  v_slot := LOWER(TRIM(COALESCE(p_meal_slot, '')));

  IF v_slot NOT IN ('lunch', 'dinner') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Meal slot must be lunch or dinner';
  END IF;

  IF p_start_date IS NULL OR p_start_date < CURRENT_DATE THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription start date cannot be in the past';
  END IF;

  IF COALESCE(p_amount_received, 0) < 0 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Amount received cannot be negative';
  END IF;

  SELECT
    so.id,
    so.offer_code,
    so.pricing_group_id,
    so.menu_item_id,
    so.plan_id,
    so.offer_kind,
    so.package_price,
    so.included_credits,
    so.delivery_fee_policy,
    so.allow_lunch,
    so.allow_dinner,
    so.requires_parent_subscription,
    so.active,
    pg.code AS pricing_group_code,
    pg.requires_student_verification,
    mi.name AS menu_name,
    mi.cost AS menu_cost
  INTO v_offer
  FROM public.subscription_offers so
  JOIN public.pricing_groups pg ON pg.id = so.pricing_group_id
  JOIN public.menu_items mi ON mi.id = so.menu_item_id
  WHERE so.id = p_offer_id;

  IF NOT FOUND OR v_offer.active = false THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Selected subscription offer is not active';
  END IF;

  IF v_offer.offer_kind NOT IN ('main_meal', 'standalone_snack') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Snack add-ons must be attached to a matching Student meal subscription';
  END IF;

  IF (v_slot = 'lunch' AND v_offer.allow_lunch = false)
     OR (v_slot = 'dinner' AND v_offer.allow_dinner = false) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'This offer is not available for the selected meal slot';
  END IF;

  IF v_offer.requires_student_verification THEN
    SELECT student_verification_status
      INTO v_student_status
      FROM public.customers
     WHERE id = p_customer_id;

    IF NOT FOUND THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Customer not found';
    END IF;

    IF v_student_status <> 'verified' THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Student subscription requires a verified Student ID/customer verification';
    END IF;
  ELSE
    PERFORM 1 FROM public.customers WHERE id = p_customer_id;

    IF NOT FOUND THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Customer not found';
    END IF;
  END IF;

  -- Calculate delivery fee for main subscription.
  IF v_offer.delivery_fee_policy = 'distance' THEN
    v_delivery_fee := public.calculate_regular_delivery_fee(p_delivery_distance_km);
  ELSE
    v_delivery_fee := 0;
  END IF;

  v_delivery_total := ROUND(v_delivery_fee * v_offer.included_credits, 2);
  v_main_total := ROUND(v_offer.package_price + v_delivery_total, 2);

  -- Optional attached Student Snack Add-on.
  IF p_snack_addon_offer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
    SELECT
      so.id,
      so.offer_code,
      so.pricing_group_id,
      so.menu_item_id,
      so.plan_id,
      so.offer_kind,
      so.package_price,
      so.included_credits,
      so.delivery_fee_policy,
      so.allow_lunch,
      so.allow_dinner,
      so.requires_parent_subscription,
      so.active,
      pg.code AS pricing_group_code,
      mi.name AS menu_name,
      mi.cost AS menu_cost
    INTO v_addon
    FROM public.subscription_offers so
    JOIN public.pricing_groups pg ON pg.id = so.pricing_group_id
    JOIN public.menu_items mi ON mi.id = so.menu_item_id
    WHERE so.id = p_snack_addon_offer_id;

    IF NOT FOUND
       OR v_addon.active = false
       OR v_addon.offer_kind <> 'snack_addon'
       OR v_addon.requires_parent_subscription = false THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Selected snack offer is not a valid attached snack add-on';
    END IF;

    IF v_offer.pricing_group_code <> 'student'
       OR v_addon.pricing_group_code <> 'student'
       OR v_offer.offer_kind <> 'main_meal' THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Snack add-on can only be attached to a Student main meal subscription';
    END IF;

    IF v_slot <> 'lunch' THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Student meal and snack subscriptions are Lunch-only';
    END IF;

    IF v_addon.plan_id <> v_offer.plan_id THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Snack add-on plan must match the main Student meal plan duration';
    END IF;

    IF v_addon.included_credits > v_offer.included_credits THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Snack credits cannot exceed main meal credits';
    END IF;

    -- Attached Student snack delivery is included/free.
    IF v_addon.delivery_fee_policy <> 'included' THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Attached Student snack offer must have included delivery';
    END IF;

    v_addon_delivery_fee := 0;
    v_addon_delivery_total := 0;
    v_addon_total := ROUND(v_addon.package_price + v_addon_delivery_total, 2);
  END IF;

  v_received_total := COALESCE(p_amount_received, 0);

  -- Payment is allocated to main plan first, then add-on.
  v_main_received := LEAST(v_received_total, v_main_total);
  v_addon_received := GREATEST(v_received_total - v_main_total, 0);

  INSERT INTO public.orders (
    customer_id,
    menu_item_id,
    order_type,
    plan_id,
    plan_credits,
    credits_used,

    pricing_group_id,
    subscription_offer_id,
    current_offer_id,

    meal_slot,
    delivery_distance_km,
    delivery_fee_per_delivery,

    original_food_total_amount,
    original_delivery_total_amount,
    food_total_amount,
    delivery_total_amount,

    original_total_amount,
    total_amount,
    amount_received,
    balance_due,

    payment_status,
    payment_mode,
    notes,
    subscription_instructions
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id,
    v_offer.menu_item_id,
    'subscription',
    v_offer.plan_id,
    v_offer.included_credits,
    0,

    v_offer.pricing_group_id,
    v_offer.id,
    v_offer.id,

    v_slot,
    p_delivery_distance_km,
    v_delivery_fee,

    v_offer.package_price,
    v_delivery_total,
    v_offer.package_price,
    v_delivery_total,

    v_main_total,
    v_main_total,
    v_main_received,
    ROUND(v_main_total - v_main_received, 2),

    CASE
      WHEN v_main_received >= v_main_total THEN 'paid'
      ELSE 'not_paid'
    END,
    p_payment_mode,
    NULL,
    NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_instructions, '')), '')
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_main_order_id;

  -- Option A: create all included meal deliveries upfront.
  FOR v_i IN 0..(v_offer.included_credits - 1) LOOP
    INSERT INTO public.deliveries (
      order_id,
      menu_item_id,
      meal_name_snapshot,
      unit_price,
      unit_cost,
      delivery_fee,
      scheduled_date,
      meal_slot,
      credit_source,
      status,
      notes
    )
    VALUES (
      v_main_order_id,
      v_offer.menu_item_id,
      v_offer.menu_name,
      ROUND(v_offer.package_price / v_offer.included_credits, 6),
      v_offer.menu_cost,
      v_delivery_fee,
      p_start_date + v_i,
      v_slot,
      'included',
      'pending',
      NULL
    );
  END LOOP;

  -- Create linked snack order + snack deliveries if selected.
  IF p_snack_addon_offer_id IS NOT NULL THEN
    INSERT INTO public.orders (
      customer_id,
      menu_item_id,
      order_type,
      plan_id,
      plan_credits,
      credits_used,

      pricing_group_id,
      subscription_offer_id,
      current_offer_id,
      parent_order_id,

      meal_slot,
      delivery_distance_km,
      delivery_fee_per_delivery,

      original_food_total_amount,
      original_delivery_total_amount,
      food_total_amount,
      delivery_total_amount,

      original_total_amount,
      total_amount,
      amount_received,
      balance_due,

      payment_status,
      payment_mode
    )
    VALUES (
      p_customer_id,
      v_addon.menu_item_id,
      'subscription',
      v_addon.plan_id,
      v_addon.included_credits,
      0,

      v_addon.pricing_group_id,
      v_addon.id,
      v_addon.id,
      v_main_order_id,

      'lunch',
      p_delivery_distance_km,
      0,

      v_addon.package_price,
      0,
      v_addon.package_price,
      0,

      v_addon_total,
      v_addon_total,
      v_addon_received,
      ROUND(v_addon_total - v_addon_received, 2),

      CASE
        WHEN v_addon_received >= v_addon_total THEN 'paid'
        ELSE 'not_paid'
      END,
      p_payment_mode
    )
    RETURNING id INTO v_addon_order_id;

    -- Snack rows attach to first 7/30 successful main Lunch credits.
    FOR v_i IN 0..(v_addon.included_credits - 1) LOOP
      SELECT id
        INTO v_main_delivery_id
        FROM public.deliveries
       WHERE order_id = v_main_order_id
         AND scheduled_date = p_start_date + v_i
         AND meal_slot = 'lunch'
       LIMIT 1;

      INSERT INTO public.deliveries (
        order_id,
        menu_item_id,
        meal_name_snapshot,
        unit_price,
        unit_cost,
        delivery_fee,
        scheduled_date,
        meal_slot,
        credit_source,
        status,
        notes,
        linked_main_delivery_id
      )
      VALUES (
        v_addon_order_id,
        v_addon.menu_item_id,
        v_addon.menu_name,
        ROUND(v_addon.package_price / v_addon.included_credits, 6),
        v_addon.menu_cost,
        0,
        p_start_date + v_i,
        'lunch',
        'included',
        'pending',
        NULL,
        v_main_delivery_id
      );
    END LOOP;
  END IF;

  RETURN v_main_order_id;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 13. SPECIAL ONE-TIME ORDER
-- One-time is optional/manual for special or valuable customers.
-- Food amount is manually approved and entered.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.create_special_one_time_order(
  p_customer_id UUID,
  p_menu_item_id UUID,
  p_meal_slot TEXT,
  p_delivery_date DATE,
  p_delivery_distance_km NUMERIC,
  p_food_amount NUMERIC,
  p_amount_received NUMERIC,
  p_payment_mode TEXT,
  p_notes TEXT,
  p_special_request_reason TEXT
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_item RECORD;
  v_regular_group_id UUID;
  v_delivery_fee NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_total NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_received NUMERIC(12,2);
  v_order_id UUID;
  v_slot TEXT;
BEGIN
  v_slot := LOWER(TRIM(COALESCE(p_meal_slot, '')));

  IF v_slot NOT IN ('lunch', 'dinner') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Meal slot must be lunch or dinner';
  END IF;

  IF p_delivery_date IS NULL OR p_delivery_date < CURRENT_DATE THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Delivery date cannot be in the past';
  END IF;

  IF p_food_amount IS NULL OR p_food_amount <= 0 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Approved special one-time food amount must be greater than zero';
  END IF;

  IF COALESCE(p_amount_received, 0) < 0 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Amount received cannot be negative';
  END IF;

  SELECT id, name, cost, active, catalog_code
    INTO v_item
    FROM public.menu_items
   WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;

  IF NOT FOUND OR v_item.active = false THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Selected menu item is inactive or unavailable';
  END IF;

  -- Student offers are not valid as special one-time orders currently.
  IF COALESCE(v_item.catalog_code, '') LIKE 'student_%' THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Student one-time orders are not available';
  END IF;

  SELECT id
    INTO v_regular_group_id
    FROM public.pricing_groups
   WHERE code = 'regular';

  v_delivery_fee := public.calculate_regular_delivery_fee(p_delivery_distance_km);
  v_total := ROUND(p_food_amount + v_delivery_fee, 2);
  v_received := COALESCE(p_amount_received, 0);

  INSERT INTO public.orders (
    customer_id,
    menu_item_id,
    order_type,

    pricing_group_id,
    meal_slot,
    delivery_distance_km,
    delivery_fee_per_delivery,

    is_special_request,
    special_request_reason,

    original_food_total_amount,
    original_delivery_total_amount,
    food_total_amount,
    delivery_total_amount,

    original_total_amount,
    total_amount,
    amount_received,
    balance_due,

    payment_status,
    payment_mode,
    notes
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id,
    p_menu_item_id,
    'one_time',

    v_regular_group_id,
    v_slot,
    p_delivery_distance_km,
    v_delivery_fee,

    true,
    NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_special_request_reason, '')), ''),

    p_food_amount,
    v_delivery_fee,
    p_food_amount,
    v_delivery_fee,

    v_total,
    v_total,
    v_received,
    ROUND(v_total - v_received, 2),

    CASE
      WHEN v_received >= v_total THEN 'paid'
      ELSE 'not_paid'
    END,
    p_payment_mode,
    NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '')
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  INSERT INTO public.deliveries (
    order_id,
    menu_item_id,
    meal_name_snapshot,
    unit_price,
    unit_cost,
    delivery_fee,
    scheduled_date,
    meal_slot,
    credit_source,
    status,
    notes
  )
  VALUES (
    v_order_id,
    p_menu_item_id,
    v_item.name,
    p_food_amount,
    v_item.cost,
    v_delivery_fee,
    p_delivery_date,
    v_slot,
    'included',
    'pending',
    NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '')
  );

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 14. REGULAR LUNCH -> DINNER SLOT CHANGE
-- Uses same credit. No extra price. Student plans are blocked.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.move_pending_delivery_to_slot(
  p_delivery_id UUID,
  p_new_meal_slot TEXT
)
RETURNS VOID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_group_code TEXT;
  v_order_id UUID;
  v_new_slot TEXT;
BEGIN
  v_new_slot := LOWER(TRIM(COALESCE(p_new_meal_slot, '')));

  IF v_new_slot NOT IN ('lunch', 'dinner') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'New meal slot must be lunch or dinner';
  END IF;

  SELECT
    d.order_id,
    pg.code
  INTO v_order_id, v_group_code
  FROM public.deliveries d
  JOIN public.orders o ON o.id = d.order_id
  JOIN public.pricing_groups pg ON pg.id = o.pricing_group_id
  WHERE d.id = p_delivery_id
    AND d.status = 'pending'
    AND d.credit_source = 'included'
    AND o.order_type = 'subscription'
    AND o.parent_order_id IS NULL;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Only pending main subscription deliveries can change meal slot';
  END IF;

  IF v_group_code <> 'regular' THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Student subscriptions are Lunch-only and cannot be moved to Dinner';
  END IF;

  UPDATE public.deliveries
     SET meal_slot = v_new_slot
   WHERE id = p_delivery_id;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 15. EXTRA DINNER CREDIT
--
-- Adds an extra Dinner while regular Lunch schedule continues.
-- Later skipped Lunch can settle oldest delivered extra Dinner.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.create_extra_dinner_credit(
  p_order_id UUID,
  p_delivery_date DATE,
  p_notes TEXT DEFAULT NULL
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order RECORD;
  v_template RECORD;
  v_extra_delivery_id UUID;
  v_extra_credit_id UUID;
BEGIN
  IF p_delivery_date IS NULL OR p_delivery_date < CURRENT_DATE THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Extra Dinner date cannot be in the past';
  END IF;

  SELECT
    o.id,
    o.order_type,
    o.parent_order_id,
    o.plan_credits,
    o.credits_used,
    pg.code AS pricing_group_code
  INTO v_order
  FROM public.orders o
  JOIN public.pricing_groups pg ON pg.id = o.pricing_group_id
  WHERE o.id = p_order_id
  FOR UPDATE;

  IF NOT FOUND
     OR v_order.order_type <> 'subscription'
     OR v_order.parent_order_id IS NOT NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Main subscription order not found';
  END IF;

  IF v_order.pricing_group_code <> 'regular' THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Extra Dinner credit is available only for Regular subscriptions';
  END IF;

  IF v_order.credits_used >= v_order.plan_credits THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription is already completed';
  END IF;

  IF EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM public.deliveries
    WHERE order_id = p_order_id
      AND scheduled_date = p_delivery_date
      AND meal_slot = 'dinner'
  ) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'This subscription already has a Dinner delivery on the selected date';
  END IF;

  -- Extra Dinner uses current next pending pack price per credit.
  SELECT
    menu_item_id,
    meal_name_snapshot,
    unit_price,
    unit_cost,
    delivery_fee
  INTO v_template
  FROM public.deliveries
  WHERE order_id = p_order_id
    AND credit_source = 'included'
    AND status = 'pending'
  ORDER BY scheduled_date
  LIMIT 1;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'No pending subscription credit is available for pricing the extra Dinner';
  END IF;

  INSERT INTO public.deliveries (
    order_id,
    menu_item_id,
    meal_name_snapshot,
    unit_price,
    unit_cost,
    delivery_fee,
    scheduled_date,
    meal_slot,
    credit_source,
    status,
    notes
  )
  VALUES (
    p_order_id,
    v_template.menu_item_id,
    v_template.meal_name_snapshot,
    v_template.unit_price,
    v_template.unit_cost,
    v_template.delivery_fee,
    p_delivery_date,
    'dinner',
    'extra',
    'pending',
    NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '')
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_extra_delivery_id;

  INSERT INTO public.subscription_extra_credits (
    order_id,
    delivery_id,
    status,
    food_amount,
    delivery_amount,
    total_amount,
    notes
  )
  VALUES (
    p_order_id,
    v_extra_delivery_id,
    'due',
    ROUND(v_template.unit_price, 2),
    ROUND(v_template.delivery_fee, 2),
    ROUND(v_template.unit_price + v_template.delivery_fee, 2),
    NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '')
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_extra_credit_id;

  PERFORM public.recalculate_order_financials(p_order_id);

  RETURN v_extra_credit_id;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 16. SKIP + EXTEND
--
-- Normal skip:
--   missed + replacement after latest date.
--
-- If oldest delivered extra Dinner is due:
--   missed Lunch settles that Dinner,
--   no replacement Lunch is created.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.skip_delivery_and_extend(
  p_delivery_id UUID,
  p_skip_reason TEXT DEFAULT NULL
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id UUID;
  v_credit_source TEXT;
  v_extra_credit_id UUID;
  v_extra_delivery_id UUID;
  v_replacement_delivery_id UUID;
BEGIN
  SELECT d.order_id, d.credit_source
    INTO v_order_id, v_credit_source
    FROM public.deliveries d
    JOIN public.orders o ON o.id = d.order_id
   WHERE d.id = p_delivery_id
     AND d.status = 'pending'
     AND o.order_type = 'subscription'
   FOR UPDATE;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Only pending subscription deliveries can be skipped';
  END IF;

  -- Find oldest delivered extra Dinner still due.
  -- It can be settled by this skipped included Lunch credit.
  IF v_credit_source = 'included' THEN
    SELECT e.id, e.delivery_id
      INTO v_extra_credit_id, v_extra_delivery_id
      FROM public.subscription_extra_credits e
      JOIN public.deliveries extra_delivery
        ON extra_delivery.id = e.delivery_id
     WHERE e.order_id = v_order_id
       AND e.status = 'due'
       AND extra_delivery.status = 'delivered'
     ORDER BY extra_delivery.scheduled_date, e.created_at
     LIMIT 1;
  END IF;

  IF v_extra_credit_id IS NOT NULL THEN
    -- No replacement row is created because the past extra Dinner
    -- now consumes this skipped Lunch credit.
    UPDATE public.deliveries
       SET skip_reason = NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_skip_reason, '')), ''),
           settles_extra_credit_id = v_extra_credit_id,
           status = 'missed'
     WHERE id = p_delivery_id;

    UPDATE public.subscription_extra_credits
       SET status = 'settled_by_skip',
           settled_by_delivery_id = p_delivery_id,
           settled_at = now()
     WHERE id = v_extra_credit_id;

    -- Extra Dinner now becomes one consumed included plan credit.
    UPDATE public.orders
       SET credits_used = credits_used + 1,
           updated_at = now()
     WHERE id = v_order_id
       AND credits_used < plan_credits;

    PERFORM public.recalculate_order_financials(v_order_id);

    RETURN v_extra_delivery_id;
  END IF;

  -- Normal missed/skip flow: trigger creates replacement automatically.
  UPDATE public.deliveries
     SET skip_reason = NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_skip_reason, '')), ''),
         status = 'missed'
   WHERE id = p_delivery_id;

  SELECT id
    INTO v_replacement_delivery_id
    FROM public.deliveries
   WHERE replacement_for_delivery_id = p_delivery_id
   ORDER BY created_at DESC
   LIMIT 1;

  RETURN v_replacement_delivery_id;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 17. CHANGE FUTURE PACK
--
-- Only same pricing group, same plan duration,
-- and same included-credit count are allowed.
--
-- This blocks 30-credit Protein <-> 31-credit pack changes.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.change_future_subscription_offer(
  p_order_id UUID,
  p_from_date DATE,
  p_new_offer_id UUID
)
RETURNS INTEGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order RECORD;
  v_new_offer RECORD;
  v_updated_count INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF p_from_date IS NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Choose the date from which the pack should change';
  END IF;

  SELECT
    o.id,
    o.order_type,
    o.parent_order_id,
    o.pricing_group_id,
    o.plan_id,
    o.plan_credits,
    o.subscription_offer_id
  INTO v_order
  FROM public.orders o
  WHERE o.id = p_order_id
  FOR UPDATE;

  IF NOT FOUND
     OR v_order.order_type <> 'subscription'
     OR v_order.parent_order_id IS NOT NULL
     OR v_order.subscription_offer_id IS NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Catalog subscription order not found';
  END IF;

  SELECT
    so.id,
    so.pricing_group_id,
    so.plan_id,
    so.included_credits,
    so.offer_kind,
    so.package_price,
    so.active,
    mi.id AS menu_item_id,
    mi.name AS menu_name,
    mi.cost AS menu_cost
  INTO v_new_offer
  FROM public.subscription_offers so
  JOIN public.menu_items mi ON mi.id = so.menu_item_id
  WHERE so.id = p_new_offer_id;

  IF NOT FOUND
     OR v_new_offer.active = false
     OR v_new_offer.offer_kind <> 'main_meal' THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Selected replacement pack is not active';
  END IF;

  IF v_new_offer.pricing_group_id <> v_order.pricing_group_id THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Regular and Student packs cannot be switched mid-subscription';
  END IF;

  IF v_new_offer.plan_id <> v_order.plan_id THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Pack changes must stay within the same plan duration';
  END IF;

  IF v_new_offer.included_credits <> v_order.plan_credits THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Cannot change between plans with different credit counts';
  END IF;

  UPDATE public.deliveries
     SET menu_item_id = v_new_offer.menu_item_id,
         meal_name_snapshot = v_new_offer.menu_name,
         unit_price = ROUND(v_new_offer.package_price / v_new_offer.included_credits, 6),
         unit_cost = v_new_offer.menu_cost
   WHERE order_id = p_order_id
     AND credit_source = 'included'
     AND status = 'pending'
     AND scheduled_date >= p_from_date;

  GET DIAGNOSTICS v_updated_count = ROW_COUNT;

  IF v_updated_count = 0 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'No pending deliveries exist from the selected date onward';
  END IF;

  UPDATE public.orders
     SET current_offer_id = p_new_offer_id,
         updated_at = now()
   WHERE id = p_order_id;

  PERFORM public.recalculate_order_financials(p_order_id);

  RETURN v_updated_count;
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 18. ONE-DAY CATALOG CUSTOMIZATION
-- Changes meal pack + note for one pending delivery only.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.set_catalog_delivery_customization(
  p_delivery_id UUID,
  p_new_offer_id UUID,
  p_notes TEXT
)
RETURNS VOID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_delivery_order RECORD;
  v_new_offer RECORD;
BEGIN
  SELECT
    o.id AS order_id,
    o.pricing_group_id,
    o.plan_id,
    o.plan_credits
  INTO v_delivery_order
  FROM public.deliveries d
  JOIN public.orders o ON o.id = d.order_id
  WHERE d.id = p_delivery_id
    AND d.status = 'pending'
    AND d.credit_source = 'included'
    AND o.order_type = 'subscription'
    AND o.parent_order_id IS NULL;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Only pending main subscription deliveries can be customized';
  END IF;

  SELECT
    so.id,
    so.pricing_group_id,
    so.plan_id,
    so.included_credits,
    so.offer_kind,
    so.package_price,
    so.active,
    mi.id AS menu_item_id,
    mi.name AS menu_name,
    mi.cost AS menu_cost
  INTO v_new_offer
  FROM public.subscription_offers so
  JOIN public.menu_items mi ON mi.id = so.menu_item_id
  WHERE so.id = p_new_offer_id;

  IF NOT FOUND
     OR v_new_offer.active = false
     OR v_new_offer.offer_kind <> 'main_meal' THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Selected meal pack is unavailable';
  END IF;

  IF v_new_offer.pricing_group_id <> v_delivery_order.pricing_group_id
     OR v_new_offer.plan_id <> v_delivery_order.plan_id
     OR v_new_offer.included_credits <> v_delivery_order.plan_credits THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'One-day pack change must stay in the same pricing group and credit plan';
  END IF;

  UPDATE public.deliveries
     SET menu_item_id = v_new_offer.menu_item_id,
         meal_name_snapshot = v_new_offer.menu_name,
         unit_price = ROUND(v_new_offer.package_price / v_new_offer.included_credits, 6),
         unit_cost = v_new_offer.menu_cost,
         notes = NULLIF(TRIM(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '')
   WHERE id = p_delivery_id;

  PERFORM public.recalculate_order_financials(v_delivery_order.order_id);
END;
$$;

-- ============================================================
-- 19. CLEAN VIEWS FOR FUTURE FRONTEND
-- Current app will still work with existing columns.
-- New app will use additional catalog columns.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW public.subscription_overview
WITH (security_invoker = true)
AS
SELECT
  o.id AS subscription_order_id,

  c.id AS customer_id,
  c.name AS customer_name,
  c.contact AS customer_contact,
  c.address AS customer_address,
  c.student_verification_status,
  c.student_id_number,
  c.student_institution,

  p.id AS plan_id,
  p.name AS plan_name,
  p.duration_days,

  pg.code AS pricing_group_code,
  pg.name AS pricing_group_name,

  o.meal_slot,

  o.subscription_offer_id AS original_offer_id,
  original_offer.offer_code AS original_offer_code,

  o.current_offer_id,
  current_offer.offer_code AS current_offer_code,

  o.menu_item_id AS original_menu_item_id,
  original_menu.name AS original_menu_item_name,

  o.plan_credits,
  o.credits_used,
  GREATEST(o.plan_credits - o.credits_used, 0) AS credits_remaining,

  o.subscription_instructions,

  o.original_food_total_amount,
  o.original_delivery_total_amount,
  o.original_total_amount,

  o.food_total_amount,
  o.delivery_total_amount,
  o.total_amount AS revised_total_amount,

  o.delivery_distance_km,
  o.delivery_fee_per_delivery,

  o.amount_received,
  o.balance_due,
  GREATEST(o.balance_due, 0) AS amount_due,
  GREATEST(-o.balance_due, 0) AS customer_credit,

  o.payment_status,
  o.payment_mode,

  counts.delivered_count,
  counts.pending_count,
  counts.missed_count,
  counts.cancelled_count,

  extra.extra_due_count,
  extra.extra_due_amount,

  next_delivery.scheduled_date AS next_delivery_date,
  next_delivery.menu_item_id AS current_future_menu_item_id,
  next_delivery.meal_name_snapshot AS current_future_menu_item_name,
  next_delivery.unit_price AS current_future_unit_price,
  next_delivery.delivery_fee AS current_future_delivery_fee,
  next_delivery.is_auto_extension AS next_delivery_is_auto_extension,

  CASE
    WHEN o.credits_used >= o.plan_credits THEN 'completed'
    WHEN next_delivery.scheduled_date IS NULL THEN 'needs_attention'
    ELSE 'active'
  END AS subscription_state,

  o.created_at,
  o.updated_at

FROM public.orders o
JOIN public.customers c ON c.id = o.customer_id
LEFT JOIN public.plans p ON p.id = o.plan_id
LEFT JOIN public.pricing_groups pg ON pg.id = o.pricing_group_id
LEFT JOIN public.subscription_offers original_offer
  ON original_offer.id = o.subscription_offer_id
LEFT JOIN public.subscription_offers current_offer
  ON current_offer.id = o.current_offer_id
LEFT JOIN public.menu_items original_menu
  ON original_menu.id = o.menu_item_id

LEFT JOIN LATERAL (
  SELECT
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE d.status = 'delivered') AS delivered_count,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (
      WHERE d.status = 'pending'
        AND d.credit_source = 'included'
    ) AS pending_count,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE d.status = 'missed') AS missed_count,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE d.status = 'cancelled') AS cancelled_count
  FROM public.deliveries d
  WHERE d.order_id = o.id
) counts ON true

LEFT JOIN LATERAL (
  SELECT
    COUNT(*) AS extra_due_count,
    COALESCE(SUM(e.total_amount), 0) AS extra_due_amount
  FROM public.subscription_extra_credits e
  WHERE e.order_id = o.id
    AND e.status = 'due'
) extra ON true

LEFT JOIN LATERAL (
  SELECT
    d.scheduled_date,
    d.menu_item_id,
    d.meal_name_snapshot,
    d.unit_price,
    d.delivery_fee,
    d.is_auto_extension
  FROM public.deliveries d
  WHERE d.order_id = o.id
    AND d.status = 'pending'
    AND d.credit_source = 'included'
  ORDER BY d.scheduled_date ASC
  LIMIT 1
) next_delivery ON true

WHERE o.order_type = 'subscription'
  AND o.parent_order_id IS NULL;

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW public.subscription_delivery_timeline
WITH (security_invoker = true)
AS
SELECT
  d.id AS delivery_id,
  d.order_id AS subscription_order_id,

  c.id AS customer_id,
  c.name AS customer_name,
  c.contact AS customer_contact,
  c.address AS customer_address,

  d.scheduled_date,
  d.meal_slot,
  d.status,
  d.credit_source,

  d.menu_item_id,
  d.meal_name_snapshot,
  d.unit_price,
  d.unit_cost,
  d.delivery_fee,

  d.notes AS customization_notes,
  d.skip_reason,

  d.is_auto_extension,
  d.replacement_for_delivery_id,
  missed_delivery.scheduled_date AS replacement_for_missed_date,

  d.linked_main_delivery_id,
  d.settles_extra_credit_id,

  o.subscription_instructions,
  o.plan_credits,
  o.credits_used,
  GREATEST(o.plan_credits - o.credits_used, 0) AS credits_remaining

FROM public.deliveries d
JOIN public.orders o ON o.id = d.order_id
JOIN public.customers c ON c.id = o.customer_id

LEFT JOIN public.deliveries missed_delivery
  ON missed_delivery.id = d.replacement_for_delivery_id

WHERE o.order_type = 'subscription';

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW public.subscription_addon_overview
WITH (security_invoker = true)
AS
SELECT
  addon_order.id AS addon_order_id,
  addon_order.parent_order_id AS main_subscription_order_id,

  addon_offer.offer_code AS addon_offer_code,
  addon_item.name AS addon_name,

  addon_order.plan_credits,
  addon_order.credits_used,
  GREATEST(addon_order.plan_credits - addon_order.credits_used, 0) AS credits_remaining,

  addon_order.total_amount,
  addon_order.amount_received,
  addon_order.balance_due,

  COUNT(*) FILTER (
    WHERE d.status = 'pending'
  ) AS pending_count,

  COUNT(*) FILTER (
    WHERE d.status = 'delivered'
  ) AS delivered_count

FROM public.orders addon_order
JOIN public.subscription_offers addon_offer
  ON addon_offer.id = addon_order.subscription_offer_id
JOIN public.menu_items addon_item
  ON addon_item.id = addon_order.menu_item_id
LEFT JOIN public.deliveries d
  ON d.order_id = addon_order.id

WHERE addon_order.parent_order_id IS NOT NULL
GROUP BY
  addon_order.id,
  addon_order.parent_order_id,
  addon_offer.offer_code,
  addon_item.name,
  addon_order.plan_credits,
  addon_order.credits_used,
  addon_order.total_amount,
  addon_order.amount_received,
  addon_order.balance_due;

-- ============================================================

ALTER TABLE public.subscription_offers ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE public.subscription_extra_credits ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

DO $$
BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_policies
    WHERE schemaname = 'public'
      AND tablename = 'pricing_groups'
      AND policyname = 'temporary_allow_all_pricing_groups'
  ) THEN

      ON public.pricing_groups
      FOR ALL
      USING (true)
      WITH CHECK (true);

      AND tablename = 'subscription_offers'
      AND policyname = 'temporary_allow_all_subscription_offers'

      ON public.subscription_offers
      FOR ALL
      USING (true)
      WITH CHECK (true);
  END IF;

    SELECT 1 FROM pg_policies
    WHERE schemaname = 'public'
      AND tablename = 'subscription_extra_credits'
      AND policyname = 'temporary_allow_all_subscription_extra_credits'
  ) THEN
    CREATE POLICY temporary_allow_all_subscription_extra_credits
      ON public.subscription_extra_credits
      FOR ALL
      USING (true)
      WITH CHECK (true);
  END IF;
END;
$$;

@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString, addDaysToDateString } from '../lib/date'
import CustomerPicker from '../components/CustomerPicker'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'
const PAYMENT_MODES = [
  { value: 'cash', label: 'Cash' },
  { value: 'upi', label: 'UPI' },
  { value: 'bank_transfer', label: 'Bank Transfer' },
  { value: 'card', label: 'Card' },
  { value: 'other', label: 'Other' },
]
function getPlanTypeFromCategory(catName) {
  if (!catName) return 'regular'
  const lower = catName.toLowerCase()
  if (lower.includes('student')) return 'student'
  if (lower.includes('addon') || lower.includes('add-on')) return 'addon'
  return 'regular'
}
function calculateDeliveryCharge(distanceKm) {
  const d = Number(distanceKm)
  if (isNaN(d) || d <= 0) return 0
  if (d <= 1.0) return 5.0
  const extra = d - 1.0
  const fullKm = Math.floor(extra)
  const remainderM = (extra - fullKm) * 1000
  const hundreds = Math.ceil(remainderM / 100)
  return 5.0 + (fullKm * 4.0) + (hundreds * 0.30)
}
export default function NewOrder() {
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orderType, setOrderType] = useState('subscription')
  const [categories, setCategories] = useState([])
  const [items, setItems] = useState([])
  const [selectedCategory, setSelectedCategory] = useState('')
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState(null)
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState([])
  const [selectedPlan, setSelectedPlan] = useState(null)
  const [planPrice, setPlanPrice] = useState(0)
  const [mealSession, setMealSession] = useState('lunch')
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
  const [distanceKm, setDistanceKm] = useState('')
  const [deliveryChargePerDay, setDeliveryChargePerDay] = useState(0)
  const [paymentStatus, setPaymentStatus] = useState('not_paid')
  const [paymentMode, setPaymentMode] = useState('cash')
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('')
  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      const [catRes, itemRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('menu_categories').select('id, name, sort_order').order('sort_order'),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name, price, category_id').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])
      if (!catRes.error) setCategories(catRes.data || [])
      if (!itemRes.error) setItems(itemRes.data || [])
    }
    load()
  }, [])
  const filteredItems = selectedCategory ? items.filter(i => i.category_id === selectedCategory) : []
  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPlans() {
      if (!selectedItem) {
        setPlans([])
        setSelectedPlan(null)
        setPlanPrice(0)
        return
      }
      const cat = categories.find(c => c.id === selectedItem.category_id)
      const planType = getPlanTypeFromCategory(cat?.name)
      
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plans')
        .select('id, name, credits, duration_days, bonus_credits')
        .eq('active', true)
        .eq('plan_type', planType)
        .order('credits')
      
      if (!error) setPlans(data || [])
      setSelectedPlan(null)
      setPlanPrice(0)
    }
    loadPlans()
  }, [selectedItem, categories])
  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPrice() {
      if (!selectedItem || !selectedPlan || orderType !== 'subscription') {
        setPlanPrice(0)
        return
      }
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plan_menu_pricing')
        .select('price')
        .eq('plan_id', selectedPlan.id)
        .eq('menu_item_id', selectedItem.id)
        .eq('active', true)
        .single()
      
      if (!error && data) setPlanPrice(Number(data.price))
      else setPlanPrice(0)
    }
    loadPrice()
  }, [selectedItem, selectedPlan, orderType])
  useEffect(() => {
    const charge = calculateDeliveryCharge(distanceKm)
    setDeliveryChargePerDay(charge)
  }, [distanceKm])
  const creditsPerDay = mealSession === 'both' ? 2 : 1
  const numDays = selectedPlan ? Math.floor(selectedPlan.credits / creditsPerDay) : 0
  const remainder = selectedPlan ? selectedPlan.credits - (numDays * creditsPerDay) : 0
  const totalDeliveryDays = orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan ? numDays + (remainder > 0 ? 1 : 0) : 1
  const totalDeliveryCharges = deliveryChargePerDay * totalDeliveryDays
  const baseAmount = orderType === 'subscription' ? planPrice : (selectedItem ? Number(selectedItem.price) : 0)
  const totalAmount = baseAmount + totalDeliveryCharges
  function resetForm() {
    setCustomer(null)
    setOrderType('subscription')
    setSelectedCategory('')
    setSelectedItem(null)
    setSelectedPlan(null)
    setPlanPrice(0)
    setMealSession('lunch')
    setStartDate(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
    setDistanceKm('')
    setDeliveryChargePerDay(0)
    setPaymentStatus('not_paid')
    setPaymentMode('cash')
    setNotes('')
  }
  function validate() {
    if (!customer) return 'Please select or create a customer.'
    if (!selectedItem) return 'Please select a menu item.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && !selectedPlan) return 'Please select a plan.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && planPrice <= 0) return 'Price not found for this plan+item. Check Supabase plan_menu_pricing table.'
    if (!startDate) return 'Please pick a delivery date.'
    if (startDate < todayDateString()) return 'Delivery date cannot be in the past.'
    if (totalAmount < 0) return 'Total amount cannot be negative.'
    return ''
  }
  async function handleSubmit(e) {
    e.preventDefault()
    setError('')
    setSuccess('')
    const validationError = validate()
    if (validationError) {
      setError(validationError)
      return
    }
    setSubmitting(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.rpc('create_order_with_deliveries', {
      p_customer_id: customer.id,
      p_menu_item_id: selectedItem.id,
      p_order_type: orderType,
      p_plan_id: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.id : null,
      p_plan_credits: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.credits : null,
      p_total_amount: totalAmount,
      p_payment_status: paymentStatus,
      p_payment_mode: paymentMode,
      p_notes: notes.trim() || null,
      p_start_date: startDate,
      p_meal_session: mealSession,
      p_delivery_charges: totalDeliveryCharges,
    })
    setSubmitting(false)
    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to log order: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }
    const planDesc = orderType === 'subscription' 
      ? `${selectedPlan.credits} deliveries over ${totalDeliveryDays} days` 
      : '1 delivery'
    setSuccess(`Order logged! ${planDesc} scheduled starting ${startDate}.`)
    resetForm()
  }
  const isAddon = selectedCategory && categories.find(c => c.id === selectedCategory)?.name?.toLowerCase().includes('addon')
  return (
    <div className="max-w-xl mx-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">New Order</h1>
      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      <Alert type="success" message={success} onClose={() => setSuccess('')} />
      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Customer</label>
          <CustomerPicker selectedCustomer={customer} onSelect={setCustomer} />
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Order Type</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'subscription'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('subscription')}
              />
              Subscription
            </label>
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'one_time'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('one_time')}
              />
              One-time {isAddon && <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">(optional add-on)</span>}
            </label>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Category</label>
          <select
            value={selectedCategory}
            onChange={(e) => { setSelectedCategory(e.target.value); setSelectedItem(null); setSelectedPlan(null); setPlanPrice(0) }}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          >
            <option value="">Select category...</option>
            {categories.map((c) => (
              <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Menu Item</label>
          <select
            value={selectedItem?.id || ''}
            onChange={(e) => {
              const item = filteredItems.find(i => i.id === e.target.value)
              setSelectedItem(item || null)
            }}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            disabled={!selectedCategory}
          >
            <option value="">Select item...</option>
            {filteredItems.map((i) => (
              <option key={i.id} value={i.id}>{i.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>
        {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedItem && (
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Plan</label>
            {plans.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">No active plans for this category.</p>
            ) : (
              <select
                value={selectedPlan?.id || ''}
                onChange={(e) => {
                  const plan = plans.find(p => p.id === e.target.value)
                  setSelectedPlan(plan || null)
                }}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              >
                <option value="">Select plan...</option>
                {plans.map((p) => (
                  <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>
                    {p.name} ({p.credits} credits{p.bonus_credits > 0 ? ` incl. ${p.bonus_credits} free` : ''})
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            )}
            {planPrice > 0 && (
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Plan price: Rs.{planPrice.toFixed(2)}</p>
            )}
          </div>
        )}
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Meal Session</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            {['lunch', 'dinner', 'both'].map((s) => (
              <label key={s} className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm capitalize">
                <input
                  type="radio"
                  checked={mealSession === s}
                  onChange={() => setMealSession(s)}
                  disabled={isAddon}
                />
                {s}
              </label>
            ))}
          </div>
          {isAddon && <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Add-ons are lunch only</p>}
          {mealSession === 'both' && orderType === 'subscription' && !isAddon && (
            <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Burns 2 credits per day. Fewer total delivery days.</p>
          )}
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">
            {orderType === 'subscription' ? 'Delivery Start Date' : 'Delivery Date'}
          </label>
          <input
            type="date"
            value={startDate}
            min={todayDateString()}
            onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Delivery Distance (km)</label>
          <input
            type="number"
            min="0"
            step="0.1"
            value={distanceKm}
            onChange={(e) => setDistanceKm(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="Enter distance in km (e.g. 1.5)"
          />
          {deliveryChargePerDay > 0 && (
            <div className="mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500 space-y-0.5">
              <p>Per day charge: Rs.{deliveryChargePerDay.toFixed(2)}</p>
              {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan && (
                <p>Total delivery days: {totalDeliveryDays} × Rs.{deliveryChargePerDay.toFixed(2)} = Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}</p>
              )}
              {orderType === 'one_time' && (
                <p>One-time delivery: Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}</p>
              )}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Status</label>
            <select
              value={paymentStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              <option value="not_paid">Not Paid</option>
              <option value="paid">Paid</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Mode</label>
            <select
              value={paymentMode}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentMode(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              {PAYMENT_MODES.map((m) => (
                <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label}</option>
              ))}
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Notes (optional)</label>
          <textarea
            value={notes}
            onChange={(e) => setNotes(e.target.value)}
            rows={2}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="Allergies, gate code, delivery instructions..."
          />
        </div>
        <div className="border-t pt-4 flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Amount</p>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-700">Rs.{totalAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">
              {orderType === 'subscription' ? `Plan: Rs.${planPrice.toFixed(2)}` : `Item: Rs.${baseAmount.toFixed(2)}`} + Delivery: Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={submitting}
            className="bg-green-600 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-md font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {submitting ? 'Logging Order...' : 'Log Order'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  )
}

Delivery Charge Formula Reverse-Engineered. Building scriptE Now.
From your examples:

≤1.0 km = ₹5 flat
1.0 km = ₹5 + ₹4 per full km + ₹0.30 per 100m (or part thereof)

Examples verified:

1.1 km → ₹5 + ₹0.30 = ₹5.30 ✅
1.5 km → ₹5 + ₹1.50 = ₹6.50 ✅
2.3 km → ₹5 + ₹4 + ₹0.90 = ₹9.90 ✅
3.0 km → ₹5 + ₹8 = ₹13.00 ✅
Step 1: Confirm SQL Was Run
You need the delivery_charges column on orders and the updated function. If you already ran the SQL block from my previous message (with ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN delivery_charges...), skip this.

If not, run this small SQL now in Supabase:

SQL

ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_charges NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (delivery_charges >= 0);

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE,
  p_meal_session   TEXT DEFAULT 'lunch',
  p_delivery_charges NUMERIC DEFAULT 0
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_credits_per_day INTEGER;
  v_num_days    INTEGER;
  v_remainder   INTEGER;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;
  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required'; END IF;

  v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes, meal_session, delivery_charges
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes, p_meal_session, p_delivery_charges
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
  ELSE
    v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
    v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);
    
    FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
    END LOOP;
    
    IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_num_days || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_remainder);
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;
