# Script E - NewOrder.jsx with auto delivery charge + one-time for add-ons

@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString, addDaysToDateString } from '../lib/date'
import CustomerPicker from '../components/CustomerPicker'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const PAYMENT_MODES = [
  { value: 'cash', label: 'Cash' },
  { value: 'upi', label: 'UPI' },
  { value: 'bank_transfer', label: 'Bank Transfer' },
  { value: 'card', label: 'Card' },
  { value: 'other', label: 'Other' },
]

function getPlanTypeFromCategory(catName) {
  if (!catName) return 'regular'
  const lower = catName.toLowerCase()
  if (lower.includes('student')) return 'student'
  if (lower.includes('addon') || lower.includes('add-on')) return 'addon'
  return 'regular'
}

function calculateDeliveryCharge(distanceKm) {
  const d = Number(distanceKm)
  if (isNaN(d) || d <= 0) return 0
  if (d <= 1.0) return 5.0
  const extra = d - 1.0
  const fullKm = Math.floor(extra)
  const remainderM = (extra - fullKm) * 1000
  const hundreds = Math.ceil(remainderM / 100)
  return 5.0 + (fullKm * 4.0) + (hundreds * 0.30)
}

export default function NewOrder() {
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orderType, setOrderType] = useState('subscription')
  const [categories, setCategories] = useState([])
  const [items, setItems] = useState([])
  const [selectedCategory, setSelectedCategory] = useState('')
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState(null)
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState([])
  const [selectedPlan, setSelectedPlan] = useState(null)
  const [planPrice, setPlanPrice] = useState(0)
  const [mealSession, setMealSession] = useState('lunch')
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
  const [distanceKm, setDistanceKm] = useState('')
  const [deliveryChargePerDay, setDeliveryChargePerDay] = useState(0)
  const [paymentStatus, setPaymentStatus] = useState('not_paid')
  const [paymentMode, setPaymentMode] = useState('cash')
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      const [catRes, itemRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('menu_categories').select('id, name, sort_order').order('sort_order'),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name, price, category_id').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])
      if (!catRes.error) setCategories(catRes.data || [])
      if (!itemRes.error) setItems(itemRes.data || [])
    }
    load()
  }, [])

  const filteredItems = selectedCategory ? items.filter(i => i.category_id === selectedCategory) : []

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPlans() {
      if (!selectedItem) {
        setPlans([])
        setSelectedPlan(null)
        setPlanPrice(0)
        return
      }
      const cat = categories.find(c => c.id === selectedItem.category_id)
      const planType = getPlanTypeFromCategory(cat?.name)
      
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plans')
        .select('id, name, credits, duration_days, bonus_credits')
        .eq('active', true)
        .eq('plan_type', planType)
        .order('credits')
      
      if (!error) setPlans(data || [])
      setSelectedPlan(null)
      setPlanPrice(0)
    }
    loadPlans()
  }, [selectedItem, categories])

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPrice() {
      if (!selectedItem || !selectedPlan || orderType !== 'subscription') {
        setPlanPrice(0)
        return
      }
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plan_menu_pricing')
        .select('price')
        .eq('plan_id', selectedPlan.id)
        .eq('menu_item_id', selectedItem.id)
        .eq('active', true)
        .single()
      
      if (!error && data) setPlanPrice(Number(data.price))
      else setPlanPrice(0)
    }
    loadPrice()
  }, [selectedItem, selectedPlan, orderType])

  useEffect(() => {
    const charge = calculateDeliveryCharge(distanceKm)
    setDeliveryChargePerDay(charge)
  }, [distanceKm])

  const creditsPerDay = mealSession === 'both' ? 2 : 1
  const numDays = selectedPlan ? Math.floor(selectedPlan.credits / creditsPerDay) : 0
  const remainder = selectedPlan ? selectedPlan.credits - (numDays * creditsPerDay) : 0
  const totalDeliveryDays = orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan ? numDays + (remainder > 0 ? 1 : 0) : 1
  const totalDeliveryCharges = deliveryChargePerDay * totalDeliveryDays

  const baseAmount = orderType === 'subscription' ? planPrice : (selectedItem ? Number(selectedItem.price) : 0)
  const totalAmount = baseAmount + totalDeliveryCharges

  function resetForm() {
    setCustomer(null)
    setOrderType('subscription')
    setSelectedCategory('')
    setSelectedItem(null)
    setSelectedPlan(null)
    setPlanPrice(0)
    setMealSession('lunch')
    setStartDate(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
    setDistanceKm('')
    setDeliveryChargePerDay(0)
    setPaymentStatus('not_paid')
    setPaymentMode('cash')
    setNotes('')
  }

  function validate() {
    if (!customer) return 'Please select or create a customer.'
    if (!selectedItem) return 'Please select a menu item.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && !selectedPlan) return 'Please select a plan.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && planPrice <= 0) return 'Price not found for this plan+item. Check Supabase plan_menu_pricing table.'
    if (!startDate) return 'Please pick a delivery date.'
    if (startDate < todayDateString()) return 'Delivery date cannot be in the past.'
    if (totalAmount < 0) return 'Total amount cannot be negative.'
    return ''
  }

  async function handleSubmit(e) {
    e.preventDefault()
    setError('')
    setSuccess('')
    const validationError = validate()
    if (validationError) {
      setError(validationError)
      return
    }

    setSubmitting(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.rpc('create_order_with_deliveries', {
      p_customer_id: customer.id,
      p_menu_item_id: selectedItem.id,
      p_order_type: orderType,
      p_plan_id: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.id : null,
      p_plan_credits: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.credits : null,
      p_total_amount: totalAmount,
      p_payment_status: paymentStatus,
      p_payment_mode: paymentMode,
      p_notes: notes.trim() || null,
      p_start_date: startDate,
      p_meal_session: mealSession,
      p_delivery_charges: totalDeliveryCharges,
    })
    setSubmitting(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to log order: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }

    const planDesc = orderType === 'subscription' 
      ? `${selectedPlan.credits} deliveries over ${totalDeliveryDays} days` 
      : '1 delivery'
    setSuccess(`Order logged! ${planDesc} scheduled starting ${startDate}.`)
    resetForm()
  }

  const isAddon = selectedCategory && categories.find(c => c.id === selectedCategory)?.name?.toLowerCase().includes('addon')

  return (
    <div className="max-w-xl mx-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">New Order</h1>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      <Alert type="success" message={success} onClose={() => setSuccess('')} />

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Customer</label>
          <CustomerPicker selectedCustomer={customer} onSelect={setCustomer} />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Order Type</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'subscription'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('subscription')}
              />
              Subscription
            </label>
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'one_time'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('one_time')}
              />
              One-time {isAddon && <span className="text-xs text-gray-400 ml-1">(optional)</span>}
            </label>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Category</label>
          <select
            value={selectedCategory}
            onChange={(e) => { setSelectedCategory(e.target.value); setSelectedItem(null); setSelectedPlan(null); setPlanPrice(0) }}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          >
            <option value="">Select category...</option>
            {categories.map((c) => (
              <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Menu Item</label>
          <select
            value={selectedItem?.id || ''}
            onChange={(e) => {
              const item = filteredItems.find(i => i.id === e.target.value)
              setSelectedItem(item || null)
            }}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            disabled={!selectedCategory}
          >
            <option value="">Select item...</option>
            {filteredItems.map((i) => (
              <option key={i.id} value={i.id}>{i.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedItem && (
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Plan</label>
            {plans.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">No active plans for this category.</p>
            ) : (
              <select
                value={selectedPlan?.id || ''}
                onChange={(e) => {
                  const plan = plans.find(p => p.id === e.target.value)
                  setSelectedPlan(plan || null)
                }}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              >
                <option value="">Select plan...</option>
                {plans.map((p) => (
                  <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>
                    {p.name} ({p.credits} credits{p.bonus_credits > 0 ? ` incl. ${p.bonus_credits} free` : ''})
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            )}
            {planPrice > 0 && (
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Plan price: Rs.{planPrice.toFixed(2)}</p>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Meal Session</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            {['lunch', 'dinner', 'both'].map((s) => (
              <label key={s} className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm capitalize">
                <input
                  type="radio"
                  checked={mealSession === s}
                  onChange={() => setMealSession(s)}
                  disabled={isAddon}
                />
                {s}
              </label>
            ))}
          </div>
          {isAddon && <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Add-ons are lunch only</p>}
          {mealSession === 'both' && orderType === 'subscription' && !isAddon && (
            <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Burns 2 credits per day. Fewer total delivery days.</p>
          )}
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">
            {orderType === 'subscription' ? 'Delivery Start Date' : 'Delivery Date'}
          </label>
          <input
            type="date"
            value={startDate}
            min={todayDateString()}
            onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Delivery Distance (km)</label>
          <input
            type="number"
            min="0"
            step="0.1"
            value={distanceKm}
            onChange={(e) => setDistanceKm(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="e.g. 1.5"
          />
          {deliveryChargePerDay > 0 && (
            <div className="mt-1 text-xs text-gray-500 space-y-0.5">
              <p>Per day: Rs.{deliveryChargePerDay.toFixed(2)}</p>
              {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan && (
                <p>{totalDeliveryDays} days × Rs.{deliveryChargePerDay.toFixed(2)} = Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}</p>
              )}
              {orderType === 'one_time' && (
                <p>One-time: Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}</p>
              )}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Status</label>
            <select
              value={paymentStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              <option value="not_paid">Not Paid</option>
              <option value="paid">Paid</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Mode</label>
            <select
              value={paymentMode}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentMode(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              {PAYMENT_MODES.map((m) => (
                <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label}</option>
              ))}
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Notes (optional)</label>
          <textarea
            value={notes}
            onChange={(e) => setNotes(e.target.value)}
            rows={2}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="Allergies, gate code, delivery instructions..."
          />
        </div>

        <div className="border-t pt-4 flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Amount</p>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-700">Rs.{totalAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">
              {orderType === 'subscription' ? `Plan: Rs.${planPrice.toFixed(2)}` : `Item: Rs.${baseAmount.toFixed(2)}`} + Delivery: Rs.{totalDeliveryCharges.toFixed(2)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={submitting}
            className="bg-green-600 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-md font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {submitting ? 'Logging Order...' : 'Log Order'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  )
}

Got it. Your delivery pricing is now clear, and I will use your examples as the source of truth.

Delivery-charge formula to implement
Distance	Charge
0–1.0 km	₹5.00
1.1 km	₹5.30
1.2 km	₹5.60
1.5 km	₹6.50
2.0 km	₹9.00
2.3 km	₹9.90
2.7 km	₹11.10
3.0 km	₹13.00
This means the rule is:

text

Up to 1 km:
₹5 base fare

After 1 km:
Each completed additional km: ₹4

Remaining 100 m after a completed km:
₹0.30 per 100 m
Examples:

text

2.3 km
= ₹5 base
+ ₹4 for the second full km
+ ₹0.90 for 300 m
= ₹9.90

3.0 km
= ₹5 base
+ ₹4 for km 2
+ ₹4 for km 3
= ₹13.00
For subscriptions, customer pays upfront:

text

Package food price
+ (delivery fee per meal × included meal credits)
Example for a 31-credit plan:

text

Food pack price: ₹3,999
Distance delivery fee: ₹9.90
Credits: 31

Delivery total = ₹9.90 × 31 = ₹306.90
Customer total = ₹4,305.90
If the customer skips a day:

text

No new delivery fee is added.
The replacement delivery uses the delivery fee already paid upfront.
Dinner Credit Rule — Correct Design
You explained an important real-world scenario.

Case 1: Customer skips Lunch and wants Dinner that day
text

Lunch plan has a pending lunch delivery today.

Customer says:
"Do not send lunch; send dinner instead."

System:
Today's Lunch delivery becomes Dinner.
No extra credit.
No extra price.
Successful Dinner consumes one existing Lunch credit.
Case 2: Customer wants an extra Dinner, but Lunch schedule continues
Example:

text

Customer has a 7-credit Lunch subscription.

14 July:
Customer receives an extra Dinner.

Original Lunch schedule continues normally.
The system creates:

text

Advance Dinner Credit
Status: Due / Unsettled

Extra food value:
Current package per-credit rate

Extra delivery value:
Customer delivery fee snapshot
Example:

text

7-meal Veg South Indian pack:
₹899 ÷ 7 = ₹128.4286 per credit

Distance fee:
₹9.90

Extra Dinner Due:
₹128.4286 + ₹9.90 = ₹138.33
Later, if customer skips a Lunch meal:

text

Skipped Lunch credit settles the previous extra Dinner credit.

Result:
- No replacement Lunch delivery is created.
- Extra Dinner due amount is removed.
- That previously delivered Dinner now counts as one original plan credit.
- Customer does not receive an extra meal overall.
If the customer never skips a Lunch meal:

text

Extra Dinner remains an additional paid meal.
The customer owes the extra meal amount.
This is the correct way to support your rule without creating duplicate credits or incorrect bills.

I will keep one-time orders visible as the last/optional section in Order Entry.

Since normal one-time pricing is paused, it will work as:

text

One-Time / Special Request

- Select customer
- Select meal/pack
- Enter approved manual selling price
- Delivery fee calculated from distance
- Add reason/note:
  "VIP customer", "requested order", "special case", etc.
This avoids accidentally charging old or incorrect public one-time prices.

Let me add a simple check: if category is "Add-ons", hide the "One-time" radio or show a warning. Actually, let's just let the business owner decide — the system supports it but they don't have to use it.

Step 1: Run This Additional SQL (Delivery Charges)
Add this to your Supabase SQL Editor:

SQL

-- Add delivery charges to orders
ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS delivery_charges NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (delivery_charges >= 0);

-- Update order creation function to accept delivery charges
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE,
  p_meal_session   TEXT DEFAULT 'lunch',
  p_delivery_charges NUMERIC DEFAULT 0
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_credits_per_day INTEGER;
  v_num_days    INTEGER;
  v_remainder   INTEGER;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;
  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required'; END IF;

  v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes, meal_session, delivery_charges
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes, p_meal_session, p_delivery_charges
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
  ELSE
    v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
    v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);
    
    FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
    END LOOP;
    
    IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_num_days || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_remainder);
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;
If you haven't run the BIG SQL from my previous message yet, run that first, then run this small addition.

Step 2: scriptD.ps1 — Updated Order Form (Real Menu + Pricing Matrix)
Save this as scriptD.ps1 in your project folder:

PowerShell

# Script D - Updated NewOrder.jsx with real menu, pricing matrix, meal session, delivery charges

@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString, addDaysToDateString } from '../lib/date'
import CustomerPicker from '../components/CustomerPicker'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const PAYMENT_MODES = [
  { value: 'cash', label: 'Cash' },
  { value: 'upi', label: 'UPI' },
  { value: 'bank_transfer', label: 'Bank Transfer' },
  { value: 'card', label: 'Card' },
  { value: 'other', label: 'Other' },
]

function getPlanTypeFromCategory(catName) {
  if (!catName) return 'regular'
  const lower = catName.toLowerCase()
  if (lower.includes('student')) return 'student'
  if (lower.includes('addon') || lower.includes('add-on')) return 'addon'
  return 'regular'
}

export default function NewOrder() {
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orderType, setOrderType] = useState('one_time')
  const [categories, setCategories] = useState([])
  const [items, setItems] = useState([])
  const [selectedCategory, setSelectedCategory] = useState('')
  const [selectedItem, setSelectedItem] = useState(null)
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState([])
  const [selectedPlan, setSelectedPlan] = useState(null)
  const [planPrice, setPlanPrice] = useState(0)
  const [mealSession, setMealSession] = useState('lunch')
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
  const [deliveryCharges, setDeliveryCharges] = useState(0)
  const [paymentStatus, setPaymentStatus] = useState('not_paid')
  const [paymentMode, setPaymentMode] = useState('cash')
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      const [catRes, itemRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('menu_categories').select('id, name, sort_order').order('sort_order'),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name, price, category_id').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])
      if (!catRes.error) setCategories(catRes.data || [])
      if (!itemRes.error) setItems(itemRes.data || [])
    }
    load()
  }, [])

  const filteredItems = selectedCategory ? items.filter(i => i.category_id === selectedCategory) : []

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPlans() {
      if (!selectedItem) {
        setPlans([])
        setSelectedPlan(null)
        setPlanPrice(0)
        return
      }
      const cat = categories.find(c => c.id === selectedItem.category_id)
      const planType = getPlanTypeFromCategory(cat?.name)
      
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plans')
        .select('id, name, credits, duration_days, bonus_credits')
        .eq('active', true)
        .eq('plan_type', planType)
        .order('credits')
      
      if (!error) setPlans(data || [])
      setSelectedPlan(null)
      setPlanPrice(0)
    }
    loadPlans()
  }, [selectedItem, categories])

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPrice() {
      if (!selectedItem || !selectedPlan || orderType !== 'subscription') {
        setPlanPrice(0)
        return
      }
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plan_menu_pricing')
        .select('price')
        .eq('plan_id', selectedPlan.id)
        .eq('menu_item_id', selectedItem.id)
        .eq('active', true)
        .single()
      
      if (!error && data) setPlanPrice(Number(data.price))
      else setPlanPrice(0)
    }
    loadPrice()
  }, [selectedItem, selectedPlan, orderType])

  const itemPrice = selectedItem ? Number(selectedItem.price) : 0
  const baseAmount = orderType === 'subscription' ? planPrice : itemPrice
  const totalAmount = baseAmount + Number(deliveryCharges || 0)

  function resetForm() {
    setCustomer(null)
    setOrderType('one_time')
    setSelectedCategory('')
    setSelectedItem(null)
    setSelectedPlan(null)
    setPlanPrice(0)
    setMealSession('lunch')
    setStartDate(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
    setDeliveryCharges(0)
    setPaymentStatus('not_paid')
    setPaymentMode('cash')
    setNotes('')
  }

  function validate() {
    if (!customer) return 'Please select or create a customer.'
    if (!selectedItem) return 'Please select a menu item.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && !selectedPlan) return 'Please select a plan.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && planPrice <= 0) return 'Price not found for this plan+item. Check Supabase plan_menu_pricing table.'
    if (!startDate) return 'Please pick a delivery date.'
    if (startDate < todayDateString()) return 'Delivery date cannot be in the past.'
    if (totalAmount < 0) return 'Total amount cannot be negative.'
    return ''
  }

  async function handleSubmit(e) {
    e.preventDefault()
    setError('')
    setSuccess('')
    const validationError = validate()
    if (validationError) {
      setError(validationError)
      return
    }

    setSubmitting(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.rpc('create_order_with_deliveries', {
      p_customer_id: customer.id,
      p_menu_item_id: selectedItem.id,
      p_order_type: orderType,
      p_plan_id: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.id : null,
      p_plan_credits: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.credits : null,
      p_total_amount: totalAmount,
      p_payment_status: paymentStatus,
      p_payment_mode: paymentMode,
      p_notes: notes.trim() || null,
      p_start_date: startDate,
      p_meal_session: mealSession,
      p_delivery_charges: Number(deliveryCharges || 0),
    })
    setSubmitting(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to log order: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }

    const planDesc = orderType === 'subscription' ? `${selectedPlan.credits} deliveries` : '1 delivery'
    setSuccess(`Order logged! ${planDesc} scheduled starting ${startDate}.`)
    resetForm()
  }

  const isAddon = selectedCategory && categories.find(c => c.id === selectedCategory)?.name?.toLowerCase().includes('addon')

  return (
    <div className="max-w-xl mx-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">New Order</h1>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      <Alert type="success" message={success} onClose={() => setSuccess('')} />

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Customer</label>
          <CustomerPicker selectedCustomer={customer} onSelect={setCustomer} />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Order Type</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'one_time'}
                onChange={() => { setOrderType('one_time'); setSelectedPlan(null); setPlanPrice(0) }}
                disabled={isAddon}
              />
              One-time order
            </label>
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'subscription'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('subscription')}
              />
              Subscription
            </label>
          </div>
          {isAddon && <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Add-ons are subscription-only</p>}
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Category</label>
          <select
            value={selectedCategory}
            onChange={(e) => { setSelectedCategory(e.target.value); setSelectedItem(null); setSelectedPlan(null); setPlanPrice(0) }}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          >
            <option value="">Select category...</option>
            {categories.map((c) => (
              <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Menu Item</label>
          <select
            value={selectedItem?.id || ''}
            onChange={(e) => {
              const item = filteredItems.find(i => i.id === e.target.value)
              setSelectedItem(item || null)
            }}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            disabled={!selectedCategory}
          >
            <option value="">Select item...</option>
            {filteredItems.map((i) => (
              <option key={i.id} value={i.id}>{i.name}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        </div>

        {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedItem && (
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Plan</label>
            {plans.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">No active plans for this category.</p>
            ) : (
              <select
                value={selectedPlan?.id || ''}
                onChange={(e) => {
                  const plan = plans.find(p => p.id === e.target.value)
                  setSelectedPlan(plan || null)
                }}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              >
                <option value="">Select plan...</option>
                {plans.map((p) => (
                  <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>
                    {p.name} ({p.credits} credits{p.bonus_credits > 0 ? ` incl. ${p.bonus_credits} free` : ''})
                  </option>
                ))}
              </select>
            )}
            {planPrice > 0 && (
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Plan price: Rs.{planPrice.toFixed(2)}</p>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Meal Session</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            {['lunch', 'dinner', 'both'].map((s) => (
              <label key={s} className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm capitalize">
                <input
                  type="radio"
                  checked={mealSession === s}
                  onChange={() => setMealSession(s)}
                />
                {s}
              </label>
            ))}
          </div>
          {mealSession === 'both' && orderType === 'subscription' && (
            <p className="text-xs text-amber-600 mt-1">Burns 2 credits per day. Fewer total delivery days.</p>
          )}
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">
            {orderType === 'subscription' ? 'Delivery Start Date' : 'Delivery Date'}
          </label>
          <input
            type="date"
            value={startDate}
            min={todayDateString()}
            onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Delivery Charges (Rs.)</label>
          <input
            type="number"
            min="0"
            step="0.10"
            value={deliveryCharges}
            onChange={(e) => setDeliveryCharges(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="0.00"
          />
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">Base Rs.5 + Rs.4/km + Rs.0.30/100m. Enter manually for now.</p>
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Status</label>
            <select
              value={paymentStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              <option value="not_paid">Not Paid</option>
              <option value="paid">Paid</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Mode</label>
            <select
              value={paymentMode}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentMode(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              {PAYMENT_MODES.map((m) => (
                <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label}</option>
              ))}
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Notes (optional)</label>
          <textarea
            value={notes}
            onChange={(e) => setNotes(e.target.value)}
            rows={2}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="Allergies, gate code, delivery instructions..."
          />
        </div>

        <div className="border-t pt-4 flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Amount</p>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-700">Rs.{totalAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
            {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan && (
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">
                Plan: Rs.{planPrice.toFixed(2)} + Delivery: Rs.{Number(deliveryCharges||0).toFixed(2)}
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={submitting}
            className="bg-green-600 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-md font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {submitting ? 'Logging Order...' : 'Log Order'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  )
}

Response B


Your menu model is now much clearer. The current simple menu_item price × credits setup must be replaced with an editable Pack Offers catalog before real orders are used.

Confirmed business rules
Regular packs
Pack	3 credits	7 credits	30-plan credits
Veg South Indian	₹405	₹899	₹3,999 / 31 credits
Veg North Indian	₹435	₹999	₹4,299 / 31 credits
Veg Protein	₹450	₹999	₹4,399 / 30 credits
Non-Veg South Indian	₹525	₹1,199	₹5,199 / 31 credits
Non-Veg North Indian	₹540	₹1,225	₹5,299 / 31 credits
Student packs — verified students only, vegetarian currently
Pack	3 credits	7 credits	30-plan credits
Student South Indian	₹300	₹679	₹2,899 / 31 credits
Student North Indian	₹330	₹549	₹3,199 / 31 credits
Student Snacks	Not available	₹420	₹1,800 / 30 credits
Also confirmed:

Student packs require verified student status.
Lunch/Dinner are normally separate subscriptions.
Lunch and Dinner have the same pack prices.
A customer receiving both lunch and dinner successfully uses 2 credits.
A lunch credit may be moved to dinner on a specific date.
A customer may pull a future lunch credit forward for dinner.
Extra credit can be added to an existing subscription and shown as due.
One-time orders are currently paused; only special/manual exceptions later.
Student standalone snack one-time order is not available.
Student snack add-on moves with the main meal when that meal is skipped.
Student snack 30-plan has 30 snack credits even when main meal has 31 credits.
Standalone snack subscription is not free delivery.
Regular and Student offers cannot be switched mid-subscription.
Delivery Pricing: One Important Ambiguity
You gave:

text

Base fare: ₹5
Less than 1 km: base fare
Per km: ₹4
Per 100 metres: ₹0.30
I understand the intent, but I must not invent the formula because these values can calculate differently.

For example, please tell me the exact delivery charge you expect for these distances:

text

0.8 km = ₹__
1.0 km = ₹__
1.4 km = ₹__
2.0 km = ₹__
2.7 km = ₹__
This lets me encode the exact formula safely.

Recommended implementation
Because the project currently does not use Google Maps distance calculation:

During customer/order setup, you enter delivery distance manually, such as:
text

2.4 km
Lunchmate calculates the delivery charge from your approved formula.
That delivery fee is saved as a snapshot for the subscription/delivery.
The customer pays:
text

Pack price + (delivery charge × successful meal credits)
For example:

text

7-credit regular plan
Meal pack price: ₹899
Delivery distance fee: ₹11.20 per delivery

Delivery total: ₹11.20 × 7 = ₹78.40
Subscription total: ₹977.40
When one meal is skipped:

text

No extra charge is added.
The replacement delivery uses that same delivery-fee amount.
The customer still receives 7 successful meals.
Confirm payment timing for delivery fees
Choose one:

text

A. Subscription delivery fees are collected upfront:
   delivery charge × total included credits

B. Delivery fees are collected per successful delivery

C. I decide manually for every customer
Lunch-to-Dinner Credit Rules
Your rule is workable, but needs three explicit actions in the app.

Action 1: Move today’s planned Lunch to Dinner
Example:

text

Rahul has Lunch delivery today.
Before delivery, he requests Dinner instead.

System:
Today’s pending Lunch row → changes to Dinner
Credits used → still only 1 after successful delivery
No extension
No extra price
This is a simple schedule-slot change.

Action 2: Pull a future Lunch credit forward to Dinner
Example:

text

Rahul normally has Lunch plan.

14 July: needs Dinner in addition to/instead of his normal schedule.
System uses his next pending Lunch credit.

15 July Lunch credit → moved to 14 July Dinner.
No new credit is created.
This is called Use Next Available Credit.

Please confirm what should happen to the original future date:

text

A. The next future Lunch delivery is moved to Dinner.
   That future date now has no lunch meal.

B. Dinner delivery is added now, but the future Lunch date is extended further.

C. Something else.
I recommend A because it uses one existing credit exactly once and does not create confusing extra rows.

Action 3: Add one extra credit to the subscription
Example:

text

Customer has 7 Lunch credits.
Customer needs one extra Dinner.

System:
+1 new Dinner delivery
+1 extra credit added
Amount becomes due
I need the price rule for this extra credit.

Choose one:

text

A. Use the current selected pack's package price per credit.
   Example:
   ₹899 ÷ 7 = ₹128.4286 meal value,
   plus delivery fee.

B. Use a separately configurable “Extra Meal Credit Price”
   for each pack.

C. You manually type the amount for every extra credit.
Recommendation: B. It is cleaner commercially. You can later edit extra-credit prices in Supabase without changing code.

Student Snack Clarification
Your flyer says:

text

I will therefore assume:

text

Student snack add-on delivery slot = Lunch only
Standalone Student snack subscription slot = Lunch only
Please confirm:

text

Student snacks are Lunch-only: Yes / No
Also, I will require verified student status for all Student offers, including:

text

Student South Indian
Student North Indian
Student Snack Add-on
Standalone Student Snack subscription
That follows your student-ID verification rule.

One-Time Orders
Since one-time orders are paused:

text

Normal order-entry screen:
Subscription only

One-time:
Hidden for now
The one-time database structure stays in place, but we should hide it from normal daily operations until you decide real exception prices.

Please confirm:

text

Hide One-time option from normal Order Entry for now: Yes / No

   0.8 km = ₹__
   1.0 km = ₹__
   1.4 km = ₹__
   2.0 km = ₹__

-- In create_order_with_deliveries:
v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;
v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
-- Create v_num_days rows
FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
  INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
  VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + v_i, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
END LOOP;
-- If remainder credits exist (e.g., 31 credits, both = 15 days @ 2 credits = 30 used, 1 remaining)
-- Create 1 extra row with credits_burn = remainder
v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);
IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
  INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
  VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + v_num_days, 'pending', v_remainder);
END IF;

Let me write the SQL script:

sql


-- Step 1: Add meal_session to orders
ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_session TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'lunch' 
  CHECK (meal_session IN ('lunch', 'dinner', 'both'));
-- Step 2: Add credits_burn to deliveries for proper credit tracking
ALTER TABLE deliveries ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS credits_burn INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 CHECK (credits_burn > 0);
-- Step 3: Update trigger to use credits_burn
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type    TEXT;
  v_plan_credits  INTEGER;
  v_credits_used  INTEGER;
  v_latest_date   DATE;
  v_credits_burn  INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;
  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used, meal_session
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used, v_credits_burn
    FROM orders
   WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  
  v_credits_burn := CASE WHEN v_credits_burn = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;
  -- On delivered: increment by credits_burn
  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN
    UPDATE orders
       SET credits_used = LEAST(credits_used + v_credits_burn, plan_credits)
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  END IF;
  -- On missed: extend for subscriptions
  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN
    IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
      SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
      IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
        SELECT MAX(scheduled_date) INTO v_latest_date FROM deliveries WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
        INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
          VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day', 'pending', v_credits_burn)
          ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
      END IF;
    END IF;
  END IF;
  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;
-- Step 4: Update create_order_with_deliveries function
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE,
  p_meal_session   TEXT DEFAULT 'lunch'
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_credits_per_day INTEGER;
  v_num_days    INTEGER;
  v_remainder   INTEGER;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;
  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;
  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required'; END IF;
  v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;
  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes, meal_session
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes, p_meal_session
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;
  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
  ELSE
    v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
    v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);
    
    FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
    END LOOP;
    
    IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_num_days || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_remainder);
    END IF;
  END IF;
  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;

Critical Business Rules Understood — Updating Schema + Order Form Now
Your menu photos and answers reveal several things my initial schema missed:

What You Told Me	What Changes
Lunch + Dinner = 2 credits/day	orders.meal_session + deliveries.credits_burn
Real prices are matrix-based (3-day ₹405, 7-day ₹899, 30-day ₹3,999 — not simple multiplication)	New plan_menu_pricing table
Student plans exist (cheaper, need ID verification later)	plans.plan_type = 'student'
Add-ons (Snacks) can be standalone or with meals	Snacks as separate category
30-day plans include +1 free (31 credits)	plans.bonus_credits
No 3-day snacks	Only 7-day and 30-day in pricing matrix
Step 1: Run This SQL in Supabase
Go to: https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/ukrztdeqzbbroowcphwk/sql/new

Paste this entire block → Run:

SQL

-- ============================================================
-- SCHEMA UPGRADE: Real Menu, Pricing Matrix, Lunch/Dinner
-- ============================================================

-- 1. Add meal session tracking
ALTER TABLE orders ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_session TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'lunch' 
  CHECK (meal_session IN ('lunch', 'dinner', 'both'));

-- 2. Add credits_burn to deliveries (1 for lunch/dinner, 2 for both)
ALTER TABLE deliveries ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS credits_burn INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1 CHECK (credits_burn > 0);

-- 3. Add plan metadata
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS duration_days INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS plan_type TEXT CHECK (plan_type IN ('regular', 'student', 'addon'));
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS bonus_credits INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;

-- 4. Create pricing matrix (exact prices from your menu cards)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS plan_menu_pricing (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  plan_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  price NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE (plan_id, menu_item_id)
);

ALTER TABLE plan_menu_pricing ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- 5. Update trigger to use credits_burn
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type    TEXT;
  v_plan_credits  INTEGER;
  v_credits_used  INTEGER;
  v_latest_date   DATE;
  v_meal_session  TEXT;
  v_credits_burn  INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used, meal_session
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used, v_meal_session
    FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  
  v_credits_burn := CASE WHEN v_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN
    UPDATE orders
       SET credits_used = LEAST(credits_used + v_credits_burn, plan_credits)
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  END IF;

  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN
    IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
      SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
      IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
        SELECT MAX(scheduled_date) INTO v_latest_date FROM deliveries WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;
        INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
          VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day', 'pending', v_credits_burn)
          ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
      END IF;
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

-- 6. Update order creation function with meal_session support
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE,
  p_meal_session   TEXT DEFAULT 'lunch'
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_credits_per_day INTEGER;
  v_num_days    INTEGER;
  v_remainder   INTEGER;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;
  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required'; END IF;

  v_credits_per_day := CASE WHEN p_meal_session = 'both' THEN 2 ELSE 1 END;

  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes, meal_session
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes, p_meal_session
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
  ELSE
    v_num_days := FLOOR(p_plan_credits::NUMERIC / v_credits_per_day);
    v_remainder := p_plan_credits - (v_num_days * v_credits_per_day);
    
    FOR v_i IN 0..(v_num_days - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_credits_per_day);
    END LOOP;
    
    IF v_remainder > 0 THEN
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status, credits_burn)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_num_days || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending', v_remainder);
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;

-- 7. Seed REAL menu data from your photos
DO $$
DECLARE
  c_reg_v UUID; c_reg_nv UUID; c_stud_v UUID; c_addon UUID;
  i_srv UUID; i_rnv UUID; i_prv UUID;
  i_srn UUID; i_rnn UUID;
  i_ssv UUID; i_nsv UUID;
  i_snack UUID;
  p3r UUID; p7r UUID; p30r UUID;
  p3s UUID; p7s UUID; p30s UUID;
  p7a UUID; p30a UUID;
BEGIN
  -- Clean old demo data
  UPDATE menu_items SET active = false;
  UPDATE plans SET active = false;
  DELETE FROM plan_menu_pricing;

  -- Categories
  INSERT INTO menu_categories (name, sort_order) VALUES ('Regular - Veg', 1) RETURNING id INTO c_reg_v;
  INSERT INTO menu_categories (name, sort_order) VALUES ('Regular - Non-Veg', 2) RETURNING id INTO c_reg_nv;
  INSERT INTO menu_categories (name, sort_order) VALUES ('Student - Veg', 3) RETURNING id INTO c_stud_v;

sql


-- Add columns to plans for duration and type
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS duration_days INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS plan_type TEXT CHECK (plan_type IN ('regular', 'student'));
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS bonus_credits INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;
-- Create plan pricing matrix
CREATE TABLE plan_menu_pricing (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  plan_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  price NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE (plan_id, menu_item_id)
);

);

  INSERT INTO plans (name, credits, duration_days, plan_type, bonus_credits, active) VALUES ('30-Day Snack', 30, 30, 'addon', 0, true) RETURNING id INTO plan_30a;

Now, let me write the response.

Got It — Your Real Menu Changes Everything (In a Good Way)
Your menu has plan-specific pricing (3-day vs 7-day vs 30-day all cost differently for the same pack), student tiers, and add-ons. The current schema assumes menu_item.price × credits, which doesn't work for your business.

Example: South Indian Veg is ₹405 for 3-day, ₹899 for 7-day, ₹3,999 for 30-day. That's not a simple multiple.

I need to add a pricing matrix table: plan + item = exact price. Then update the order form to look up prices from this matrix instead of doing math.

Step 1: Run This SQL in Supabase
Go to: https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/ukrztdeqzbbroowcphwk/sql/new

Paste this entire block → Run:

SQL

-- ============================================================
-- SCHEMA UPGRADE: Real Menu + Pricing Matrix
-- ============================================================

-- 1. Add plan metadata
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS duration_days INTEGER;
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS plan_type TEXT CHECK (plan_type IN ('regular', 'student', 'addon'));
ALTER TABLE plans ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS bonus_credits INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0;

COMMENT ON COLUMN plans.duration_days IS 'Duration in days (3, 7, 30)';
COMMENT ON COLUMN plans.plan_type IS 'regular, student, or addon';
COMMENT ON COLUMN plans.bonus_credits IS 'Extra free meals (e.g., +1 meal free in 30-day plans)';

-- 2. Create pricing matrix
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS plan_menu_pricing (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  plan_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  menu_item_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  price NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
  active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE (plan_id, menu_item_id)
);

ALTER TABLE plan_menu_pricing ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plan_menu_pricing" ON plan_menu_pricing FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- 3. Seed real data (atomic block)
DO $$
DECLARE
  cat_reg_veg UUID; cat_reg_nonveg UUID; cat_stud_veg UUID; cat_addon UUID;
  item_south_regveg UUID; item_north_regveg UUID; item_protein_regveg UUID;
  item_south_regnonveg UUID; item_north_regnonveg UUID;
  item_south_studveg UUID; item_north_studveg UUID; item_snacks UUID;
  plan_3r UUID; plan_7r UUID; plan_30r UUID;
  plan_3s UUID; plan_7s UUID; plan_30s UUID;
  plan_7a UUID; plan_30a UUID;
BEGIN
  -- Deactivate old demo data (keeps rows, hides from app)
  UPDATE menu_items SET active = false;
  UPDATE plans SET active = false;

  -- Categories
  INSERT INTO menu_categories (name, sort_order) VALUES ('Regular - Vegetarian', 1) RETURNING id INTO cat_reg_veg;
  INSERT INTO menu_categories (name, sort_order) VALUES ('Regular - Non-Vegetarian', 2) RETURNING id INTO cat_reg_nonveg;

text

menu item price × credits

text

text

Meal Pack: Veg South Indian
Plan: 7 Meals

Plan duration: 30 days

text

₹899 ÷ 7 = ₹128.43

Instead the system will store enough decimal precision internally and round only the final total:

text

₹899 ÷ 7 = ₹128.4286...
Final total = ₹899.00   ✅

text

A skipped meal has no delivery fee.

Its replacement delivery has the normal delivery fee.

Because the customer still receives the same total number of successful meal deliveries,
the final delivery charge remains:
delivery fee × total credits.

text

One day is skipped:
No ₹20 fee on skipped day

Final delivery fee still = ₹140

Important: Current App Pricing Is Not Correct for This Flyer Yet
Right now the app calculates:

text

menu item price × credits

text

Pricing group + Pack + Plan credits = fixed package price
Example:

text

Regular Vegetarian

7-meal plan = Rs.899
It is not simply a normal item price multiplied by 7.

So do not enter real paid orders yet. Your current orders are good test data, but the actual menu needs a proper editable pricing catalog.

Menu I Read From Your Images
Regular Lunch / Dinner Packs
Rates are exclusive of delivery charges.

Vegetarian

Recommended Editable Database Structure
Instead of hardcoding this in React, we will add editable Supabase tables:

text

pricing_groups
├─ Regular Lunch / Dinner
└─ Student Lunch

menu_items
├─ South Indian Pack - Vegetarian
├─ North Indian Pack - Vegetarian
├─ Protein Pack - Vegetarian
├─ South Indian Pack - Non-Vegetarian
├─ North Indian Pack - Non-Vegetarian
├─ South Indian Student Pack
├─ North Indian Student Pack
└─ Snacks Add-on

plans
├─ 3 Meals      → 3 credits
├─ 7 Meals      → 7 credits
└─ 30 Meals + 1 Free → 31 credits

plan_prices
├─ pricing_group
├─ menu_item
├─ plan
├─ selling_price
├─ delivery_charge
└─ active
This means you can change any price in Supabase later without code changes.

Critical Credits Rule: 30-Day Plan + 1 Free Meal
Because Lunchmate uses meal credits, not calendar days:

text

“30 Day Plan + 1 Meal Free”
= 31 successful meal credits
So if a customer skips five days:

text

They still receive 31 successful deliveries.
The plan simply extends further.
That is exactly compatible with your core rule.

For example:

text

South Indian Veg 30 + 1 Pack
Price: Rs.3,999
Credits: 31
The effective per-delivery value for future price changes would be:

text

Rs.3,999 / 31 = Rs.129.00 per credit approximately
If they change their future meal pack, the system can recalculate only the remaining future meal value while preserving already delivered meal history.

Response B


You are correct: Supabase deliveries table is backend data, not the daily working screen.

Your new app flow will be:

text

Today's Deliveries
→ only meals scheduled today

Subscriptions
→ one clean card per customer subscription

Open Subscription
→ that one customer's credits, meal history, missed/skipped days,
  auto-added replacement meal, payment balance, and edits
Your SQL upgrade is already done, so now add the frontend screens.

Important current behavior
With the SQL you already ran:

Single-day meal customization changes one pending delivery.
Skip & Extend copies that day's meal and note to the replacement delivery, because you selected 3B.
Change all future meals updates all pending meals from the selected date onward.
It preserves one-day notes, but it replaces the meal choice for all future pending rows. If you previously customized a meal for a single date, you can reapply that one-date meal customization afterward.
Step 1: Create scriptC.ps1
Open Notepad from PowerShell:

PowerShell

notepad scriptC.ps1
Paste this entire script into Notepad, then save it.

PowerShell

$utf8NoBom = New-Object System.Text.UTF8Encoding($false)

function Write-Utf8NoBom {
  param(
    [string]$Path,
    [string]$Content
  )

  $fullPath = Join-Path $PWD $Path
  $folder = Split-Path $fullPath -Parent

  if (-not (Test-Path $folder)) {
    New-Item -ItemType Directory -Force -Path $folder | Out-Null
  }

  [System.IO.File]::WriteAllText($fullPath, $Content, $utf8NoBom)
}

# ============================================================
# Subscriptions list page
# ============================================================

Write-Utf8NoBom "src/pages/Subscriptions.jsx" @'
import { useCallback, useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react'
import { Link } from 'react-router-dom'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

function money(value) {
  return `Rs.${Number(value || 0).toFixed(2)}`
}

function stateStyle(state) {
  if (state === 'active') return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800'
  if (state === 'completed') return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800'
  return 'bg-amber-100 text-amber-800'
}

export default function Subscriptions() {
  const [subscriptions, setSubscriptions] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
  const [stateFilter, setStateFilter] = useState('active')

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    setError('')

    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('subscription_overview')
      .select('*')
      .order('next_delivery_date', { ascending: true })

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
      setSubscriptions([])
    } else {
      setSubscriptions(data || [])
    }

    setLoading(false)
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => {
    load()
  }, [load])

  const filteredSubscriptions = useMemo(() => {
    const search = query.trim().toLowerCase()

    return subscriptions.filter((subscription) => {
      const matchesState =
        stateFilter === 'all' || subscription.subscription_state === stateFilter

      const searchableText = [
        subscription.customer_name,
        subscription.customer_contact,
        subscription.customer_address,
        subscription.plan_name,
        subscription.original_menu_item_name,
        subscription.current_future_menu_item_name,
      ]
        .filter(Boolean)
        .join(' ')
        .toLowerCase()

      return matchesState && (!search || searchableText.includes(search))
    })
  }, [subscriptions, query, stateFilter])

  return (
    <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 md:flex-row md:items-center md:justify-between mb-5">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Subscriptions</h1>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">
            One card per customer plan. Open a plan to see its full meal schedule.
          </p>
        </div>

        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={load}
          className="text-sm text-green-700 font-medium hover:underline"
        >
          Refresh
        </button>
      </div>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />

      <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-4 mb-4 grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-[1fr_180px]">
        <input
          type="text"
          value={query}
          onChange={(event) => setQuery(event.target.value)}
          placeholder="Search by customer, phone, address, meal..."
          className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
        />

        <select
          value={stateFilter}
          onChange={(event) => setStateFilter(event.target.value)}
          className="border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
        >
          <option value="active">Active subscriptions</option>
          <option value="completed">Completed subscriptions</option>
          <option value="needs_attention">Needs attention</option>
          <option value="all">All subscriptions</option>
        </select>
      </div>

      {loading ? (
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Loading subscriptions...</p>
      ) : filteredSubscriptions.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-8 text-center text-sm text-gray-500">
          No subscriptions found for this filter.
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2">
          {filteredSubscriptions.map((subscription) => (
            <article
              key={subscription.subscription_order_id}
              className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-5 shadow-sm"
            >
              <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                <div>
                  <h2 className="font-bold text-lg">{subscription.customer_name}</h2>
                  <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{subscription.customer_contact}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">
                    {subscription.customer_address}
                  </p>
                </div>

                <span
                  className={`text-xs font-medium rounded-full px-2 py-1 ${stateStyle(
                    subscription.subscription_state
                  )}`}
                >
                  {subscription.subscription_state.replace('_', ' ')}
                </span>
              </div>

              <div className="border-t mt-4 pt-4 grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-sm">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-500">Plan</p>
                  <p className="font-medium">{subscription.plan_name}</p>
                </div>

                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-500">Next delivery</p>
                  <p className="font-medium">
                    {subscription.next_delivery_date || 'No pending delivery'}
                  </p>
                </div>

                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-500">Current future meal</p>
                  <p className="font-medium">
                    {subscription.current_future_menu_item_name || 'Completed'}
                  </p>
                </div>

                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-500">Credits</p>
                  <p className="font-medium">
                    {subscription.credits_used}/{subscription.plan_credits} used
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-green-700">
                    {subscription.credits_remaining} remaining
                  </p>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4 bg-gray-50 border rounded-md p-3 text-sm">
                <p className="text-gray-500">Instructions</p>
                <p className="mt-1">
                  {subscription.subscription_instructions || 'No permanent instructions'}
                </p>
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4 flex items-end justify-between gap-3">
                <div className="text-sm">
                  {Number(subscription.amount_due) > 0 ? (
                    <>
                      <p className="text-gray-500">Customer still owes</p>
                      <p className="font-bold text-red-700">
                        {money(subscription.amount_due)}
                      </p>
                    </>
                  ) : Number(subscription.customer_credit) > 0 ? (
                    <>
                      <p className="text-gray-500">Customer credit/refund due</p>
                      <p className="font-bold text-blue-700">
                        {money(subscription.customer_credit)}
                      </p>
                    </>
                  ) : (
                    <>
                      <p className="text-gray-500">Payment balance</p>
                      <p className="font-bold text-green-700">Settled</p>
                    </>
                  )}
                </div>

                <Link
                  to={`/subscriptions/${subscription.subscription_order_id}`}
                  className="bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-green-700"
                >
                  Open Subscription
                </Link>
              </div>
            </article>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}
'@
