Write-Utf8NoBom "src/pages/SubscriptionDetails.jsx" @'
import { Fragment, useCallback, useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { Link, useParams } from 'react-router-dom'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString } from '../lib/date'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

function money(value) {
  return `Rs.${Number(value || 0).toFixed(2)}`
}

const STATUS_STYLE = {
  pending: 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800',
  delivered: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800',
  missed: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800',
  cancelled: 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-700',
}

export default function SubscriptionDetails() {
  const { orderId } = useParams()

  const [overview, setOverview] = useState(null)
  const [timeline, setTimeline] = useState([])
  const [menuItems, setMenuItems] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [busy, setBusy] = useState('')
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('')

  const [instructions, setInstructions] = useState('')
  const [futureDate, setFutureDate] = useState(todayDateString())
  const [futureMealId, setFutureMealId] = useState('')
  const [amountReceived, setAmountReceived] = useState('0')
  const [paymentMode, setPaymentMode] = useState('cash')

  const [editingDeliveryId, setEditingDeliveryId] = useState(null)
  const [oneDayMealId, setOneDayMealId] = useState('')
  const [oneDayNotes, setOneDayNotes] = useState('')

  const [skippingDeliveryId, setSkippingDeliveryId] = useState(null)
  const [skipReason, setSkipReason] = useState('')

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    setError('')

    const [overviewResult, timelineResult, menuResult] = await Promise.all([
      supabase
        .from('subscription_overview')
        .select('*')
        .eq('subscription_order_id', orderId)
        .maybeSingle(),

      supabase
        .from('subscription_delivery_timeline')
        .select('*')
        .eq('subscription_order_id', orderId)
        .order('scheduled_date', { ascending: true }),

      supabase
        .from('menu_items')
        .select('id, name, price')
        .eq('active', true)
        .order('name'),
    ])

    if (overviewResult.error) {
      setError(overviewResult.error.message)
    } else if (!overviewResult.data) {
      setError('Subscription not found.')
    } else {
      const data = overviewResult.data
      setOverview(data)
      setInstructions(data.subscription_instructions || '')
      setFutureDate(data.next_delivery_date || todayDateString())
      setFutureMealId(data.current_future_menu_item_id || '')
      setAmountReceived(String(data.amount_received ?? 0))
      setPaymentMode(data.payment_mode || 'cash')
    }

    if (timelineResult.error) {
      setError((current) => current || timelineResult.error.message)
      setTimeline([])
    } else {
      setTimeline(timelineResult.data || [])
    }

    if (menuResult.error) {
      setError((current) => current || menuResult.error.message)
      setMenuItems([])
    } else {
      setMenuItems(menuResult.data || [])
    }

    setLoading(false)
  }, [orderId])

  useEffect(() => {
    load()
  }, [load])

  async function execute(actionKey, request, message) {
    setBusy(actionKey)
    setError('')
    setSuccess('')

    const { error } = await request()

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
    } else {
      setSuccess(message)
      await load()
    }

    setBusy('')
  }

  function saveInstructions() {
    execute(
      'instructions',
      () =>
        supabase.rpc('set_subscription_instructions', {
          p_order_id: orderId,
          p_instructions: instructions.trim() || null,
        }),
      'Subscription instructions updated.'
    )
  }

  function saveFutureMeal() {
    if (!futureDate || !futureMealId) {
      setError('Select both a meal and the date from which it should apply.')
      return
    }

    execute(
      'future-meal',
      () =>
        supabase.rpc('change_future_subscription_meal', {
          p_order_id: orderId,
          p_from_date: futureDate,
          p_menu_item_id: futureMealId,
        }),
      'Future pending meals were updated and subscription total was recalculated.'
    )
  }

  function startOneDayEdit(delivery) {
    setEditingDeliveryId(delivery.delivery_id)
    setOneDayMealId(delivery.menu_item_id)
    setOneDayNotes(delivery.customization_notes || '')
    setSkippingDeliveryId(null)
  }

  function saveOneDayCustomization(delivery) {
    if (!oneDayMealId) {
      setError('Select a meal for this delivery.')
      return
    }

    execute(
      `one-day-${delivery.delivery_id}`,
      () =>
        supabase.rpc('set_delivery_customization', {
          p_delivery_id: delivery.delivery_id,
          p_menu_item_id: oneDayMealId,
          p_notes: oneDayNotes.trim() || null,
        }),
      `Customization saved for ${delivery.scheduled_date}.`
    )

    setEditingDeliveryId(null)
  }

  function openSkip(deliveryId) {
    setSkippingDeliveryId(deliveryId)
    setSkipReason('')
    setEditingDeliveryId(null)
  }

  function confirmSkip(delivery) {
    const confirmed = window.confirm(
      `Skip ${delivery.scheduled_date}? No credit will be used. A replacement delivery will be added after the current final schedule date.`
    )

    if (!confirmed) return

    execute(
      `skip-${delivery.delivery_id}`,
      () =>
        supabase.rpc('skip_delivery_and_extend', {
          p_delivery_id: delivery.delivery_id,
          p_skip_reason: skipReason.trim() || null,
        }),
      'Delivery skipped. A replacement pending meal was added at the end of the plan.'
    )

    setSkippingDeliveryId(null)
    setSkipReason('')
  }

  function saveAmountReceived() {
    const parsedAmount = Number(amountReceived)

    if (Number.isNaN(parsedAmount) || parsedAmount < 0) {
      setError('Enter a valid amount received.')
      return
    }

    execute(
      'payment',
      () =>
        supabase.rpc('set_order_amount_received', {
          p_order_id: orderId,
          p_amount_received: parsedAmount,
          p_payment_mode: paymentMode,
        }),
      'Amount received and payment balance updated.'
    )
  }

  if (loading) {
    return <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Loading subscription...</p>
  }

  if (!overview) {
    return (
      <div>
        <Alert type="error" message={error || 'Subscription not found.'} />
        <Link to="/subscriptions" className="text-sm text-green-700 hover:underline">
          Back to subscriptions
        </Link>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
      <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 md:flex-row md:items-start md:justify-between mb-5">
        <div>
          <Link to="/subscriptions" className="text-sm text-green-700 hover:underline">
            Back to subscriptions
          </Link>

          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold mt-2">{overview.customer_name}</h1>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{overview.customer_contact}</p>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">{overview.customer_address}</p>
        </div>

        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={load}
          className="text-sm text-green-700 font-medium hover:underline"
        >
          Refresh
        </button>
      </div>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      <Alert type="success" message={success} onClose={() => setSuccess('')} />

      <section className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-5 mb-4">
        <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-4">
          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">Plan</p>
            <p className="font-bold mt-1">{overview.plan_name}</p>
          </div>

          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">Original meal</p>
            <p className="font-bold mt-1">{overview.original_menu_item_name}</p>
          </div>

          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">Current next meal</p>
            <p className="font-bold mt-1">
              {overview.current_future_menu_item_name || 'Plan completed'}
            </p>
          </div>

          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">Next delivery</p>
            <p className="font-bold mt-1">
              {overview.next_delivery_date || 'No pending delivery'}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="border-t mt-5 pt-5 grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-4">
          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">Credits used</p>
            <p className="text-xl font-bold mt-1">
              {overview.credits_used}/{overview.plan_credits}
            </p>
          </div>

          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">Credits remaining</p>
            <p className="text-xl font-bold text-green-700 mt-1">
              {overview.credits_remaining}
            </p>
          </div>

          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">Missed/skipped</p>
            <p className="text-xl font-bold text-red-700 mt-1">
              {overview.missed_count}
            </p>
          </div>

          <div>
            <p className="text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">Pending meals</p>
            <p className="text-xl font-bold text-amber-700 mt-1">
              {overview.pending_count}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>

      <div className="grid gap-4 lg:grid-cols-2 mb-4">
        <section className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-5">
          <h2 className="font-bold">Permanent subscription instructions</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">
            These apply to the whole plan, such as less oil, no onion, or call first.
          </p>

          <textarea
            value={instructions}
            onChange={(event) => setInstructions(event.target.value)}
            rows={4}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm mt-3"
            placeholder="Less oil, no onion, call before delivery..."
          />

          <button
            type="button"
            disabled={busy === 'instructions'}
            onClick={saveInstructions}
            className="mt-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {busy === 'instructions' ? 'Saving...' : 'Save Instructions'}
          </button>
        </section>

        <section className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-5">
          <h2 className="font-bold">Payment and revised price</h2>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 mt-3 text-sm">
            <div>
              <p className="text-gray-500">Original total</p>
              <p className="font-bold">{money(overview.original_total_amount)}</p>
            </div>

            <div>
              <p className="text-gray-500">Current revised total</p>
              <p className="font-bold">{money(overview.revised_total_amount)}</p>
            </div>

            <div>
              <p className="text-gray-500">Customer still owes</p>
              <p className="font-bold text-red-700">{money(overview.amount_due)}</p>
            </div>

            <div>
              <p className="text-gray-500">Customer credit/refund</p>
              <p className="font-bold text-blue-700">
                {money(overview.customer_credit)}
              </p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 mt-4">
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Total received so far</label>
              <input
                type="number"
                min="0"
                step="0.01"
                value={amountReceived}
                onChange={(event) => setAmountReceived(event.target.value)}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              />
            </div>

            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment mode</label>
              <select
                value={paymentMode}
                onChange={(event) => setPaymentMode(event.target.value)}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              >
                <option value="cash">Cash</option>
                <option value="upi">UPI</option>
                <option value="bank_transfer">Bank Transfer</option>
                <option value="card">Card</option>
                <option value="other">Other</option>
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>

          <button
            type="button"
            disabled={busy === 'payment'}
            onClick={saveAmountReceived}
            className="mt-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {busy === 'payment' ? 'Saving...' : 'Save Payment Amount'}
          </button>
        </section>
      </div>

      <section className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-5 mb-4">
        <h2 className="font-bold">Change meal for future pending deliveries</h2>
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">
          This changes every pending meal from the selected date onward and recalculates the subscription price.
          One-day notes remain, but meal choices can be customized again afterward if needed.
        </p>

        <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-3 mt-4">
          <input
            type="date"
            min={todayDateString()}
            value={futureDate}
            onChange={(event) => setFutureDate(event.target.value)}
            className="border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />

          <select
            value={futureMealId}
            onChange={(event) => setFutureMealId(event.target.value)}
            className="border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          >
            <option value="">Select future meal...</option>
            {menuItems.map((item) => (
              <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>
                {item.name} - {money(item.price)}
              </option>
            ))}
          </select>

          <button
            type="button"
            disabled={busy === 'future-meal'}
            onClick={saveFutureMeal}
            className="bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {busy === 'future-meal' ? 'Updating...' : 'Update Future Meals'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </section>

      <section className="bg-white border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
        <div className="p-5 border-b">
          <h2 className="font-bold">Delivery schedule and history</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">
            Delivered and missed rows are history. Only pending rows can be changed or skipped.
          </p>
        </div>

        <div className="overflow-x-auto">
          <table className="w-full text-sm">
            <thead className="bg-gray-50 text-left text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">
              <tr>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Date</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Status</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Meal</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Price</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">One-day note</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Schedule info</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right">Actions</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>

            <tbody>
              {timeline.map((delivery) => (
                <Fragment key={delivery.delivery_id}>
                  <tr className="border-t align-top">
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 font-medium whitespace-nowrap">
                      {delivery.scheduled_date}
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <span
                        className={`text-xs font-medium rounded-full px-2 py-1 ${
                          STATUS_STYLE[delivery.status] || 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-700'
                        }`}
                      >
                        {delivery.status}
                      </span>
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <p className="font-medium">{delivery.meal_name_snapshot}</p>
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3 whitespace-nowrap">
                      {money(delivery.unit_price)}
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3 max-w-xs">
                      {delivery.customization_notes || '-'}
                      {delivery.skip_reason && (
                        <p className="text-xs text-red-700 mt-1">
                          Skip reason: {delivery.skip_reason}
                        </p>
                      )}
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      {delivery.is_auto_extension ? (
                        <span className="text-xs text-blue-700">
                          Replacement for missed {delivery.replacement_for_missed_date}
                        </span>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">Original schedule</span>
                      )}
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right whitespace-nowrap">
                      {delivery.status === 'pending' ? (
                        <div className="flex justify-end gap-2">
                          <button
                            type="button"
                            onClick={() => startOneDayEdit(delivery)}
                            className="border rounded-md px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-gray-50"
                          >
                            Customize
                          </button>

                          <button
                            type="button"
                            onClick={() => openSkip(delivery.delivery_id)}
                            className="bg-red-600 text-white rounded-md px-3 py-1.5 text-xs hover:bg-red-700"
                          >
                            Skip & Extend
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">Finalized</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                  </tr>

                  {editingDeliveryId === delivery.delivery_id && (
                    <tr className="border-t bg-green-50">
                      <td colSpan="7" className="p-4">
                        <p className="font-medium text-sm mb-3">
                          Customize {delivery.scheduled_date}
                        </p>

                        <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-[1fr_2fr_auto_auto]">
                          <select
                            value={oneDayMealId}
                            onChange={(event) => setOneDayMealId(event.target.value)}
                            className="border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
                          >
                            <option value="">Select meal...</option>
                            {menuItems.map((item) => (
                              <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>
                                {item.name} - {money(item.price)}
                              </option>
                            ))}
                          </select>

                          <input
                            type="text"
                            value={oneDayNotes}
                            onChange={(event) => setOneDayNotes(event.target.value)}
                            placeholder="One-day note, e.g. no rice / extra salad"
                            className="border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
                          />

                          <button
                            type="button"
                            disabled={busy === `one-day-${delivery.delivery_id}`}
                            onClick={() => saveOneDayCustomization(delivery)}
                            className="bg-green-600 text-white rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Save
                          </button>

                          <button
                            type="button"
                            onClick={() => setEditingDeliveryId(null)}
                            className="border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
                          >
                            Cancel
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  )}

                  {skippingDeliveryId === delivery.delivery_id && (
                    <tr className="border-t bg-red-50">
                      <td colSpan="7" className="p-4">
                        <p className="font-medium text-sm">
                          Skip {delivery.scheduled_date} and extend this plan
                        </p>
                        <p className="text-xs text-gray-600 mt-1">
                          The same meal and one-day note will be copied to the replacement delivery.
                          No credit will be deducted.
                        </p>

                        <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row gap-3 mt-3">
                          <input
                            type="text"
                            value={skipReason}
                            onChange={(event) => setSkipReason(event.target.value)}
                            placeholder="Optional skip reason, e.g. customer travelling"
                            className="flex-1 border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
                          />

                          <button
                            type="button"
                            disabled={busy === `skip-${delivery.delivery_id}`}
                            onClick={() => confirmSkip(delivery)}
                            className="bg-red-600 text-white rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Confirm Skip & Extend
                          </button>

                          <button
                            type="button"
                            onClick={() => setSkippingDeliveryId(null)}
                            className="border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
                          >
                            Cancel
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      </td>
                    </tr>
                  )}
                </Fragment>
              ))}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </section>
    </div>
  )
}
'@

# ============================================================
# Improved Today's Deliveries page
# Shows actual customized delivery meal, not only original order meal.
# ============================================================

Write-Utf8NoBom "src/pages/Deliveries.jsx" @'
import { useCallback, useEffect, useState } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString } from '../lib/date'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const STATUS_STYLES = {
  pending: 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800',
  delivered: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800',
  missed: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800',
  cancelled: 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600',
}

function money(value) {
  return `Rs.${Number(value || 0).toFixed(2)}`
}

export default function Deliveries() {
  const [deliveries, setDeliveries] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [updatingId, setUpdatingId] = useState(null)

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    setError('')

    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('deliveries')
      .select(`
        id,
        scheduled_date,
        status,
        notes,
        meal_name_snapshot,
        unit_price,
        is_auto_extension,
        orders (
          id,
          order_type,
          plan_credits,
          credits_used,
          subscription_instructions,
          customers ( name, contact, address )
        )
      `)
      .eq('scheduled_date', todayDateString())
      .order('id')

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
      setDeliveries([])
    } else {
      setDeliveries(data || [])
    }

    setLoading(false)
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => {
    load()
  }, [load])

  async function updateStatus(delivery, newStatus) {
    const order = delivery.orders
    const isSubscription = order?.order_type === 'subscription'

    if (
      newStatus === 'missed' &&
      isSubscription &&
      !window.confirm(
        'Skip this subscription delivery? No credit will be used and the plan will extend automatically.'
      )
    ) {
      return
    }

    setUpdatingId(delivery.id)
    setError('')

    const result =
      newStatus === 'missed' && isSubscription
        ? await supabase.rpc('skip_delivery_and_extend', {
            p_delivery_id: delivery.id,
            p_skip_reason: null,
          })
        : await supabase
            .from('deliveries')
            .update({ status: newStatus })
            .eq('id', delivery.id)

    if (result.error) {
      setError(`Failed to update delivery: ${result.error.message}`)
    } else {
      await load()
    }

    setUpdatingId(null)
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Today's Deliveries</h1>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">
            Only meals scheduled for today are shown here.
          </p>
        </div>

        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={load}
          className="text-sm text-green-700 font-medium hover:underline"
        >
          Refresh
        </button>
      </div>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />

      {loading ? (
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">Loading deliveries...</p>
      ) : deliveries.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-8 text-center text-sm text-gray-500">
          No deliveries scheduled for today.
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg overflow-x-auto">
          <table className="w-full text-sm">
            <thead className="bg-gray-50 text-left text-xs uppercase text-gray-500">
              <tr>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Customer</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Meal for today</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Plan / credits</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Instructions</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3">Status</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-3 text-right">Actions</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>

            <tbody>
              {deliveries.map((delivery) => {
                const order = delivery.orders
                const customer = order?.customers
                const isPending = delivery.status === 'pending'
                const isSubscription = order?.order_type === 'subscription'

                return (
                  <tr key={delivery.id} className="border-t align-top">
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <p className="font-medium">{customer?.name || '-'}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{customer?.contact || ''}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1">{customer?.address || ''}</p>
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <p className="font-medium">{delivery.meal_name_snapshot || '-'}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{money(delivery.unit_price)}</p>

                      {delivery.notes && (
                        <p className="text-xs text-blue-700 mt-1">
                          Today note: {delivery.notes}
                        </p>
                      )}

                      {delivery.is_auto_extension && (
                        <p className="text-xs text-purple-700 mt-1">
                          Auto-extension replacement
                        </p>
                      )}
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      {isSubscription ? (
                        <>
                          <p className="font-medium">Subscription</p>
                          <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">
                            {order.credits_used}/{order.plan_credits} used
                          </p>
                          <p className="text-xs text-green-700">
                            {Math.max(order.plan_credits - order.credits_used, 0)} remaining
                          </p>
                        </>
                      ) : (
                        <span>One-time</span>
                      )}
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3 max-w-xs text-xs text-gray-600">
                      {order?.subscription_instructions || '-'}
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <span
                        className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${
                          STATUS_STYLES[delivery.status]
                        }`}
                      >
                        {delivery.status}
                      </span>
                    </td>

                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                      {isPending ? (
                        <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
                          <button
                            type="button"
                            disabled={updatingId === delivery.id}
                            onClick={() => updateStatus(delivery, 'delivered')}
                            className="bg-green-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Delivered
                          </button>

                          <button
                            type="button"
                            disabled={updatingId === delivery.id}
                            onClick={() => updateStatus(delivery, 'missed')}
                            className="bg-red-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            {isSubscription ? 'Skip & Extend' : 'Missed'}
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">Finalized</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )
              })}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

Response B


Correct decision. We will support:

A: permanent subscription instructions
B: one-day meal/customization notes
C: change meal for all future pending deliveries
D: change meal for one date only
E: skip a future date and auto-extend
Price Option B: meal changes automatically revise the subscription amount
Payment Option 2A: track amount_received and signed balance_due
Skip Option 3B: if a customized delivery is skipped, its replacement repeats the same custom meal and note
Important behavior after this upgrade
Example:

text

Original:
7 × Non-Veg Thali at Rs.150 = Rs.1,050

Delivered:
13 Jul → Non-Veg Thali → Rs.150

Future meal changed:
14–19 Jul → Veg Thali → Rs.120 each

Revised subscription total:
Rs.150 + (6 × Rs.120) = Rs.870
If the customer already paid Rs.1,050:

text

Amount received: Rs.1,050
Revised total:   Rs.870
Balance due:     -Rs.180

Meaning: customer has Rs.180 credit/refund due.
If a one-day custom meal is skipped:

text

15 Jul → Green Salad, no dressing → missed
20 Jul → Green Salad, no dressing → replacement pending
The replacement preserves the selected custom meal and note because you chose 3B.

Run This SQL Upgrade in Supabase
Open your SQL editor:

text

https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/ukrztdeqzbbroowcphwk/sql/new
Paste the entire block below and click Run.

This preserves your existing customers, orders, and deliveries. It upgrades the schema and replaces the old delivery trigger/RPC safely.

SQL

BEGIN;

-- ============================================================
-- LUNCHMATE OS: Subscription workspace + customization upgrade
-- ============================================================

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 1. Upgrade ORDERS
-- ------------------------------------------------------------

ALTER TABLE public.orders
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS subscription_instructions TEXT,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS original_total_amount NUMERIC(10,2),
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS amount_received NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
    CHECK (amount_received >= 0),
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS balance_due NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now();

-- Preserve historical original totals.
-- Existing paid orders are assumed to have received their original total,
-- because the old schema only had paid / not_paid.
UPDATE public.orders
SET
  original_total_amount = COALESCE(original_total_amount, total_amount),
  amount_received = CASE
    WHEN amount_received = 0 AND payment_status = 'paid' THEN total_amount
    ELSE amount_received
  END,
  balance_due = total_amount - CASE
    WHEN amount_received = 0 AND payment_status = 'paid' THEN total_amount
    ELSE amount_received
  END,
  updated_at = now();

ALTER TABLE public.orders
  ALTER COLUMN original_total_amount SET NOT NULL;

-- Permanent subscription instructions:
-- preserve existing subscription order notes as instructions.
UPDATE public.orders
SET subscription_instructions = notes
WHERE order_type = 'subscription'
  AND subscription_instructions IS NULL
  AND NULLIF(trim(COALESCE(notes, '')), '') IS NOT NULL;

-- One-time orders do not use credits.
-- This corrects any old test data where a one-time delivered order
-- accidentally incremented credits_used through the old trigger.
UPDATE public.orders
SET credits_used = 0
WHERE order_type = 'one_time'
  AND credits_used <> 0;


-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 2. Upgrade DELIVERIES
-- Each delivery gets its own meal/price snapshot.
-- This protects history when meal prices or names change later.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------

ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS menu_item_id UUID,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS meal_name_snapshot TEXT,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS unit_price NUMERIC(10,2),
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS unit_cost NUMERIC(10,2),
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS is_auto_extension BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS replacement_for_delivery_id UUID,
  ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS skip_reason TEXT;

-- Backfill all existing delivery rows using their order's original meal.
UPDATE public.deliveries d
SET
  menu_item_id = COALESCE(d.menu_item_id, o.menu_item_id),
  meal_name_snapshot = COALESCE(d.meal_name_snapshot, mi.name),
  unit_price = COALESCE(
    d.unit_price,
    CASE
      WHEN o.order_type = 'subscription' AND o.plan_credits > 0
        THEN ROUND(o.total_amount / o.plan_credits, 2)
      ELSE o.total_amount
    END
  ),
  unit_cost = COALESCE(d.unit_cost, mi.cost)
FROM public.orders o
JOIN public.menu_items mi ON mi.id = o.menu_item_id
WHERE d.order_id = o.id;

ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
  ALTER COLUMN menu_item_id SET NOT NULL,
  ALTER COLUMN meal_name_snapshot SET NOT NULL,
  ALTER COLUMN unit_price SET NOT NULL,
  ALTER COLUMN unit_cost SET NOT NULL;

DO $$
BEGIN
  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_menu_item_id_fkey'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_menu_item_id_fkey
      FOREIGN KEY (menu_item_id)
      REFERENCES public.menu_items(id)
      ON DELETE RESTRICT;
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_replacement_for_delivery_id_fkey'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_replacement_for_delivery_id_fkey
      FOREIGN KEY (replacement_for_delivery_id)
      REFERENCES public.deliveries(id)
      ON DELETE SET NULL;
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_unit_price_non_negative'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_unit_price_non_negative
      CHECK (unit_price >= 0);
  END IF;

  IF NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM pg_constraint
    WHERE conname = 'deliveries_unit_cost_non_negative'
  ) THEN
    ALTER TABLE public.deliveries
      ADD CONSTRAINT deliveries_unit_cost_non_negative
      CHECK (unit_cost >= 0);
  END IF;
END;
$$;

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_deliveries_menu_item_id
  ON public.deliveries(menu_item_id);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_deliveries_replacement_for_delivery_id
  ON public.deliveries(replacement_for_delivery_id);


-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 3. Recalculate subscription financial total
--
-- Revised total =
-- delivered meal prices + pending scheduled meal prices
--
-- Missed and cancelled deliveries are excluded.
-- A missed delivery creates a replacement pending delivery,
-- so the customer is never charged twice for a missed meal.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.recalculate_subscription_financials(
  p_order_id UUID
)
RETURNS VOID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type TEXT;
  v_amount_received NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_revised_total NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_balance NUMERIC(10,2);
BEGIN
  SELECT order_type, amount_received
    INTO v_order_type, v_amount_received
    FROM public.orders
   WHERE id = p_order_id
   FOR UPDATE;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Order not found';
  END IF;

  IF v_order_type <> 'subscription' THEN
    RETURN;
  END IF;

  SELECT COALESCE(
    ROUND(
      SUM(unit_price) FILTER (
        WHERE status IN ('pending', 'delivered')
      ),
      2
    ),
    0
  )
  INTO v_revised_total
  FROM public.deliveries
  WHERE order_id = p_order_id;

  v_balance := ROUND(v_revised_total - COALESCE(v_amount_received, 0), 2);

  UPDATE public.orders
     SET total_amount = v_revised_total,
         balance_due = v_balance,
         payment_status = CASE
           WHEN v_balance <= 0 THEN 'paid'
           ELSE 'not_paid'
         END,
         updated_at = now()
   WHERE id = p_order_id;
END;
$$;


-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 4. Replace delivery status trigger
--
-- Delivered:
--   consumes one subscription credit only.
--
-- Missed:
--   consumes no credit.
--   creates one replacement pending delivery after the latest date.
--   repeats custom meal + customization note because you selected 3B.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type TEXT;
  v_plan_credits INTEGER;
  v_credits_used INTEGER;
  v_latest_date DATE;
BEGIN
  IF OLD.status IS NOT DISTINCT FROM NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  -- Delivered/missed/cancelled records are historical.
  -- The app will allow edits only while a delivery is pending.
  IF OLD.status <> 'pending' THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Only pending deliveries can have their status changed';
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used
    FROM public.orders
   WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Order not found for this delivery';
  END IF;

  -- Successful delivery consumes exactly one subscription credit.
  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
    UPDATE public.orders
       SET credits_used = credits_used + 1,
           updated_at = now()
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id
       AND credits_used < plan_credits
    RETURNING credits_used INTO v_credits_used;

    IF NOT FOUND THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'All meal credits have already been used for this subscription';
    END IF;
  END IF;

  -- Missed delivery: no credit deduction; create replacement after last date.
  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
    IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
      SELECT MAX(scheduled_date)
        INTO v_latest_date
        FROM public.deliveries
       WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;

      INSERT INTO public.deliveries (
        order_id,
        menu_item_id,
        meal_name_snapshot,
        unit_price,
        unit_cost,
        scheduled_date,
        status,
        notes,
        is_auto_extension,
        replacement_for_delivery_id
      )
      VALUES (
        NEW.order_id,
        NEW.menu_item_id,
        NEW.meal_name_snapshot,
        NEW.unit_price,
        NEW.unit_cost,
        v_latest_date + 1,
        'pending',
        NEW.notes,
        true,
        NEW.id
      )
      ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
    END IF;
  END IF;

  -- Price changes, skipped meals, and completed meals can update
  -- the live revised subscription total.
  IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
    PERFORM public.recalculate_subscription_financials(NEW.order_id);
  END IF;

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS trg_delivery_status_change ON public.deliveries;

CREATE TRIGGER trg_delivery_status_change
  AFTER UPDATE OF status ON public.deliveries
  FOR EACH ROW
  EXECUTE FUNCTION public.handle_delivery_status_change();


-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 5. Keep current frontend compatible.
--
-- The current React app sends plan credits and total amount.
-- This function accepts those parameters but calculates price
-- server-side from live Supabase menu/plan data.
-- Client-provided p_total_amount is intentionally ignored.
-- ------------------------------------------------------------

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id UUID;
  v_menu_name TEXT;
  v_menu_price NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_menu_cost NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_plan_credits INTEGER;
  v_plan_active BOOLEAN;
  v_delivery_count INTEGER;
  v_initial_total NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_amount_received NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_balance_due NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_notes TEXT;
  v_i INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF p_order_type NOT IN ('one_time', 'subscription') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Order type must be one_time or subscription';
  END IF;

  IF p_payment_status NOT IN ('paid', 'not_paid') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Payment status must be paid or not_paid';
  END IF;

  IF p_start_date IS NULL OR p_start_date < CURRENT_DATE THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Delivery date cannot be in the past';
  END IF;

  PERFORM 1
    FROM public.customers
   WHERE id = p_customer_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Customer not found';
  END IF;

  SELECT name, price, cost, active
    INTO v_menu_name, v_menu_price, v_menu_cost, v_menu_active
    FROM public.menu_items
   WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  END IF;

  IF v_menu_active = false THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is inactive';
  END IF;

  v_notes := NULLIF(trim(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '');

  -- One-time order
  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    IF p_plan_id IS NOT NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NOT NULL THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'One-time orders must not include a plan';
    END IF;

    v_delivery_count := 1;
  END IF;

  -- Subscription order
  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
    IF p_plan_id IS NULL THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
    END IF;

    SELECT credits, active
      INTO v_plan_credits, v_plan_active
      FROM public.plans
     WHERE id = p_plan_id;

    IF NOT FOUND THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Plan not found';
    END IF;

    IF v_plan_active = false THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'This plan is inactive';
    END IF;

    IF p_plan_credits IS DISTINCT FROM v_plan_credits THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Plan credits changed. Refresh the page and select the plan again.';
    END IF;

    v_delivery_count := v_plan_credits;
  END IF;

  -- Server-calculated price.
  -- p_total_amount from browser is deliberately not trusted.
  v_initial_total := ROUND(v_menu_price * v_delivery_count, 2);

  v_amount_received := CASE
    WHEN p_payment_status = 'paid' THEN v_initial_total
    ELSE 0
  END;

  v_balance_due := ROUND(v_initial_total - v_amount_received, 2);

  INSERT INTO public.orders (
    customer_id,
    menu_item_id,
    order_type,
    plan_id,
    plan_credits,
    credits_used,
    original_total_amount,
    total_amount,
    amount_received,
    balance_due,
    payment_status,
    payment_mode,
    notes,
    subscription_instructions
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id,
    p_menu_item_id,
    p_order_type,
    CASE WHEN p_order_type = 'subscription' THEN p_plan_id ELSE NULL END,
    CASE WHEN p_order_type = 'subscription' THEN v_plan_credits ELSE NULL END,
    0,
    v_initial_total,
    v_initial_total,
    v_amount_received,
    v_balance_due,
    p_payment_status,
    p_payment_mode,
    v_notes,
    CASE WHEN p_order_type = 'subscription' THEN v_notes ELSE NULL END
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  -- Option A: create every scheduled delivery row upfront.
  FOR v_i IN 0..(v_delivery_count - 1) LOOP
    INSERT INTO public.deliveries (
      order_id,
      menu_item_id,
      meal_name_snapshot,
      unit_price,
      unit_cost,
      scheduled_date,
      status,
      notes
    )
    VALUES (
      v_order_id,
      p_menu_item_id,
      v_menu_name,
      v_menu_price,
      v_menu_cost,
      p_start_date + v_i,
      'pending',
      CASE
        WHEN p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN v_notes
        ELSE NULL
      END
    );
  END LOOP;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;


-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 6. Subscription edit functions for the future frontend
-- ------------------------------------------------------------

-- Edit permanent subscription instructions.
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.set_subscription_instructions(
  p_order_id UUID,
  p_instructions TEXT
)
RETURNS VOID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
BEGIN
  UPDATE public.orders
     SET subscription_instructions = NULLIF(trim(COALESCE(p_instructions, '')), ''),
         updated_at = now()
   WHERE id = p_order_id
     AND order_type = 'subscription';

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Active subscription order not found';
  END IF;
END;
$$;


-- Change one pending delivery only.
-- Example: 15 July only = Green Salad + "No dressing".
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.set_delivery_customization(
  p_delivery_id UUID,
  p_menu_item_id UUID,
  p_notes TEXT
)
RETURNS VOID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_menu_name TEXT;
  v_menu_price NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_menu_cost NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_order_id UUID;
BEGIN
  SELECT name, price, cost, active
    INTO v_menu_name, v_menu_price, v_menu_cost, v_menu_active
    FROM public.menu_items
   WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;

  IF NOT FOUND OR v_menu_active = false THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Selected menu item is not active';
  END IF;

  UPDATE public.deliveries d
     SET menu_item_id = p_menu_item_id,
         meal_name_snapshot = v_menu_name,
         unit_price = v_menu_price,
         unit_cost = v_menu_cost,
         notes = NULLIF(trim(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '')
    FROM public.orders o
   WHERE d.id = p_delivery_id
     AND d.order_id = o.id
     AND o.order_type = 'subscription'
     AND d.status = 'pending'
  RETURNING d.order_id INTO v_order_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Only pending subscription deliveries can be customized';
  END IF;

  PERFORM public.recalculate_subscription_financials(v_order_id);
END;
$$;


-- Change meal for every pending delivery from a selected date onward.
-- Delivered and missed history is never changed.
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.change_future_subscription_meal(
  p_order_id UUID,
  p_from_date DATE,
  p_menu_item_id UUID
)
RETURNS INTEGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_menu_name TEXT;
  v_menu_price NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_menu_cost NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_updated_count INTEGER;
BEGIN
  IF p_from_date IS NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Choose the date from which the meal should change';
  END IF;

  PERFORM 1
    FROM public.orders
   WHERE id = p_order_id
     AND order_type = 'subscription';

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription order not found';
  END IF;

  SELECT name, price, cost, active
    INTO v_menu_name, v_menu_price, v_menu_cost, v_menu_active
    FROM public.menu_items
   WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;

  IF NOT FOUND OR v_menu_active = false THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Selected menu item is not active';
  END IF;

  UPDATE public.deliveries
     SET menu_item_id = p_menu_item_id,
         meal_name_snapshot = v_menu_name,
         unit_price = v_menu_price,
         unit_cost = v_menu_cost
   WHERE order_id = p_order_id
     AND status = 'pending'
     AND scheduled_date >= p_from_date;

  GET DIAGNOSTICS v_updated_count = ROW_COUNT;

  IF v_updated_count = 0 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'No pending deliveries exist from the selected date onward';
  END IF;

  PERFORM public.recalculate_subscription_financials(p_order_id);

  RETURN v_updated_count;
END;
$$;


-- Skip one selected future delivery and extend the plan automatically.
-- Existing meal customization + delivery notes are copied to replacement.
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.skip_delivery_and_extend(
  p_delivery_id UUID,
  p_skip_reason TEXT DEFAULT NULL
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id UUID;
  v_replacement_delivery_id UUID;
BEGIN
  UPDATE public.deliveries d
     SET skip_reason = NULLIF(trim(COALESCE(p_skip_reason, '')), ''),
         status = 'missed'
    FROM public.orders o
   WHERE d.id = p_delivery_id
     AND d.order_id = o.id
     AND o.order_type = 'subscription'
     AND d.status = 'pending'
  RETURNING d.order_id INTO v_order_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Only pending subscription deliveries can be skipped';
  END IF;

  -- The status trigger has now created the replacement row.
  SELECT id
    INTO v_replacement_delivery_id
    FROM public.deliveries
   WHERE replacement_for_delivery_id = p_delivery_id
   ORDER BY created_at DESC
   LIMIT 1;

  RETURN v_replacement_delivery_id;
END;
$$;


-- Record/change amount received.
-- Positive balance_due means customer still owes money.
-- Negative balance_due means customer has account credit/refund due.
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.set_order_amount_received(
  p_order_id UUID,
  p_amount_received NUMERIC,
  p_payment_mode TEXT DEFAULT NULL
)
RETURNS VOID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type TEXT;
  v_total NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_balance NUMERIC(10,2);
BEGIN
  IF p_amount_received IS NULL OR p_amount_received < 0 THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Amount received cannot be negative';
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, total_amount
    INTO v_order_type, v_total
    FROM public.orders
   WHERE id = p_order_id
   FOR UPDATE;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Order not found';
  END IF;

  UPDATE public.orders
     SET amount_received = ROUND(p_amount_received, 2),
         payment_mode = COALESCE(NULLIF(trim(COALESCE(p_payment_mode, '')), ''), payment_mode),
         updated_at = now()
   WHERE id = p_order_id;

  IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
    PERFORM public.recalculate_subscription_financials(p_order_id);
  ELSE
    v_balance := ROUND(v_total - p_amount_received, 2);

    UPDATE public.orders
       SET balance_due = v_balance,
           payment_status = CASE
             WHEN v_balance <= 0 THEN 'paid'
             ELSE 'not_paid'
           END,
           updated_at = now()
     WHERE id = p_order_id;
  END IF;
END;
$$;


-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 7. Clean database views for the new frontend screens
-- ------------------------------------------------------------

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW public.subscription_overview
WITH (security_invoker = true)
AS
SELECT
  o.id AS subscription_order_id,

  c.id AS customer_id,
  c.name AS customer_name,
  c.contact AS customer_contact,
  c.address AS customer_address,

  p.id AS plan_id,
  p.name AS plan_name,

  o.menu_item_id AS original_menu_item_id,
  original_menu.name AS original_menu_item_name,

  o.plan_credits,
  o.credits_used,
  GREATEST(o.plan_credits - o.credits_used, 0) AS credits_remaining,

  o.subscription_instructions,

  o.original_total_amount,
  o.total_amount AS revised_total_amount,
  o.amount_received,
  o.balance_due,

  GREATEST(o.balance_due, 0) AS amount_due,
  GREATEST(-o.balance_due, 0) AS customer_credit,

  o.payment_status,
  o.payment_mode,

  counts.delivered_count,
  counts.pending_count,
  counts.missed_count,
  counts.cancelled_count,

  next_delivery.scheduled_date AS next_delivery_date,
  next_delivery.menu_item_id AS current_future_menu_item_id,
  next_delivery.meal_name_snapshot AS current_future_menu_item_name,
  next_delivery.unit_price AS current_future_unit_price,
  next_delivery.is_auto_extension AS next_delivery_is_auto_extension,

  CASE
    WHEN o.credits_used >= o.plan_credits THEN 'completed'
    WHEN next_delivery.scheduled_date IS NULL THEN 'needs_attention'
    ELSE 'active'
  END AS subscription_state,

  o.created_at,
  o.updated_at

FROM public.orders o
JOIN public.customers c ON c.id = o.customer_id
JOIN public.plans p ON p.id = o.plan_id
JOIN public.menu_items original_menu ON original_menu.id = o.menu_item_id

LEFT JOIN LATERAL (
  SELECT
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE d.status = 'delivered') AS delivered_count,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE d.status = 'pending') AS pending_count,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE d.status = 'missed') AS missed_count,
    COUNT(*) FILTER (WHERE d.status = 'cancelled') AS cancelled_count
  FROM public.deliveries d
  WHERE d.order_id = o.id
) counts ON true

LEFT JOIN LATERAL (
  SELECT
    d.scheduled_date,
    d.menu_item_id,
    d.meal_name_snapshot,
    d.unit_price,
    d.is_auto_extension
  FROM public.deliveries d
  WHERE d.order_id = o.id
    AND d.status = 'pending'
  ORDER BY d.scheduled_date ASC
  LIMIT 1
) next_delivery ON true

WHERE o.order_type = 'subscription';


CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW public.subscription_delivery_timeline
WITH (security_invoker = true)
AS
SELECT
  d.id AS delivery_id,
  d.order_id AS subscription_order_id,

  c.id AS customer_id,
  c.name AS customer_name,
  c.contact AS customer_contact,
  c.address AS customer_address,

  d.scheduled_date,
  d.status,

  d.menu_item_id,
  d.meal_name_snapshot,
  d.unit_price,
  d.unit_cost,

  d.notes AS customization_notes,
  d.skip_reason,

  d.is_auto_extension,
  d.replacement_for_delivery_id,
  missed_delivery.scheduled_date AS replacement_for_missed_date,

  o.subscription_instructions,
  o.plan_credits,
  o.credits_used,
  GREATEST(o.plan_credits - o.credits_used, 0) AS credits_remaining

FROM public.deliveries d
JOIN public.orders o ON o.id = d.order_id
JOIN public.customers c ON c.id = o.customer_id

LEFT JOIN public.deliveries missed_delivery
  ON missed_delivery.id = d.replacement_for_delivery_id

WHERE o.order_type = 'subscription';

) FROM PUBLIC;

GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.create_order_with_deliveries(
  UUID, UUID, TEXT, UUID, INTEGER, NUMERIC, TEXT, TEXT, TEXT, DATE
) TO anon, authenticated;

GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.set_subscription_instructions(UUID, TEXT)
TO anon, authenticated;

GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.set_delivery_customization(UUID, UUID, TEXT)
TO anon, authenticated;

GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.change_future_subscription_meal(UUID, DATE, UUID)
TO anon, authenticated;

GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.skip_delivery_and_extend(UUID, TEXT)
TO anon, authenticated;

GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.set_order_amount_received(UUID, NUMERIC, TEXT)
TO anon, authenticated;

GRANT SELECT ON public.subscription_overview TO anon, authenticated;
GRANT SELECT ON public.subscription_delivery_timeline TO anon, authenticated;

@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useParams, Link } from 'react-router-dom'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'
const STATUS_STYLES = {
  pending: 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800',
  delivered: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800',
  missed: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800',
  cancelled: 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600',
}
export default function CustomerDetail() {
  const { id } = useParams()
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orders, setOrders] = useState([])
  const [deliveries, setDeliveries] = useState([])
  const [menuItems, setMenuItems] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [updatingDeliveryId, setUpdatingDeliveryId] = useState(null)
  const [updatingOrderId, setUpdatingOrderId] = useState(null)
  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      setLoading(true)
      setError('')
      const [custRes, ordersRes, delivRes, itemsRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('customers').select('*').eq('id', id).single(),
        supabase.from('orders').select('*, menu_items(name, price), plans(name, credits)').eq('customer_id', id).order('created_at', { ascending: false }),
        supabase.from('deliveries').select('*, orders!inner(customer_id)').eq('orders.customer_id', id).order('scheduled_date', { ascending: true }),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])
      if (custRes.error) setError(custRes.error.message)
      else if (ordersRes.error) setError(ordersRes.error.message)
      else if (delivRes.error) setError(delivRes.error.message)
      else {
        setCustomer(custRes.data)
        setOrders(ordersRes.data || [])
        setDeliveries(delivRes.data || [])
        setMenuItems(itemsRes.data || [])
      }
      setLoading(false)
    }
    load()
  }, [id])
  async function updateDeliveryStatus(deliveryId, newStatus) {
    setUpdatingDeliveryId(deliveryId)
    setError('')
    const { error } = await supabase.from('deliveries').update({ status: newStatus }).eq('id', deliveryId)
    setUpdatingDeliveryId(null)
    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to update: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }
    // Refresh deliveries
    const { data } = await supabase.from('deliveries').select('*, orders!inner(customer_id)').eq('orders.customer_id', id).order('scheduled_date', { ascending: true })
    setDeliveries(data || [])
    // Refresh orders to get updated credits_used
    const { data: oData } = await supabase.from('orders').select('*, menu_items(name, price), plans(name, credits)').eq('customer_id', id).order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    setOrders(oData || [])
  }
  async function updateOrderMeal(orderId, newMenuItemId) {
    setUpdatingOrderId(orderId)
    setError('')
    const { error } = await supabase.from('orders').update({ menu_item_id: newMenuItemId }).eq('id', orderId)
    setUpdatingOrderId(null)
    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to update meal: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }
    const { data: oData } = await supabase.from('orders').select('*, menu_items(name, price), plans(name, credits)').eq('customer_id', id).order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    setOrders(oData || [])
  }
  if (loading) return <p className="p-6 text-sm text-gray-500">Loading customer...</p>
  if (!customer) return <p className="p-6 text-sm text-red-600">Customer not found.</p>
  const activeOrders = orders.filter(o => o.order_type === 'subscription' && o.credits_used < o.plan_credits)
  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-gray-500 mb-2">
        <Link to="/deliveries" className="hover:underline text-green-700">Back to Deliveries</Link>
        <span>/</span>
        <span>Customer</span>
      </div>
      <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">{customer.name}</h1>
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{customer.contact}</p>
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{customer.address}</p>
      </div>
      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      {activeOrders.length > 0 && (
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <h2 className="font-bold text-lg">Active Subscriptions</h2>
          {activeOrders.map(order => {
            const remaining = (order.plan_credits || 0) - (order.credits_used || 0)
            const orderDeliveries = deliveries.filter(d => d.order_id === order.id)
            const nextPending = orderDeliveries.find(d => d.status === 'pending')
            return (
              <div key={order.id} className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-4">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                  <div>
                    <p className="font-medium">{order.plans?.name || 'Subscription'}</p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Meal: {order.menu_items?.name || '-'}</p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Credits: {order.credits_used} used / {order.plan_credits} total</p>
                    <p className="text-sm font-medium text-green-700">{remaining} remaining</p>
                    {nextPending && (
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Next delivery: {nextPending.scheduled_date}</p>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <label className="block text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">Change Meal</label>
                    <select
                      disabled={updatingOrderId === order.id}
                      value={order.menu_item_id || ''}
                      onChange={(e) => updateOrderMeal(order.id, e.target.value)}
                      className="border rounded-md text-sm px-2 py-1"
                    >
                      {menuItems.map(item => (
                        <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>{item.name}</option>
                      ))}
                    </select>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            )
          })}
        </div>
      )}
      <div>
        <h2 className="font-bold text-lg mb-3">Delivery Timeline</h2>
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
          <table className="w-full text-sm">
            <thead className="bg-gray-50 text-left text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase">
              <tr>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Date</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Item</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Status</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Notes</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2 text-right">Actions</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {deliveries.map(d => {
                const order = orders.find(o => o.id === d.order_id)
                const isPending = d.status === 'pending'
                return (
                  <tr key={d.id} className="border-t">
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">{d.scheduled_date}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">{order?.menu_items?.name || '-'}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${STATUS_STYLES[d.status]}`}>
                        {d.status}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-gray-500">{d.notes || '-'}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                      {isPending ? (
                        <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingDeliveryId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateDeliveryStatus(d.id, 'delivered')}
                            className="bg-green-600 text-white text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Deliver
                          </button>
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingDeliveryId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateDeliveryStatus(d.id, 'missed')}
                            className="bg-red-600 text-white text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Miss
                          </button>
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingDeliveryId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateDeliveryStatus(d.id, 'cancelled')}
                            className="bg-gray-500 text-white text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Skip
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">{d.status}</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )
              })}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
