# Script C - Customer Tracker + Route Updates

@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { useParams, Link } from 'react-router-dom'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const STATUS_STYLES = {
  pending: 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800',
  delivered: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800',
  missed: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800',
  cancelled: 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600',
}

export default function CustomerDetail() {
  const { id } = useParams()
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orders, setOrders] = useState([])
  const [deliveries, setDeliveries] = useState([])
  const [menuItems, setMenuItems] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [updatingDeliveryId, setUpdatingDeliveryId] = useState(null)
  const [updatingOrderId, setUpdatingOrderId] = useState(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      setLoading(true)
      setError('')

      const [custRes, ordersRes, delivRes, itemsRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('customers').select('*').eq('id', id).single(),
        supabase.from('orders').select('*, menu_items(name, price), plans(name, credits)').eq('customer_id', id).order('created_at', { ascending: false }),
        supabase.from('deliveries').select('*, orders!inner(customer_id)').eq('orders.customer_id', id).order('scheduled_date', { ascending: true }),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])

      if (custRes.error) setError(custRes.error.message)
      else if (ordersRes.error) setError(ordersRes.error.message)
      else if (delivRes.error) setError(delivRes.error.message)
      else {
        setCustomer(custRes.data)
        setOrders(ordersRes.data || [])
        setDeliveries(delivRes.data || [])
        setMenuItems(itemsRes.data || [])
      }
      setLoading(false)
    }
    load()
  }, [id])

  async function updateDeliveryStatus(deliveryId, newStatus) {
    setUpdatingDeliveryId(deliveryId)
    setError('')
    const { error } = await supabase.from('deliveries').update({ status: newStatus }).eq('id', deliveryId)
    setUpdatingDeliveryId(null)
    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to update: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }
    const { data } = await supabase.from('deliveries').select('*, orders!inner(customer_id)').eq('orders.customer_id', id).order('scheduled_date', { ascending: true })
    setDeliveries(data || [])
    const { data: oData } = await supabase.from('orders').select('*, menu_items(name, price), plans(name, credits)').eq('customer_id', id).order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    setOrders(oData || [])
  }

  async function updateOrderMeal(orderId, newMenuItemId) {
    setUpdatingOrderId(orderId)
    setError('')
    const { error } = await supabase.from('orders').update({ menu_item_id: newMenuItemId }).eq('id', orderId)
    setUpdatingOrderId(null)
    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to update meal: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }
    const { data: oData } = await supabase.from('orders').select('*, menu_items(name, price), plans(name, credits)').eq('customer_id', id).order('created_at', { ascending: false })
    setOrders(oData || [])
  }

  if (loading) return <p className="p-6 text-sm text-gray-500">Loading customer...</p>
  if (!customer) return <p className="p-6 text-sm text-red-600">Customer not found.</p>

  const activeOrders = orders.filter(o => o.order_type === 'subscription' && o.credits_used < o.plan_credits)

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto space-y-6">
      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-gray-500 mb-2">
        <Link to="/deliveries" className="hover:underline text-green-700">Back to Deliveries</Link>
        <span>/</span>
        <span>Customer</span>
      </div>

      <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-6">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">{customer.name}</h1>
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{customer.contact}</p>
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">{customer.address}</p>
      </div>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />

      {activeOrders.length > 0 && (
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <h2 className="font-bold text-lg">Active Subscriptions</h2>
          {activeOrders.map(order => {
            const remaining = (order.plan_credits || 0) - (order.credits_used || 0)
            const orderDeliveries = deliveries.filter(d => d.order_id === order.id)
            const nextPending = orderDeliveries.find(d => d.status === 'pending')
            return (
              <div key={order.id} className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-4">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                  <div>
                    <p className="font-medium">{order.plans?.name || 'Subscription'}</p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Meal: {order.menu_items?.name || '-'}</p>
                    <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">Credits: {order.credits_used} used / {order.plan_credits} total</p>
                    <p className="text-sm font-medium text-green-700">{remaining} remaining</p>
                    {nextPending && (
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Next delivery: {nextPending.scheduled_date}</p>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <label className="block text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1">Change Meal</label>
                    <select
                      disabled={updatingOrderId === order.id}
                      value={order.menu_item_id || ''}
                      onChange={(e) => updateOrderMeal(order.id, e.target.value)}
                      className="border rounded-md text-sm px-2 py-1"
                    >
                      {menuItems.map(item => (
                        <option key={item.id} value={item.id}>{item.name}</option>
                      ))}
                    </select>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            )
          })}
        </div>
      )}

      <div>
        <h2 className="font-bold text-lg mb-3">Delivery Timeline</h2>
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
          <table className="w-full text-sm">
            <thead className="bg-gray-50 text-left text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase">
              <tr>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Date</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Item</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Status</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Notes</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2 text-right">Actions</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {deliveries.map(d => {
                const order = orders.find(o => o.id === d.order_id)
                const isPending = d.status === 'pending'
                return (
                  <tr key={d.id} className="border-t">
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">{d.scheduled_date}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">{order?.menu_items?.name || '-'}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${STATUS_STYLES[d.status]}`}>
                        {d.status}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-gray-500">{d.notes || '-'}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                      {isPending ? (
                        <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingDeliveryId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateDeliveryStatus(d.id, 'delivered')}
                            className="bg-green-600 text-white text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Deliver
                          </button>
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingDeliveryId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateDeliveryStatus(d.id, 'missed')}
                            className="bg-red-600 text-white text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Miss
                          </button>
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingDeliveryId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateDeliveryStatus(d.id, 'cancelled')}
                            className="bg-gray-500 text-white text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Skip
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">{d.status}</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )
              })}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
'@ | Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 src/pages/CustomerDetail.jsx

@'
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'
import { Link } from 'react-router-dom'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString } from '../lib/date'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const STATUS_STYLES = {
  pending: 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800',
  delivered: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800',
  missed: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800',
  cancelled: 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600',
}

export default function Deliveries() {
  const [deliveries, setDeliveries] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [updatingId, setUpdatingId] = useState(null)

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    setError('')
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('deliveries')
      .select(`
        id, scheduled_date, status, notes,
        orders (
          id, order_type, plan_credits, credits_used,
          customers ( id, name, contact, address ),
          menu_items ( name )
        )
      `)
      .eq('scheduled_date', todayDateString())
      .order('id')

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
    } else {
      setDeliveries(data || [])
    }
    setLoading(false)
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => { load() }, [load])

  async function updateStatus(deliveryId, newStatus) {
    setUpdatingId(deliveryId)
    setError('')
    const { error } = await supabase
      .from('deliveries')
      .update({ status: newStatus })
      .eq('id', deliveryId)
    setUpdatingId(null)
    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to update delivery: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }
    load()
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Today's Deliveries</h1>
        <button onClick={load} className="text-sm text-green-700 hover:underline">Refresh</button>
      </div>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />

      {loading ? (
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">Loading...</p>
      ) : deliveries.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-8 text-center text-gray-500 text-sm">
          No deliveries scheduled for today.
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
          <table className="w-full text-sm">
            <thead className="bg-gray-50 text-left text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase">
              <tr>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Customer</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Item</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Type</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Status</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2 text-right">Actions</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {deliveries.map((d) => {
                const order = d.orders
                const customer = order?.customers
                const item = order?.menu_items
                const isPending = d.status === 'pending'
                return (
                  <tr key={d.id} className="border-t">
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <Link to={`/customer/${customer?.id}`} className="font-medium text-green-700 hover:underline">
                        {customer?.name || '-'}
                      </Link>
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{customer?.contact}</p>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">{item?.name || '-'}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      {order?.order_type === 'subscription' ? (
                        <span className="text-xs">
                          Subscription
                          <span className="text-gray-400"> ({order.credits_used}/{order.plan_credits})</span>
                        </span>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs">One-time</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${STATUS_STYLES[d.status]}`}>
                        {d.status}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                      {isPending ? (
                        <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateStatus(d.id, 'delivered')}
                            className="bg-green-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Delivered
                          </button>
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateStatus(d.id, 'missed')}
                            className="bg-red-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Missed
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">-</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )
              })}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

import { HashRouter, Routes, Route, NavLink } from 'react-router-dom'
import NewOrder from './pages/NewOrder.jsx'
import Deliveries from './pages/Deliveries.jsx'
import CustomerDetail from './pages/CustomerDetail.jsx'

export default function App() {
  return (
    <HashRouter>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50">
        <nav className="bg-white shadow-sm border-b">
          <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
            <span className="font-bold text-lg text-green-700">Lunchmate OS</span>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <NavLink
                to="/"
                end
                className={({ isActive }) =>
                  `px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm font-medium ${isActive ? 'bg-green-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-100'}`
                }
              >
                New Order
              </NavLink>
              <NavLink
                to="/deliveries"
                className={({ isActive }) =>
                  `px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm font-medium ${isActive ? 'bg-green-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-100'}`
                }
              >
                Today's Deliveries
              </NavLink>
            </div>
          </div>
        </nav>
        <main className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 py-6">
          <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<NewOrder />} />
            <Route path="/deliveries" element={<Deliveries />} />
            <Route path="/customer/:id" element={<CustomerDetail />} />
          </Routes>
        </main>
      </div>
    </HashRouter>
  )
}

Response B


Yes — we will fix this properly in the app.

Your normal workflow should not be Supabase deliveries table. That raw table is only backend/admin data. The app will get:

text

Subscriptions
→ one clean card per customer plan

Open Subscription
→ one customer’s complete schedule, credits, meal changes, notes, skips
Before I write the SQL upgrade, your Option B choice creates three important money/customization rules that must be confirmed.

1. How automatic price recalculation should work
Example:

text

Customer buys 7 Non-Veg Thalis at Rs.150 each
Original total: Rs.1,050

1 meal is successfully delivered:
13 Jul → Non-Veg Thali → Rs.150

Customer changes all future meals to Veg Thali:
6 remaining meals × Rs.120 = Rs.720
The revised order total would become:

text

Rs.150 delivered + Rs.720 future meals = Rs.870
A missed day does not create an extra charge:

text

13 Jul → Missed (excluded from price)
20 Jul → New pending replacement meal (included in price)
So there are always prices for exactly the customer’s remaining meal credits, not double charges for skipped days.

Confirm this formula
Reply:

text

1. Confirmed
if this is correct.

2. What happens if the subscription was already marked Paid?
Changing from a higher-priced meal to a lower-priced meal—or the opposite—changes the final total.

Example:

text

Customer paid: Rs.1,050
Revised total after meal change: Rs.870

Customer has Rs.180 credit/refund due.
Or:

text

Customer paid: Rs.840
Revised total after meal change: Rs.900

Customer still needs to pay Rs.60.
Your current schema only has:

text

paid / not_paid
That is not enough to safely represent a revised paid subscription.

Recommended option: track Amount Received and Remaining Balance
I will add these fields:

text

orders.amount_received
orders.balance_due
The app can then clearly show:

text

Original total: Rs.1,050
Revised total: Rs.870
Amount received: Rs.1,050
Customer credit: Rs.180
Or:

text

Revised total: Rs.900
Amount received: Rs.840
Balance due: Rs.60
This is not a full ledger or accounting module. It is just the minimum needed so meal changes do not make payment information incorrect.

Choose one:

text

2A. Add amount received and balance due — recommended
or:

text

2B. Allow meal-price changes only for not-paid subscriptions
or:

text

2C. Recalculate total but keep paid/not-paid unchanged
I strongly recommend 2A.

Your Confirmed Customization Features
You selected Yes for all features. We will support:

Feature	Where it is stored
Permanent instructions for the plan	Subscription-level instructions
One-day instruction	Delivery-specific note
Change meal for all future pending deliveries	Updates future pending delivery rows
Change meal on one date only	Updates only one pending delivery row
Skip/pause future delivery	Marks it missed, then auto-adds one future pending row
Important Database Design Rule
We need two levels of meal details.

Subscription Default
Example:

text

Original subscription: Non-Veg Thali
Current future meal: Veg Thali
Permanent instruction: Less oil, no onion
Per-Delivery Snapshot / Override
Example:

text

15 July:
Meal: Green Salad
One-day note: No dressing today
This is important because historical records must remain accurate.

If Rahul was sent Non-Veg Thali on 13 July, then changes to Veg Thali from 14 July:

text

13 July remains Non-Veg Thali forever
14 July onwards become Veg Thali
We must never rewrite already delivered or missed history.

How Skip / Missed Will Work in the UI
The database status remains missed, because that is your existing schema rule.

But in the app, the button can say:

text

Skip & Extend
instead of just:

text

Missed
This is friendlier and clearer for planned customer skips.

When clicked:

text

Customer skips 16 July
→ 16 July becomes missed
→ no credit is deducted
→ one new pending meal is added after the latest scheduled date
Two Final Decisions Needed Before I Give the SQL Upgrade
I need these because they affect real financial records and cannot be guessed safely.

Question 1 — Meal Change Price Rule
Example:

text

Customer bought:
7 Non-Veg Thalis at Rs.150 each
Total: Rs.1,050

Later customer asks:
“From tomorrow, change to Veg Thali at Rs.120.”
What should happen to the original subscription amount?

Option A — No automatic price change — Recommended
text

Original total stays Rs.1,050.
Meal change is treated as a service substitution.
No refund, extra payment, or amount recalculation happens automatically.
This is simplest and safest because invoices/ledgers/refunds are explicitly out of scope right now.

Option B — Automatically recalculate remaining value
text

Future Non-Veg meals become Veg meals.
Subscription total/payment amount changes automatically.
This needs payment adjustments, refunds, extra collections, and ledger logic. That starts moving into the later accounting module.

My recommendation: Option A.

Question 2 — “Change Future Meal” Effective Date
I recommend this behavior:

text

Change meal for:
- This delivery only
OR
- All pending deliveries from a chosen date onward
Example:

text

Customer changes to Veg Thali from 20 July.

13–19 July: unchanged
20 July onward: Veg Thali
Delivered/missed rows: never changed
The app will allow editing only pending delivery rows. Delivered and missed records remain history.

Wait, but Get-Content might mess with encoding. Actually, a better approach is:

powershell


$paths = @("package.json", "postcss.config.js", "vite.config.js", "tailwind.config.js")
foreach ($p in $paths) {
    $bytes = [System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes($p)
    # Remove BOM if present (EF BB BF)
    if ($bytes.Length -ge 3 -and $bytes[0] -eq 0xEF -and $bytes[1] -eq 0xBB -and $bytes[2] -eq 0xBF) {
        $bytes = $bytes[3..($bytes.Length-1)]
        [System.IO.File]::WriteAllBytes($p, $bytes)
        Write-Host "Fixed BOM in $p"
    } else {
        Write-Host "No BOM in $p"
    }
}
This is robust and handles the issue directly.

PS C:\Users\gandh\lunchmate-1.c-version> Get-Content src\pages\NewOrder.jsx
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString, addDaysToDateString } from '../lib/date'
import CustomerPicker from '../components/CustomerPicker'
import MenuPicker from '../components/MenuPicker'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const PAYMENT_MODES = [
  { value: 'cash', label: 'Cash' },
  { value: 'upi', label: 'UPI' },
  { value: 'bank_transfer', label: 'Bank Transfer' },
  { value: 'card', label: 'Card' },
  { value: 'other', label: 'Other' },
]

export default function NewOrder() {
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orderType, setOrderType] = useState('one_time')
  const [menuItem, setMenuItem] = useState(null)
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState([])
  const [planId, setPlanId] = useState('')
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
  const [paymentStatus, setPaymentStatus] = useState('not_paid')
  const [paymentMode, setPaymentMode] = useState('cash')
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPlans() {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plans')
        .select('id, name, credits')
        .eq('active', true)
        .order('credits')
      if (!error) setPlans(data || [])
    }
    loadPlans()
  }, [])

  const selectedPlan = plans.find((p) => p.id === planId) || null
  const unitCount = orderType === 'subscription' ? (selectedPlan?.credits || 0) : 1
  const totalAmount = menuItem ? Number(menuItem.price) * unitCount : 0

  function resetForm() {
    setCustomer(null)
    setOrderType('one_time')
    setMenuItem(null)
    setPlanId('')
    setStartDate(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
    setPaymentStatus('not_paid')
    setPaymentMode('cash')
    setNotes('')
  }

  function validate() {
    if (!customer) return 'Please select or create a customer.'
    if (!menuItem) return 'Please select a menu item.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && !selectedPlan) return 'Please select a plan for the subscription.'
    if (!startDate) return 'Please pick a delivery date.'
    if (startDate < todayDateString()) return 'Delivery date cannot be in the past.'
    if (totalAmount <= 0) return 'Total amount must be greater than zero.'
    return ''
  }

  async function handleSubmit(e) {
    e.preventDefault()
    setError('')
    setSuccess('')
    const validationError = validate()
    if (validationError) {
      setError(validationError)
      return
    }

    setSubmitting(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.rpc('create_order_with_deliveries', {
      p_customer_id: customer.id,
      p_menu_item_id: menuItem.id,
      p_order_type: orderType,
      p_plan_id: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.id : null,
      p_plan_credits: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.credits : null,
      p_total_amount: totalAmount,
      p_payment_status: paymentStatus,
      p_payment_mode: paymentMode,
      p_notes: notes.trim() || null,
      p_start_date: startDate,
    })
    setSubmitting(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to log order: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }

    setSuccess(
      orderType === 'subscription'
        ? `Order logged! ${selectedPlan.credits} deliveries scheduled starting ${startDate}.`
        : `Order logged! Delivery scheduled for ${startDate}.`
    )
    resetForm()
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-xl mx-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">New Order</h1>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      <Alert type="success" message={success} onClose={() => setSuccess('')} />

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Customer</label>
          <CustomerPicker selectedCustomer={customer} onSelect={setCustomer} />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Order Type</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'one_time'}
                onChange={() => { setOrderType('one_time'); setPlanId('') }}
              />
              One-time order
            </label>
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'subscription'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('subscription')}
              />
              Subscription
            </label>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Menu Item</label>
          <MenuPicker selectedItem={menuItem} onSelect={setMenuItem} />
        </div>

        {orderType === 'subscription' && (
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Plan</label>
            {plans.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">No active plans found. Add some in Supabase - plans.</p>
            ) : (
              <select
                value={planId}
                onChange={(e) => setPlanId(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              >
                <option value="">Select a plan...</option>
                {plans.map((p) => (
                  <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>{p.name} ({p.credits} credits)</option>
                ))}
              </select>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">
            {orderType === 'subscription' ? 'Delivery Start Date' : 'Delivery Date'}
          </label>
          <input
            type="date"
            value={startDate}
            min={todayDateString()}
            onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Status</label>
            <select
              value={paymentStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              <option value="not_paid">Not Paid</option>
              <option value="paid">Paid</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Mode</label>
            <select
              value={paymentMode}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentMode(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              {PAYMENT_MODES.map((m) => (
                <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label}</option>
              ))}
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Notes (optional)</label>
          <textarea
            value={notes}
            onChange={(e) => setNotes(e.target.value)}
            rows={2}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="Allergies, gate code, delivery instructions..."
          />
        </div>

        <div className="border-t pt-4 flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Amount</p>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-700">Rs.{totalAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
            {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan && menuItem && (
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">
                Rs.{Number(menuItem.price).toFixed(2)} x {selectedPlan.credits} meals
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={submitting}
            className="bg-green-600 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-md font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {submitting ? 'Logging Order...' : 'Log Order'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  )
}

🎉 All Files Created Successfully!

⚠️ CRITICAL: Did You Run the SQL Addendum?
Before the app works, your database needs the create_order_with_deliveries function. I gave this to you earlier but never got confirmation.

Go here right now:
https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/ukrztdeqzbbroowcphwk/sql/new

Paste this SQL and click Run:

SQL

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;

  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required';
  END IF;

  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending');
  ELSE
    FOR v_i IN 0..(p_plan_credits - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending');
    END LOOP;
  END IF;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;
Confirm: "SQL addendum done" before proceeding.

# Script B - Pages + GitHub Actions Deploy

@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString, addDaysToDateString } from '../lib/date'
import CustomerPicker from '../components/CustomerPicker'
import MenuPicker from '../components/MenuPicker'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const PAYMENT_MODES = [
  { value: 'cash', label: 'Cash' },
  { value: 'upi', label: 'UPI' },
  { value: 'bank_transfer', label: 'Bank Transfer' },
  { value: 'card', label: 'Card' },
  { value: 'other', label: 'Other' },
]

export default function NewOrder() {
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orderType, setOrderType] = useState('one_time')
  const [menuItem, setMenuItem] = useState(null)
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState([])
  const [planId, setPlanId] = useState('')
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
  const [paymentStatus, setPaymentStatus] = useState('not_paid')
  const [paymentMode, setPaymentMode] = useState('cash')
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPlans() {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plans')
        .select('id, name, credits')
        .eq('active', true)
        .order('credits')
      if (!error) setPlans(data || [])
    }
    loadPlans()
  }, [])

  const selectedPlan = plans.find((p) => p.id === planId) || null
  const unitCount = orderType === 'subscription' ? (selectedPlan?.credits || 0) : 1
  const totalAmount = menuItem ? Number(menuItem.price) * unitCount : 0

  function resetForm() {
    setCustomer(null)
    setOrderType('one_time')
    setMenuItem(null)
    setPlanId('')
    setStartDate(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
    setPaymentStatus('not_paid')
    setPaymentMode('cash')
    setNotes('')
  }

  function validate() {
    if (!customer) return 'Please select or create a customer.'
    if (!menuItem) return 'Please select a menu item.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && !selectedPlan) return 'Please select a plan for the subscription.'
    if (!startDate) return 'Please pick a delivery date.'
    if (startDate < todayDateString()) return 'Delivery date cannot be in the past.'
    if (totalAmount <= 0) return 'Total amount must be greater than zero.'
    return ''
  }

  async function handleSubmit(e) {
    e.preventDefault()
    setError('')
    setSuccess('')
    const validationError = validate()
    if (validationError) {
      setError(validationError)
      return
    }

    setSubmitting(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.rpc('create_order_with_deliveries', {
      p_customer_id: customer.id,
      p_menu_item_id: menuItem.id,
      p_order_type: orderType,
      p_plan_id: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.id : null,
      p_plan_credits: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.credits : null,
      p_total_amount: totalAmount,
      p_payment_status: paymentStatus,
      p_payment_mode: paymentMode,
      p_notes: notes.trim() || null,
      p_start_date: startDate,
    })
    setSubmitting(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to log order: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }

    setSuccess(
      orderType === 'subscription'
        ? `Order logged! ${selectedPlan.credits} deliveries scheduled starting ${startDate}.`
        : `Order logged! Delivery scheduled for ${startDate}.`
    )
    resetForm()
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-xl mx-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">New Order</h1>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      <Alert type="success" message={success} onClose={() => setSuccess('')} />

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Customer</label>
          <CustomerPicker selectedCustomer={customer} onSelect={setCustomer} />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Order Type</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'one_time'}
                onChange={() => { setOrderType('one_time'); setPlanId('') }}
              />
              One-time order
            </label>
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'subscription'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('subscription')}
              />
              Subscription
            </label>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Menu Item</label>
          <MenuPicker selectedItem={menuItem} onSelect={setMenuItem} />
        </div>

        {orderType === 'subscription' && (
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Plan</label>
            {plans.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">No active plans found. Add some in Supabase - plans.</p>
            ) : (
              <select
                value={planId}
                onChange={(e) => setPlanId(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              >
                <option value="">Select a plan...</option>
                {plans.map((p) => (
                  <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>{p.name} ({p.credits} credits)</option>
                ))}
              </select>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">
            {orderType === 'subscription' ? 'Delivery Start Date' : 'Delivery Date'}
          </label>
          <input
            type="date"
            value={startDate}
            min={todayDateString()}
            onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Status</label>
            <select
              value={paymentStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              <option value="not_paid">Not Paid</option>
              <option value="paid">Paid</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Mode</label>
            <select
              value={paymentMode}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentMode(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              {PAYMENT_MODES.map((m) => (
                <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label}</option>
              ))}
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Notes (optional)</label>
          <textarea
            value={notes}
            onChange={(e) => setNotes(e.target.value)}
            rows={2}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="Allergies, gate code, delivery instructions..."
          />
        </div>

        <div className="border-t pt-4 flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Amount</p>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-700">Rs.{totalAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
            {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan && menuItem && (
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">
                Rs.{Number(menuItem.price).toFixed(2)} x {selectedPlan.credits} meals
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={submitting}
            className="bg-green-600 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-md font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {submitting ? 'Logging Order...' : 'Log Order'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  )
}
'@ | Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 src/pages/NewOrder.jsx

@'
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString } from '../lib/date'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const STATUS_STYLES = {
  pending: 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800',
  delivered: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800',
  missed: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800',
  cancelled: 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600',
}

export default function Deliveries() {
  const [deliveries, setDeliveries] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [updatingId, setUpdatingId] = useState(null)

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    setError('')
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('deliveries')
      .select(`
        id, scheduled_date, status, notes,
        orders (
          id, order_type, plan_credits, credits_used,
          customers ( name, contact, address ),
          menu_items ( name )
        )
      `)
      .eq('scheduled_date', todayDateString())
      .order('id')

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
    } else {
      setDeliveries(data || [])
    }
    setLoading(false)
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => { load() }, [load])

  async function updateStatus(deliveryId, newStatus) {
    setUpdatingId(deliveryId)
    setError('')
    const { error } = await supabase
      .from('deliveries')
      .update({ status: newStatus })
      .eq('id', deliveryId)
    setUpdatingId(null)
    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to update delivery: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }
    load()
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Today's Deliveries</h1>
        <button onClick={load} className="text-sm text-green-700 hover:underline">Refresh</button>
      </div>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />

      {loading ? (
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">Loading...</p>
      ) : deliveries.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-8 text-center text-gray-500 text-sm">
          No deliveries scheduled for today.
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
          <table className="w-full text-sm">
            <thead className="bg-gray-50 text-left text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase">
              <tr>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Customer</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Item</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Type</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Status</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2 text-right">Actions</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {deliveries.map((d) => {
                const order = d.orders
                const customer = order?.customers
                const item = order?.menu_items
                const isPending = d.status === 'pending'
                return (
                  <tr key={d.id} className="border-t">
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <p className="font-medium">{customer?.name || '-'}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{customer?.contact}</p>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">{item?.name || '-'}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      {order?.order_type === 'subscription' ? (
                        <span className="text-xs">
                          Subscription
                          <span className="text-gray-400"> ({order.credits_used}/{order.plan_credits})</span>
                        </span>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs">One-time</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${STATUS_STYLES[d.status]}`}>
                        {d.status}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                      {isPending ? (
                        <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateStatus(d.id, 'delivered')}
                            className="bg-green-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Delivered
                          </button>
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateStatus(d.id, 'missed')}
                            className="bg-red-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Missed
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">-</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )
              })}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

SQL

-- ============================================================
-- Lunchmate Module 1:
-- Safe order creation + Option A delivery schedule generation
--
-- Creates all subscription delivery rows upfront:
-- 7-credit plan = 7 pending delivery rows
-- 30-credit plan = 30 pending delivery rows
-- ============================================================

-- Remove the older version if it was created previously.
-- This only removes a function, never orders/customers/deliveries.
DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS public.create_order_with_deliveries(
  UUID, UUID, TEXT, UUID, INTEGER, NUMERIC, TEXT, TEXT, TEXT, DATE
);

-- Replace the delivery-status trigger function with a safer version.
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type   TEXT;
  v_plan_credits INTEGER;
  v_credits_used INTEGER;
  v_latest_date  DATE;
BEGIN
  -- Do nothing when only notes or another non-status field changes.
  IF OLD.status IS NOT DISTINCT FROM NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  -- A delivery should not be changed after it is finalized.
  -- Pending -> delivered/missed/cancelled is allowed.
  IF OLD.status <> 'pending' THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'A finalized delivery status cannot be changed';
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used
    FROM orders
   WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Order not found for this delivery';
  END IF;

  -- Credit is consumed ONLY after a successful subscription delivery.
  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
    UPDATE orders
       SET credits_used = credits_used + 1
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id
       AND credits_used < plan_credits;

    IF NOT FOUND THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'All meal credits have already been used for this order';
    END IF;
  END IF;

  -- Missed subscription delivery:
  -- Do not consume a credit.
  -- Add one new pending delivery after the current final schedule date.
  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
    IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
      SELECT MAX(scheduled_date)
        INTO v_latest_date
        FROM deliveries
       WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;

      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
      VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + 1, 'pending')
      ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

-- Create all order + delivery records in one safe database operation.
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id       UUID;
  v_menu_price     NUMERIC(10,2);
  v_menu_active    BOOLEAN;
  v_plan_credits   INTEGER;
  v_plan_active    BOOLEAN;
  v_delivery_count INTEGER;
  v_i              INTEGER;
BEGIN
  -- Basic server-side validation
  IF p_order_type NOT IN ('one_time', 'subscription') THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Order type must be one_time or subscription';
  END IF;

  IF p_start_date IS NULL OR p_start_date < CURRENT_DATE THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Delivery start date cannot be in the past';
  END IF;

  -- Confirm customer exists
  PERFORM 1
    FROM customers
   WHERE id = p_customer_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Customer not found';
  END IF;

  -- Read the LIVE menu price from the database.
  -- The frontend cannot manually alter the final order amount.
  SELECT price, active
    INTO v_menu_price, v_menu_active
    FROM menu_items
   WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;

  IF NOT FOUND THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  END IF;

  IF v_menu_active = false THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  -- One-time order rules
  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    IF p_plan_id IS NOT NULL THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'One-time orders must not have a plan';
    END IF;

    v_delivery_count := 1;

    INSERT INTO orders (
      customer_id,
      menu_item_id,
      order_type,
      plan_id,
      plan_credits,
      total_amount,
      payment_status,
      payment_mode,
      notes
    )
    VALUES (
      p_customer_id,
      p_menu_item_id,
      'one_time',
      NULL,
      NULL,
      v_menu_price,
      p_payment_status,
      p_payment_mode,
      NULLIF(trim(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '')
    )
    RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;
  END IF;

  -- Subscription order rules
  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
    IF p_plan_id IS NULL THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
    END IF;

    SELECT credits, active
      INTO v_plan_credits, v_plan_active
      FROM plans
     WHERE id = p_plan_id;

    IF NOT FOUND THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'Plan not found';
    END IF;

    IF v_plan_active = false THEN
      RAISE EXCEPTION 'This plan is no longer active';
    END IF;

    v_delivery_count := v_plan_credits;

    INSERT INTO orders (
      customer_id,
      menu_item_id,
      order_type,
      plan_id,
      plan_credits,
      total_amount,
      payment_status,
      payment_mode,
      notes
    )
    VALUES (
      p_customer_id,
      p_menu_item_id,
      'subscription',
      p_plan_id,
      v_plan_credits,
      v_menu_price * v_plan_credits,
      p_payment_status,
      p_payment_mode,
      NULLIF(trim(COALESCE(p_notes, '')), '')
    )
    RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;
  END IF;

  -- Option A:
  -- Generate all delivery rows upfront, one per calendar day.
  FOR v_i IN 0..(v_delivery_count - 1) LOOP
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + v_i, 'pending');
  END LOOP;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;

-- Let the dashboard call the function using the Supabase anon key.
GRANT EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.create_order_with_deliveries(
  UUID, UUID, TEXT, UUID, TEXT, TEXT, TEXT, DATE
) TO anon, authenticated;

The current schema means this calculation:

text

Subscription total = selected menu item price × plan credits
Example:

text

Veg Thali = Rs.120
7-meal plan = Rs.120 × 7 = Rs.840
30-meal plan = Rs.120 × 30 = Rs.3,600
This is editable because you can change the menu price in Supabase.

text

SQL function done. Pricing Option 2.
Meaning: for example, a 7-meal plan could be Rs.700 even if 7 individual meals total Rs.840.

# Script A - Components + App.jsx

@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'

export default function CustomerPicker({ selectedCustomer, onSelect }) {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
  const [results, setResults] = useState([])
  const [searching, setSearching] = useState(false)
  const [showNewForm, setShowNewForm] = useState(false)
  const [newCustomer, setNewCustomer] = useState({ name: '', contact: '', address: '' })
  const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!query.trim() || selectedCustomer) {
      setResults([])
      return
    }
    setSearching(true)
    const timer = setTimeout(async () => {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('customers')
        .select('id, name, contact, address')
        .or(`name.ilike.%${query}%,contact.ilike.%${query}%`)
        .limit(8)
      if (!error) setResults(data || [])
      setSearching(false)
    }, 300)
    return () => clearTimeout(timer)
  }, [query, selectedCustomer])

  async function handleCreate() {
    setError('')
    if (!newCustomer.name.trim() || !newCustomer.contact.trim() || !newCustomer.address.trim()) {
      setError('Name, contact, and address are all required.')
      return
    }
    setCreating(true)
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('customers')
      .insert({
        name: newCustomer.name.trim(),
        contact: newCustomer.contact.trim(),
        address: newCustomer.address.trim(),
      })
      .select()
      .single()
    setCreating(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
      return
    }
    onSelect(data)
    setShowNewForm(false)
    setNewCustomer({ name: '', contact: '', address: '' })
  }

  if (selectedCustomer) {
    return (
      <div className="border rounded-md p-3 bg-green-50 border-green-200 flex justify-between items-center">
        <div>
          <p className="font-medium text-sm">{selectedCustomer.name}</p>
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-600">
            {selectedCustomer.contact} - {selectedCustomer.address}
          </p>
        </div>
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={() => onSelect(null)}
          className="text-xs text-red-600 hover:underline"
        >
          Change
        </button>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div>
      {!showNewForm ? (
        <>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={query}
            onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Search customer by name or phone..."
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          {searching && <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1">Searching...</p>}
          {results.length > 0 && (
            <div className="border rounded-md mt-1 max-h-48 overflow-y-auto">
              {results.map((c) => (
                <button
                  type="button"
                  key={c.id}
                  onClick={() => { onSelect(c); setQuery('') }}
                  className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 text-sm border-b last:border-b-0"
                >
                  <p className="font-medium">{c.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{c.contact}</p>
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
          {query.trim() && !searching && results.length === 0 && (
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">No matches found.</p>
          )}
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setShowNewForm(true)}
            className="text-xs text-green-700 font-medium mt-2 hover:underline"
          >
            + Create new customer
          </button>
        </>
      ) : (
        <div className="border rounded-md p-3 space-y-2">
          {error && <p className="text-xs text-red-600">{error}</p>}
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Full name"
            value={newCustomer.name}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, name: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Phone number"
            value={newCustomer.contact}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, contact: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Delivery address"
            value={newCustomer.address}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, address: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            <button
              type="button"
              disabled={creating}
              onClick={handleCreate}
              className="bg-green-600 text-white text-sm px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {creating ? 'Saving...' : 'Save Customer'}
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => { setShowNewForm(false); setError('') }}
              className="text-sm px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md border"
            >
              Cancel
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'

export default function MenuPicker({ selectedItem, onSelect }) {
  const [categories, setCategories] = useState([])
  const [items, setItems] = useState([])
  const [categoryId, setCategoryId] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      setLoading(true)
      const [catRes, itemRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('menu_categories').select('id, name').order('sort_order'),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name, price, category_id').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])
      if (catRes.error || itemRes.error) {
        setError((catRes.error || itemRes.error).message)
      } else {
        setCategories(catRes.data || [])
        setItems(itemRes.data || [])
      }
      setLoading(false)
    }
    load()
  }, [])

  const filteredItems = categoryId ? items.filter((i) => i.category_id === categoryId) : items

  if (loading) return <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">Loading menu...</p>
  if (error) return <p className="text-sm text-red-600">Error loading menu: {error}</p>
  if (items.length === 0)
    return (
      <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">
        No active menu items found. Add some in Supabase - menu_items.
      </p>
    )

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      <select
        value={categoryId}
        onChange={(e) => { setCategoryId(e.target.value); onSelect(null) }}
        className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
      >
        <option value="">All Categories</option>
        {categories.map((c) => (
          <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>
        ))}
      </select>
      <select
        value={selectedItem?.id || ''}
        onChange={(e) => {
          const item = filteredItems.find((i) => i.id === e.target.value)
          onSelect(item || null)
        }}
        className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
      >
        <option value="">Select a menu item...</option>
        {filteredItems.map((i) => (
          <option key={i.id} value={i.id}>
            {i.name} - Rs.{Number(i.price).toFixed(2)}
          </option>
        ))}
      </select>
    </div>
  )
}

if (!message) return null

const styles = {

x
</button>
)}
</div>
)
}

# src/components/Alert.jsx
@'
export default function Alert({ type = 'info', message, onClose }) {
  if (!message) return null

  const styles = {
    error: 'bg-red-50 text-red-800 border-red-200',
    success: 'bg-green-50 text-green-800 border-green-200',
    info: 'bg-blue-50 text-blue-800 border-blue-200',
  }

  return (
    <div className={`border rounded-md px-4 py-3 mb-4 flex justify-between items-start ${styles[type]}`}>
      <span className="text-sm">{message}</span>
      {onClose && (
        <button onClick={onClose} className="ml-4 text-sm font-bold opacity-60 hover:opacity-100">
          x
        </button>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}
'@ | Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 src/components/Alert.jsx

# src/components/CustomerPicker.jsx
@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'

export default function CustomerPicker({ selectedCustomer, onSelect }) {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
  const [results, setResults] = useState([])
  const [searching, setSearching] = useState(false)
  const [showNewForm, setShowNewForm] = useState(false)
  const [newCustomer, setNewCustomer] = useState({ name: '', contact: '', address: '' })
  const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!query.trim() || selectedCustomer) {
      setResults([])
      return
    }
    setSearching(true)
    const timer = setTimeout(async () => {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('customers')
        .select('id, name, contact, address')
        .or(`name.ilike.%${query}%,contact.ilike.%${query}%`)
        .limit(8)
      if (!error) setResults(data || [])
      setSearching(false)
    }, 300)
    return () => clearTimeout(timer)
  }, [query, selectedCustomer])

  async function handleCreate() {
    setError('')
    if (!newCustomer.name.trim() || !newCustomer.contact.trim() || !newCustomer.address.trim()) {
      setError('Name, contact, and address are all required.')
      return
    }
    setCreating(true)
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('customers')
      .insert({
        name: newCustomer.name.trim(),
        contact: newCustomer.contact.trim(),
        address: newCustomer.address.trim(),
      })
      .select()
      .single()
    setCreating(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
      return
    }
    onSelect(data)
    setShowNewForm(false)
    setNewCustomer({ name: '', contact: '', address: '' })
  }

  if (selectedCustomer) {
    return (
      <div className="border rounded-md p-3 bg-green-50 border-green-200 flex justify-between items-center">
        <div>
          <p className="font-medium text-sm">{selectedCustomer.name}</p>
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-600">
            {selectedCustomer.contact} - {selectedCustomer.address}
          </p>
        </div>
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={() => onSelect(null)}
          className="text-xs text-red-600 hover:underline"
        >
          Change
        </button>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div>
      {!showNewForm ? (
        <>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={query}
            onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Search customer by name or phone..."
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          {searching && <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1">Searching...</p>}
          {results.length > 0 && (
            <div className="border rounded-md mt-1 max-h-48 overflow-y-auto">
              {results.map((c) => (
                <button
                  type="button"
                  key={c.id}
                  onClick={() => { onSelect(c); setQuery('') }}
                  className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 text-sm border-b last:border-b-0"
                >
                  <p className="font-medium">{c.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{c.contact}</p>
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
          {query.trim() && !searching && results.length === 0 && (
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">No matches found.</p>
          )}
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setShowNewForm(true)}
            className="text-xs text-green-700 font-medium mt-2 hover:underline"
          >
            + Create new customer
          </button>
        </>
      ) : (
        <div className="border rounded-md p-3 space-y-2">
          {error && <p className="text-xs text-red-600">{error}</p>}
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Full name"
            value={newCustomer.name}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, name: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Phone number"
            value={newCustomer.contact}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, contact: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Delivery address"
            value={newCustomer.address}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, address: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            <button
              type="button"
              disabled={creating}
              onClick={handleCreate}
              className="bg-green-600 text-white text-sm px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {creating ? 'Saving...' : 'Save Customer'}
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => { setShowNewForm(false); setError('') }}
              className="text-sm px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md border"
            >
              Cancel
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}
'@ | Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 src/components/CustomerPicker.jsx

# src/components/MenuPicker.jsx
@'
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'

export default function MenuPicker({ selectedItem, onSelect }) {
  const [categories, setCategories] = useState([])
  const [items, setItems] = useState([])
  const [categoryId, setCategoryId] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      setLoading(true)
      const [catRes, itemRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('menu_categories').select('id, name').order('sort_order'),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name, price, category_id').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])
      if (catRes.error || itemRes.error) {
        setError((catRes.error || itemRes.error).message)
      } else {
        setCategories(catRes.data || [])
        setItems(itemRes.data || [])
      }
      setLoading(false)
    }
    load()
  }, [])

  const filteredItems = categoryId ? items.filter((i) => i.category_id === categoryId) : items

  if (loading) return <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">Loading menu...</p>
  if (error) return <p className="text-sm text-red-600">Error loading menu: {error}</p>
  if (items.length === 0)
    return (
      <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">
        No active menu items found. Add some in Supabase - menu_items.
      </p>
    )

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      <select
        value={categoryId}
        onChange={(e) => { setCategoryId(e.target.value); onSelect(null) }}
        className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
      >
        <option value="">All Categories</option>
        {categories.map((c) => (
          <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>
        ))}
      </select>
      <select
        value={selectedItem?.id || ''}
        onChange={(e) => {
          const item = filteredItems.find((i) => i.id === e.target.value)
          onSelect(item || null)
        }}
        className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
      >
        <option value="">Select a menu item...</option>
        {filteredItems.map((i) => (
          <option key={i.id} value={i.id}>
            {i.name} - Rs.{Number(i.price).toFixed(2)}
          </option>
        ))}
      </select>
    </div>
  )
}
'@ | Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 src/components/MenuPicker.jsx

# src/lib/date.js
@'
export function todayDateString() {
  const d = new Date()
  return formatDate(d)
}

export function addDaysToDateString(dateStr, days) {
  const d = new Date(dateStr + 'T00:00:00')
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + days)
  return formatDate(d)
}

function formatDate(d) {
  const year = d.getFullYear()
  const month = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
  const day = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')
  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`
}

claude-sonnet-4-6
Found the Problem — PowerShell Uses Different Commands
The cat << 'EOF' syntax is Linux/Mac only. PowerShell doesn't understand it. That's why every file failed. But the good news:

The git clone worked perfectly. You're in the right folder. We just need PowerShell-compatible commands.

The Fix — One Single PowerShell Script
Copy this entire block, paste it into PowerShell all at once, press Enter:

PowerShell

# Create folders
New-Item -ItemType Directory -Force -Path ".github/workflows","src/lib","src/components","src/pages","public" | Out-Null

Let's Fix This — Tell Me Exactly What You're Seeing
First — What Terminal Are You Using?
Look at what's open on your computer right now:

What it looks like	What it is	Tell me
Black/dark window, says "bash" or "$" at the end	Git Bash	"Git Bash"
Blue window, says "PS" before the cursor	PowerShell	"PowerShell"
Black window, says "C:>"	Command Prompt	"CMD"
Mac — white/dark window with "%" or "$"	Mac Terminal	"Mac Terminal"
Second — What Error Are You Seeing?
Paste the exact error text here. Common ones and what they mean:

Error you see	What it means
'cat' is not recognized	You're in CMD or PowerShell — wrong terminal
git: command not found	Git isn't installed
Permission denied	Need to run as administrator
fatal: repository not found	Git clone URL issue
Quickest Fix — Skip Terminal Completely
Since you're hitting terminal issues, let's use GitHub's website instead. It's actually faster for someone not used to terminal.

Here's the plan — I give you files one at a time, you create them directly on GitHub. No terminal needed at all until the very end (just 2 commands).

Do you want to switch to this approach? Just say yes and I'll start immediately — one file at a time, copy-paste into GitHub's web editor.

OR

Tell me your terminal type + paste the exact error and I'll fix the terminal approach.

Which is easier for you right now?

What That Status Page Actually Says

text

Workers AI experiencing degraded availability 
(affects @cf/moonshotai/kimi-k2.6 and kimi-k2.7-code models)
This is Cloudflare's AI product — completely unrelated to DNS, domains, or your website hosting. Your DNS management is not affected at all.

The 521 error you saw earlier was likely a temporary dashboard glitch. DNS itself is working fine.

Try Cloudflare Dashboard Again Right Now
Open a fresh tab:

text

https://dash.cloudflare.com
Log in → click lunchmate.live → DNS → Records

If it loads normally → add the 4 A records I listed earlier and come back.

If it still shows 521 → we skip Cloudflare for now and do DNS a different way (directly through your domain registrar — Namecheap). The build still proceeds in parallel.

Don't Wait on This — Start the Terminal Build Now
Cloudflare DNS can be fixed anytime. The code build is what unlocks everything else.

Open your terminal (Git Bash on Windows, Terminal on Mac) and run this:

"Request failed with status 521" — Easy Fix
What This Error Means
521 is not a DNS error — it's a Cloudflare error that means "the web server refused the connection." This is happening because:

Your www.lunchmate.live CNAME is set to Proxied (orange cloud)
Cloudflare is trying to proxy traffic through to GitHub Pages
But GitHub Pages hasn't verified your domain yet — so it's refusing Cloudflare's connection
This causes the 521 error even when you try to add a new DNS record (Cloudflare's own dashboard is hitting this conflict)
The fix is simple: turn off the orange proxy on your existing www record first.

Fix — Do This in Order
Step 1: Fix the existing www record first
Close this "Add record" popup (click Cancel)
Click "Edit" on the existing www.lunchmate.live CNAME row

claude-sonnet-5-high
Confirmed. Building Full Module Now.
Before the frontend code — one small addition to your database is required. Here's why, then the code.

⚠️ Run This One More SQL Block First
Your original schema is solid, but "Option A" (generate all delivery rows on order creation) needs to happen atomically — meaning: if creating the order succeeds but creating deliveries fails halfway, you'd end up with a broken half-order. To prevent that, I'm adding one Postgres function that does both in a single all-or-nothing transaction.

This does NOT touch your existing tables or data — it only adds one new function.

Go to SQL Editor → paste this → Run:

SQL

-- ============================================================
-- ADDENDUM: Atomic order + delivery creation (Option A)
-- Run this once. Does not affect existing tables/data.
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION create_order_with_deliveries(
  p_customer_id    UUID,
  p_menu_item_id   UUID,
  p_order_type     TEXT,
  p_plan_id        UUID,
  p_plan_credits   INTEGER,
  p_total_amount   NUMERIC,
  p_payment_status TEXT,
  p_payment_mode   TEXT,
  p_notes          TEXT,
  p_start_date     DATE
)
RETURNS UUID
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
SET search_path = public
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_id    UUID;
  v_menu_active BOOLEAN;
  v_i           INTEGER;
BEGIN
  -- Server-side validation (defense in depth, even if frontend already checks)
  SELECT active INTO v_menu_active FROM menu_items WHERE id = p_menu_item_id;
  IF v_menu_active IS NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Menu item not found';
  ELSIF v_menu_active = false THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'This menu item is no longer active';
  END IF;

  IF p_order_type = 'subscription' AND (p_plan_id IS NULL OR p_plan_credits IS NULL) THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'Subscription orders require a plan';
  END IF;

  IF p_start_date IS NULL THEN
    RAISE EXCEPTION 'A delivery start date is required';
  END IF;

  -- Create the order
  INSERT INTO orders (
    customer_id, menu_item_id, order_type, plan_id, plan_credits,
    total_amount, payment_status, payment_mode, notes
  )
  VALUES (
    p_customer_id, p_menu_item_id, p_order_type, p_plan_id, p_plan_credits,
    p_total_amount, p_payment_status, p_payment_mode, p_notes
  )
  RETURNING id INTO v_order_id;

  -- Create delivery rows
  IF p_order_type = 'one_time' THEN
    INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
    VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date, 'pending');
  ELSE
    FOR v_i IN 0..(p_plan_credits - 1) LOOP
      INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
      VALUES (v_order_id, p_start_date + (v_i || ' days')::INTERVAL, 'pending');
    END LOOP;
  END IF;

  RETURN v_order_id;
END;
$$;
Confirm this ran ("Success. No rows returned") before wiring the frontend to it — but I'll give you the code now so you're not blocked.

src/lib/supabase.js
