import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'

const supabaseUrl = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_URL
const supabaseAnonKey = import.meta.env.VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY

if (!supabaseUrl || !supabaseAnonKey) {
  throw new Error(
    'Missing Supabase env vars. Check your .env file (local dev) or GitHub Actions secrets (production).'
  )
}

export const supabase = createClient(supabaseUrl, supabaseAnonKey)
src/lib/date.js
JavaScript

// Local-timezone-safe date helpers (avoids UTC offset bugs from toISOString())

export function todayDateString() {
  const d = new Date()
  return formatDate(d)
}

export function addDaysToDateString(dateStr, days) {
  const d = new Date(dateStr + 'T00:00:00')
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + days)
  return formatDate(d)
}

function formatDate(d) {
  const year = d.getFullYear()
  const month = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
  const day = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')
  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`
}
src/components/Alert.jsx
React

export default function Alert({ type = 'info', message, onClose }) {
  if (!message) return null

  const styles = {
    error: 'bg-red-50 text-red-800 border-red-200',
    success: 'bg-green-50 text-green-800 border-green-200',
    info: 'bg-blue-50 text-blue-800 border-blue-200',
  }

  return (
    <div className={`border rounded-md px-4 py-3 mb-4 flex justify-between items-start ${styles[type]}`}>
      <span className="text-sm">{message}</span>
      {onClose && (
        <button onClick={onClose} className="ml-4 text-sm font-bold opacity-60 hover:opacity-100">
          ✕
        </button>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}
src/components/CustomerPicker.jsx
React

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'

export default function CustomerPicker({ selectedCustomer, onSelect }) {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('')
  const [results, setResults] = useState([])
  const [searching, setSearching] = useState(false)
  const [showNewForm, setShowNewForm] = useState(false)
  const [newCustomer, setNewCustomer] = useState({ name: '', contact: '', address: '' })
  const [creating, setCreating] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!query.trim() || selectedCustomer) {
      setResults([])
      return
    }
    setSearching(true)
    const timer = setTimeout(async () => {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('customers')
        .select('id, name, contact, address')
        .or(`name.ilike.%${query}%,contact.ilike.%${query}%`)
        .limit(8)
      if (!error) setResults(data || [])
      setSearching(false)
    }, 300)
    return () => clearTimeout(timer)
  }, [query, selectedCustomer])

  async function handleCreate() {
    setError('')
    if (!newCustomer.name.trim() || !newCustomer.contact.trim() || !newCustomer.address.trim()) {
      setError('Name, contact, and address are all required.')
      return
    }
    setCreating(true)
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('customers')
      .insert({
        name: newCustomer.name.trim(),
        contact: newCustomer.contact.trim(),
        address: newCustomer.address.trim(),
      })
      .select()
      .single()
    setCreating(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
      return
    }
    onSelect(data)
    setShowNewForm(false)
    setNewCustomer({ name: '', contact: '', address: '' })
  }

  if (selectedCustomer) {
    return (
      <div className="border rounded-md p-3 bg-green-50 border-green-200 flex justify-between items-center">
        <div>
          <p className="font-medium text-sm">{selectedCustomer.name}</p>
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-600">
            {selectedCustomer.contact} · {selectedCustomer.address}
          </p>
        </div>
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={() => onSelect(null)}
          className="text-xs text-red-600 hover:underline"
        >
          Change
        </button>
      </div>
    )
  }

  return (
    <div>
      {!showNewForm ? (
        <>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={query}
            onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Search customer by name or phone..."
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          {searching && <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1">Searching...</p>}
          {results.length > 0 && (
            <div className="border rounded-md mt-1 max-h-48 overflow-y-auto">
              {results.map((c) => (
                <button
                  type="button"
                  key={c.id}
                  onClick={() => { onSelect(c); setQuery('') }}
                  className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-gray-50 text-sm border-b last:border-b-0"
                >
                  <p className="font-medium">{c.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{c.contact}</p>
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
          {query.trim() && !searching && results.length === 0 && (
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">No matches found.</p>
          )}
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setShowNewForm(true)}
            className="text-xs text-green-700 font-medium mt-2 hover:underline"
          >
            + Create new customer
          </button>
        </>
      ) : (
        <div className="border rounded-md p-3 space-y-2">
          {error && <p className="text-xs text-red-600">{error}</p>}
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Full name"
            value={newCustomer.name}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, name: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Phone number"
            value={newCustomer.contact}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, contact: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <input
            type="text"
            placeholder="Delivery address"
            value={newCustomer.address}
            onChange={(e) => setNewCustomer({ ...newCustomer, address: e.target.value })}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            <button
              type="button"
              disabled={creating}
              onClick={handleCreate}
              className="bg-green-600 text-white text-sm px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {creating ? 'Saving...' : 'Save Customer'}
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => { setShowNewForm(false); setError('') }}
              className="text-sm px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md border"
            >
              Cancel
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}
src/components/MenuPicker.jsx
React

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'

export default function MenuPicker({ selectedItem, onSelect }) {
  const [categories, setCategories] = useState([])
  const [items, setItems] = useState([])
  const [categoryId, setCategoryId] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function load() {
      setLoading(true)
      const [catRes, itemRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.from('menu_categories').select('id, name').order('sort_order'),
        supabase.from('menu_items').select('id, name, price, category_id').eq('active', true).order('name'),
      ])
      if (catRes.error || itemRes.error) {
        setError((catRes.error || itemRes.error).message)
      } else {
        setCategories(catRes.data || [])
        setItems(itemRes.data || [])
      }
      setLoading(false)
    }
    load()
  }, [])

  const filteredItems = categoryId ? items.filter((i) => i.category_id === categoryId) : items

  if (loading) return <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">Loading menu...</p>
  if (error) return <p className="text-sm text-red-600">Error loading menu: {error}</p>
  if (items.length === 0)
    return (
      <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">
        No active menu items found. Add some in Supabase → menu_items.
      </p>
    )

  return (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      <select
        value={categoryId}
        onChange={(e) => { setCategoryId(e.target.value); onSelect(null) }}
        className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
      >
        <option value="">All Categories</option>
        {categories.map((c) => (
          <option key={c.id} value={c.id}>{c.name}</option>
        ))}
      </select>
      <select
        value={selectedItem?.id || ''}
        onChange={(e) => {
          const item = filteredItems.find((i) => i.id === e.target.value)
          onSelect(item || null)
        }}
        className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
      >
        <option value="">Select a menu item...</option>
        {filteredItems.map((i) => (
          <option key={i.id} value={i.id}>
            {i.name} — ₹{Number(i.price).toFixed(2)}
          </option>
        ))}
      </select>
    </div>
  )
}
src/pages/NewOrder.jsx
React

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString, addDaysToDateString } from '../lib/date'
import CustomerPicker from '../components/CustomerPicker'
import MenuPicker from '../components/MenuPicker'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const PAYMENT_MODES = [
  { value: 'cash', label: 'Cash' },
  { value: 'upi', label: 'UPI' },
  { value: 'bank_transfer', label: 'Bank Transfer' },
  { value: 'card', label: 'Card' },
  { value: 'other', label: 'Other' },
]

export default function NewOrder() {
  const [customer, setCustomer] = useState(null)
  const [orderType, setOrderType] = useState('one_time')
  const [menuItem, setMenuItem] = useState(null)
  const [plans, setPlans] = useState([])
  const [planId, setPlanId] = useState('')
  const [startDate, setStartDate] = useState(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
  const [paymentStatus, setPaymentStatus] = useState('not_paid')
  const [paymentMode, setPaymentMode] = useState('cash')
  const [notes, setNotes] = useState('')
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [success, setSuccess] = useState('')

  useEffect(() => {
    async function loadPlans() {
      const { data, error } = await supabase
        .from('plans')
        .select('id, name, credits')
        .eq('active', true)
        .order('credits')
      if (!error) setPlans(data || [])
    }
    loadPlans()
  }, [])

  const selectedPlan = plans.find((p) => p.id === planId) || null
  const unitCount = orderType === 'subscription' ? (selectedPlan?.credits || 0) : 1
  const totalAmount = menuItem ? Number(menuItem.price) * unitCount : 0

  function resetForm() {
    setCustomer(null)
    setOrderType('one_time')
    setMenuItem(null)
    setPlanId('')
    setStartDate(addDaysToDateString(todayDateString(), 1))
    setPaymentStatus('not_paid')
    setPaymentMode('cash')
    setNotes('')
  }

  function validate() {
    if (!customer) return 'Please select or create a customer.'
    if (!menuItem) return 'Please select a menu item.'
    if (orderType === 'subscription' && !selectedPlan) return 'Please select a plan for the subscription.'
    if (!startDate) return 'Please pick a delivery date.'
    if (startDate < todayDateString()) return 'Delivery date cannot be in the past.'
    if (totalAmount <= 0) return 'Total amount must be greater than zero.'
    return ''
  }

  async function handleSubmit(e) {
    e.preventDefault()
    setError('')
    setSuccess('')
    const validationError = validate()
    if (validationError) {
      setError(validationError)
      return
    }

    setSubmitting(true)
    const { error } = await supabase.rpc('create_order_with_deliveries', {
      p_customer_id: customer.id,
      p_menu_item_id: menuItem.id,
      p_order_type: orderType,
      p_plan_id: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.id : null,
      p_plan_credits: orderType === 'subscription' ? selectedPlan.credits : null,
      p_total_amount: totalAmount,
      p_payment_status: paymentStatus,
      p_payment_mode: paymentMode,
      p_notes: notes.trim() || null,
      p_start_date: startDate,
    })
    setSubmitting(false)

    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to log order: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }

    setSuccess(
      orderType === 'subscription'
        ? `Order logged! ${selectedPlan.credits} deliveries scheduled starting ${startDate}.`
        : `Order logged! Delivery scheduled for ${startDate}.`
    )
    resetForm()
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-xl mx-auto bg-white rounded-lg shadow-sm border p-6">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold mb-4">New Order</h1>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />
      <Alert type="success" message={success} onClose={() => setSuccess('')} />

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-5">
        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Customer</label>
          <CustomerPicker selectedCustomer={customer} onSelect={setCustomer} />
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Order Type</label>
          <div className="flex gap-4">
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'one_time'}
                onChange={() => { setOrderType('one_time'); setPlanId('') }}
              />
              One-time order
            </label>
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
              <input
                type="radio"
                checked={orderType === 'subscription'}
                onChange={() => setOrderType('subscription')}
              />
              Subscription
            </label>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Menu Item</label>
          <MenuPicker selectedItem={menuItem} onSelect={setMenuItem} />
        </div>

        {orderType === 'subscription' && (
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Plan</label>
            {plans.length === 0 ? (
              <p className="text-sm text-amber-600">No active plans found. Add some in Supabase → plans.</p>
            ) : (
              <select
                value={planId}
                onChange={(e) => setPlanId(e.target.value)}
                className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
              >
                <option value="">Select a plan...</option>
                {plans.map((p) => (
                  <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>{p.name} ({p.credits} credits)</option>
                ))}
              </select>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">
            {orderType === 'subscription' ? 'Delivery Start Date' : 'Delivery Date'}
          </label>
          <input
            type="date"
            value={startDate}
            min={todayDateString()}
            onChange={(e) => setStartDate(e.target.value)}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
          />
        </div>

        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Status</label>
            <select
              value={paymentStatus}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentStatus(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              <option value="not_paid">Not Paid</option>
              <option value="paid">Paid</option>
            </select>
          </div>
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Payment Mode</label>
            <select
              value={paymentMode}
              onChange={(e) => setPaymentMode(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            >
              {PAYMENT_MODES.map((m) => (
                <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label}</option>
              ))}
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="block text-sm font-medium mb-1">Notes (optional)</label>
          <textarea
            value={notes}
            onChange={(e) => setNotes(e.target.value)}
            rows={2}
            className="w-full border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm"
            placeholder="Allergies, gate code, delivery instructions..."
          />
        </div>

        <div className="border-t pt-4 flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Total Amount</p>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-700">₹{totalAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
            {orderType === 'subscription' && selectedPlan && menuItem && (
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">
                ₹{Number(menuItem.price).toFixed(2)} × {selectedPlan.credits} meals
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          <button
            type="submit"
            disabled={submitting}
            className="bg-green-600 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-md font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {submitting ? 'Logging Order...' : 'Log Order'}
          </button>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  )
}
src/pages/Deliveries.jsx
React

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { todayDateString } from '../lib/date'
import Alert from '../components/Alert'

const STATUS_STYLES = {
  pending: 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800',
  delivered: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800',
  missed: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800',
  cancelled: 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-600',
}

export default function Deliveries() {
  const [deliveries, setDeliveries] = useState([])
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
  const [error, setError] = useState('')
  const [updatingId, setUpdatingId] = useState(null)

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    setError('')
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from('deliveries')
      .select(`
        id, scheduled_date, status, notes,
        orders (
          id, order_type, plan_credits, credits_used,
          customers ( name, contact, address ),
          menu_items ( name )
        )
      `)
      .eq('scheduled_date', todayDateString())
      .order('id')

    if (error) {
      setError(error.message)
    } else {
      setDeliveries(data || [])
    }
    setLoading(false)
  }, [])

  useEffect(() => { load() }, [load])

  async function updateStatus(deliveryId, newStatus) {
    setUpdatingId(deliveryId)
    setError('')
    const { error } = await supabase
      .from('deliveries')
      .update({ status: newStatus })
      .eq('id', deliveryId)
    setUpdatingId(null)
    if (error) {
      setError(`Failed to update delivery: ${error.message}`)
      return
    }
    load()
  }

  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Today's Deliveries</h1>
        <button onClick={load} className="text-sm text-green-700 hover:underline">Refresh</button>
      </div>

      <Alert type="error" message={error} onClose={() => setError('')} />

      {loading ? (
        <p className="text-sm text-gray-400">Loading...</p>
      ) : deliveries.length === 0 ? (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg p-8 text-center text-gray-500 text-sm">
          No deliveries scheduled for today.
        </div>
      ) : (
        <div className="bg-white border rounded-lg overflow-hidden">
          <table className="w-full text-sm">
            <thead className="bg-gray-50 text-left text-gray-500 text-xs uppercase">
              <tr>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Customer</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Item</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Type</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2">Status</th>
                <th className="px-4 py-2 text-right">Actions</th>
              </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
              {deliveries.map((d) => {
                const order = d.orders
                const customer = order?.customers
                const item = order?.menu_items
                const isPending = d.status === 'pending'
                return (
                  <tr key={d.id} className="border-t">
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <p className="font-medium">{customer?.name || '—'}</p>
                      <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">{customer?.contact}</p>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">{item?.name || '—'}</td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      {order?.order_type === 'subscription' ? (
                        <span className="text-xs">
                          Subscription
                          <span className="text-gray-400"> ({order.credits_used}/{order.plan_credits})</span>
                        </span>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs">One-time</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3">
                      <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${STATUS_STYLES[d.status]}`}>
                        {d.status}
                      </span>
                    </td>
                    <td className="px-4 py-3 text-right">
                      {isPending ? (
                        <div className="flex gap-2 justify-end">
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateStatus(d.id, 'delivered')}
                            className="bg-green-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Delivered
                          </button>
                          <button
                            disabled={updatingId === d.id}
                            onClick={() => updateStatus(d.id, 'missed')}
                            className="bg-red-600 text-white text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md disabled:opacity-50"
                          >
                            Missed
                          </button>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">—</span>
                      )}
                    </td>
                  </tr>
                )
              })}
            </tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

import NewOrder from './pages/NewOrder.jsx'

export default function App() {
  return (
    <HashRouter>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50">

          <div className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">

            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <NavLink
                to="/"
                end
                className={({ isActive }) =>
                  `px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm font-medium ${isActive ? 'bg-green-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-100'}`
                }
              >
                New Order
              </NavLink>
              <NavLink
                to="/deliveries"
                className={({ isActive }) =>
                  `px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm font-medium ${isActive ? 'bg-green-600 text-white' : 'text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-100'}`
                }
              >
                Today's Deliveries
              </NavLink>
            </div>
          </div>
        </nav>
        <main className="max-w-5xl mx-auto px-4 py-6">
          <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<NewOrder />} />
            <Route path="/deliveries" element={<Deliveries />} />
          </Routes>
        </main>
      </div>
    </HashRouter>
  )
}
Note: Using HashRouter (URLs look like /#/deliveries) instead of BrowserRouter — this avoids the classic GitHub Pages "404 on refresh" problem since it's a static host with no server-side rewrites.

.github/workflows/deploy.yml
YAML

name: Deploy to GitHub Pages

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  workflow_dispatch:

permissions:
  contents: read
  pages: write
  id-token: write

concurrency:
  group: pages
  cancel-in-progress: true

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          cache: npm

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Build
        run: npm run build
        env:
          VITE_SUPABASE_URL: ${{ secrets.SUPABASE_URL }}
          VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY: ${{ secrets.SUPABASE_ANON_KEY }}

      - uses: actions/configure-pages@v5

      - uses: actions/upload-pages-artifact@v3
        with:
          path: ./dist

  deploy:
    needs: build
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment:
      name: github-pages
      url: ${{ steps.deployment.outputs.page_url }}
    steps:
      - id: deployment
        uses: actions/deploy-pages@v4
This reads your existing SUPABASE_URL / SUPABASE_ANON_KEY GitHub secrets and maps them to the VITE_ prefix Vite requires at build time — no need to rename your secrets.

SQL

-- ============================================================
-- LUNCHMATE OS — MODULE 1 SCHEMA
-- ============================================================

CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- customers
CREATE TABLE customers (
  id         UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  name       TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
  contact    TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(contact)) >= 7),
  address    TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(address)) > 0),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

-- menu_categories
CREATE TABLE menu_categories (
  id         UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  name       TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
  sort_order INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
);

-- menu_items
CREATE TABLE menu_items (
  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  category_id UUID REFERENCES menu_categories(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  name        TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
  price       NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
  cost        NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (cost >= 0),
  active      BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

-- plans
CREATE TABLE plans (
  id         UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  name       TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
  credits    INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (credits > 0),
  active     BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

INSERT INTO plans (name, credits) VALUES
  ('7-Meal Plan',  7),
  ('30-Meal Plan', 30);

-- orders
CREATE TABLE orders (
  id             UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  customer_id    UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES customers(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  menu_item_id   UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  order_type     TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (order_type IN ('one_time', 'subscription')),
  plan_id        UUID REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  plan_credits   INTEGER CHECK (plan_credits > 0),
  credits_used   INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  total_amount   NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (total_amount >= 0),
  payment_status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'not_paid'
                   CHECK (payment_status IN ('paid', 'not_paid')),
  payment_mode   TEXT CHECK (payment_mode IN (
                   'cash', 'upi', 'bank_transfer', 'card', 'other'
                 )),
  notes          TEXT,
  created_at     TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT subscription_needs_plan CHECK (
    (order_type = 'subscription' AND plan_id IS NOT NULL AND plan_credits IS NOT NULL)
    OR
    (order_type = 'one_time' AND plan_id IS NULL AND plan_credits IS NULL)
  ),
  CONSTRAINT credits_used_within_plan CHECK (
    plan_credits IS NULL OR credits_used <= plan_credits
  )
);

-- deliveries
CREATE TABLE deliveries (
  id             UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  order_id       UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES orders(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  scheduled_date DATE NOT NULL,
  status         TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending'
                   CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'delivered', 'missed', 'cancelled')),
  notes          TEXT,
  created_at     TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  UNIQUE (order_id, scheduled_date)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_scheduled_date ON deliveries (scheduled_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_order_id       ON deliveries (order_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_status         ON deliveries (status);

-- trigger function
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type   TEXT;
  v_plan_credits INTEGER;
  v_credits_used INTEGER;
  v_latest_date  DATE;
BEGIN
  IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used
    FROM orders
   WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

  -- on delivered: increment credits_used
  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN
    UPDATE orders
       SET credits_used = credits_used + 1
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id;
  END IF;

  -- on missed: extend schedule for subscriptions only
  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN
    IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN
      SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used
        FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

      IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN
        SELECT MAX(scheduled_date)
          INTO v_latest_date
          FROM deliveries
         WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;

        INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
          VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day', 'pending')
          ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;
      END IF;
    END IF;
  END IF;

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

CREATE TRIGGER trg_delivery_status_change
  AFTER UPDATE OF status ON deliveries
  FOR EACH ROW
  EXECUTE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change();

-- RLS
ALTER TABLE customers       ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE menu_categories ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE menu_items      ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE plans           ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE orders          ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE deliveries      ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

CREATE POLICY "allow_all_customers"       ON customers       FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_menu_categories" ON menu_categories FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_menu_items"      ON menu_items      FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plans"           ON plans           FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_orders"          ON orders          FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_deliveries"      ON deliveries      FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- seed categories
INSERT INTO menu_categories (name, sort_order) VALUES
  ('Thali',  1),
  ('Salad',  2),
  ('Snacks', 3);

-- seed menu items
INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active)
SELECT c.id, 'Veg Thali',     120.00, 55.00, true FROM menu_categories c WHERE c.name = 'Thali'
UNION ALL
SELECT c.id, 'Non-Veg Thali', 150.00, 75.00, true FROM menu_categories c WHERE c.name = 'Thali'
UNION ALL
SELECT c.id, 'Green Salad',    80.00, 30.00, true FROM menu_categories c WHERE c.name = 'Salad';

Question 2: Option A vs Option B — Delivery Row Generation
The Simple Version
This is about what happens the moment you log a new subscription order.

Imagine a customer just bought a 7-meal plan starting tomorrow.

Option A — "Create the Full Schedule Now"
The system immediately creates all 7 delivery rows in one go:

text

Order logged on: 15 July

Deliveries created instantly:
  📦 16 July → pending
  📦 17 July → pending
  📦 18 July → pending
  📦 19 July → pending
  📦 20 July → pending
  📦 21 July → pending
  📦 22 July → pending
What this means for you day-to-day:

Open "Today's Deliveries" on 18 July → you see this customer in the list automatically
You can see the full upcoming week's delivery schedule at any time
If customer misses 19 July → system pushes the last date from 22 July to 23 July automatically
Feels like a real delivery schedule / route sheet — replaces your Excel
The only downside:
If a customer says "actually start me from 20 July not 16 July" after you've already logged the order, you'd need to update a few rows in Supabase table editor. Not hard, just a manual fix.

Option B — "Create One Row at a Time, Roll Forward"
The system creates only the first delivery row right now:

text

Order logged on: 15 July

Deliveries created instantly:
  📦 16 July → pending

(nothing else yet)

When 16 July is marked "delivered" → system creates 17 July row
When 17 July is marked "delivered" → system creates 18 July row
...and so on until 7 credits are used
What this means for you day-to-day:

You can never see "next week's schedule" — only today's pending delivery exists at any moment
Simpler behind the scenes
Changing start date is easy — only one row to update
But you lose the delivery schedule view — you'd still need to mentally track who's getting delivery on which future day
Side by Side
Option A	Option B
Full schedule visible upfront?	✅ Yes	❌ No
Replaces your delivery Excel?	✅ Yes	❌ Partially
Easy to change start date?	⚠️ Edit a few rows	✅ Edit one row
"Today's Deliveries" auto-populates?	✅ Yes, always	✅ Yes, but only 1 day ahead
Missed day auto-extends?	✅ Yes	✅ Yes
Best for your business?	✅ Recommended	Only if schedules change often
My Recommendation — Option A
Because you said you want to kill Excel and manual tracking — Option A is the one that actually does that. Your "Today's Deliveries" screen becomes your route sheet automatically, every single day, for every customer, without you doing anything extra.

Orchestrated comprehensive setup guide with actionable configuration steps
Orchestrated comprehensive setup guide with actionable configuration steps
Step-by-Step Setup
Do these in order — each one unlocks the next.

Step 1: Create the Supabase project (10 min)
Go to supabase.com → Sign up with your GitHub account (keeps everything under one login).
Click New Project → name it lunchmate-os → pick a strong database password (save it somewhere — you'll need it once, rarely again) → choose the region closest to India (Singapore is usually closest).
Wait ~2 min for it to provision. You'll land on the project dashboard.
In the left sidebar, click Table Editor — this is your no-code admin panel. Bookmark this URL right now; this is where you'll manually edit prices later.
In the left sidebar, click Project Settings → API — note down your Project URL and anon public key. You'll paste these into the dashboard code once. (Don't share these publicly in a public repo — I'll show you how to keep them safe when we build.)
Step 2: Set up the GitHub repo (5 min)
You already have GitHub — go to github.com/new.
Name it lunchmate-os, keep it Public (required for free GitHub Pages), initialize with a README.
Settings → Pages → under "Build and deployment," set Source to GitHub Actions (this lets us auto-deploy every time you push code, no manual steps later).
Step 3: Claim your free domain via Student Pack (10 min)
Go to education.github.com/pack, confirm you're still verified as a student.
Find Namecheap in the offers list → claim the 1 free .me domain for 1 year.
Search for something like lunchmate.me or orderlunchmate.me and register it (free, just needs the Student Pack code).
Leave it as-is for now — you'll point it at Cloudflare in Step 4.
Step 4: Connect Cloudflare (10 min)
Go to cloudflare.com → sign up free.
Add a site → enter your new domain (lunchmate.me).
Cloudflare gives you two nameservers (e.g. ana.ns.cloudflare.com) — copy them.
Go back to Namecheap → your domain → Nameservers → switch to "Custom DNS" → paste Cloudflare's two nameservers.
Back in Cloudflare, add a CNAME record: name = @ (or www), target = yourusername.github.io. This is what makes lunchmate.me actually show your GitHub Pages site once it's live.
This step can take a few hours to propagate — totally normal, don't worry if it's not instant.
Step 5: Keep your Supabase keys safe (5 min)
In your GitHub repo, go to Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions → add two secrets: SUPABASE_URL and SUPABASE_ANON_KEY, pasting the values from Step 1.
This means your keys never sit exposed in your public code — the deployment process injects them safely at build time.
That's the entire "plumbing" — no money spent, everything free-tier or Student Pack, and it doesn't need to change even at 50+ orders/month.

Step 6: Build the first module
Everything above just prepares the ground. Now, here's the ready-to-paste prompt for Claude Code (or Cursor) to build the actual Customers + Orders + Meal Credits module — the core of the system, matching everything we've designed:

claude-sonnet-4-6
Lunchmate OS — Scaling Confirmed + Your Question Answered
Great question. Let me address both things directly.

Your Question: "Can this handle more than 50 clients in a month?"
Yes — comfortably. Here's the actual math:

Metric	Supabase Free Tier Limit	Your Usage at 50 clients/month
Database size	500 MB	~50 clients × 30 orders × 2KB per row ≈ 3 MB total
Database rows	Unlimited on free tier	~1,500 rows/month at 50 clients
API requests	50,000/month	~5,000/month at 50 clients
Concurrent users	200 simultaneous	You + 1–2 staff = 3 max
You would need to be running ~500+ active clients daily before Supabase free tier becomes a concern. 50/month is not even visible on their radar.

Now — The One Clarification I Need From You
Before I write a single line of frontend code, I need your answer to this question:

When a new subscription order is logged, how should delivery rows be generated?
Here are the two options. Please pick one:

Option A — Generate All N Rows Upfront

text

Customer buys 7-meal plan starting tomorrow →
System immediately creates 7 delivery rows:

  Day 1: 2025-07-16 → pending
  Day 2: 2025-07-17 → pending
  Day 3: 2025-07-18 → pending
  Day 4: 2025-07-19 → pending
  Day 5: 2025-07-20 → pending
  Day 6: 2025-07-21 → pending
  Day 7: 2025-07-22 → pending
Pros: You can see the full schedule in "Today's Deliveries" for any future date immediately.
Cons: If customer's start date shifts, you edit multiple rows. Missed-day trigger still handles extension correctly.

Option B — Generate Only the First Row, Then Roll Forward

text

Customer buys 7-meal plan starting tomorrow →
System creates only 1 delivery row:

  Day 1: 2025-07-16 → pending

When Day 1 is marked "delivered" → Day 2 row is auto-created
When Day 2 is marked "delivered" → Day 3 row is auto-created
...and so on until 7 credits are consumed
Pros: Clean. No future clutter. Start date changes are trivial.
Cons: You can't see the full upcoming schedule — only the next pending delivery exists at any moment.

My Recommendation for Your Business: Option A

Here's why it fits Lunchmate specifically:

"Today's Deliveries" screen becomes genuinely useful — you can see that tomorrow you have 12 deliveries scheduled without manually tracking anything
The missed-day trigger already handles extension correctly using MAX(scheduled_date) + 1 day — so even with all rows pre-generated, a missed day pushes the last row out by one more day
50 clients × 30 meals = 1,500 rows — completely trivial for Postgres
You said you want to kill Excel — Option A is the one that actually replaces your delivery schedule spreadsheet

The Process, In Short
Four layers, built in order, each one depending on the one before:

Data layer — one central place that stores customers, menu, orders, meal credits, expenses. Everything else just reads/writes to this.
No-code admin — a spreadsheet-like screen where you edit prices, menu items, and view raw data without touching code. This comes free the moment layer 1 exists.
Your dashboard — the actual app you look at: order entry, meal credit tracker, invoices, day/month profit. Talks to layer 1.
Hosting — puts the dashboard on a real link you and Manoj/Arya can open from any phone.
At 5–10 orders/day this whole stack runs on free tiers only — nothing here needs a credit card, and nothing here needs to change even if you hit 50+/month. You'd need to be doing hundreds of orders a day before any of this costs money.

Lunchmate OS — Module 1: Supabase SQL Schema
I've analyzed your requirements carefully. Before I build the frontend, here is the complete SQL to run in your Supabase SQL editor. Please read the clarification note at the bottom before running.

Step 1: Run This SQL in Supabase
SQL

-- ============================================================
-- LUNCHMATE OS — MODULE 1 SCHEMA
-- Run this entire block in Supabase SQL Editor
-- ============================================================

-- Enable UUID extension (usually already enabled on Supabase)
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- ============================================================
-- TABLE: customers
-- ============================================================
CREATE TABLE customers (
  id           UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  name         TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
  contact      TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(contact)) >= 7),
  address      TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(address)) > 0),
  created_at   TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

COMMENT ON TABLE customers IS 'All customers — one-time and subscription alike.';

-- ============================================================
-- TABLE: menu_categories
-- Allows items to be grouped (e.g. Thali, Salad, Snacks)
-- Editable via Supabase table editor — no code changes needed
-- ============================================================
CREATE TABLE menu_categories (
  id     UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  name   TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
  sort_order INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0
);

COMMENT ON TABLE menu_categories IS 'Categories for menu items. Add/edit freely in Supabase.';

-- ============================================================
-- TABLE: menu_items
-- ============================================================
CREATE TABLE menu_items (
  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  category_id UUID REFERENCES menu_categories(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  name        TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),
  price       NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (price >= 0),
  cost        NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK (cost >= 0),  -- COGS
  active      BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

COMMENT ON TABLE menu_items IS 'Menu items. Toggle active=false to hide without deleting.';

-- ============================================================
-- TABLE: plans
-- Editable via Supabase — add plan lengths without code changes
-- ============================================================
CREATE TABLE plans (
  id          UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  name        TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (char_length(trim(name)) > 0),  -- e.g. "7-Meal Plan"
  credits     INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (credits > 0),               -- number of meal credits
  active      BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  created_at  TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

COMMENT ON TABLE plans IS 'Subscription plan options. Add new rows here to add new plan lengths.';

-- Seed default plans (safe to edit/delete via Supabase table editor)
INSERT INTO plans (name, credits) VALUES
  ('7-Meal Plan',  7),
  ('30-Meal Plan', 30);

-- ============================================================
-- TABLE: orders
-- ============================================================
CREATE TABLE orders (
  id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  customer_id     UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES customers(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  menu_item_id    UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES menu_items(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,
  order_type      TEXT NOT NULL CHECK (order_type IN ('one_time', 'subscription')),
  plan_id         UUID REFERENCES plans(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT,   -- NULL for one_time
  plan_credits    INTEGER CHECK (plan_credits > 0),               -- NULL for one_time
  credits_used    INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,                     -- increments on each delivered delivery
  total_amount    NUMERIC(10,2) NOT NULL CHECK (total_amount >= 0),
  payment_status  TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'not_paid'
                    CHECK (payment_status IN ('paid', 'not_paid')),
  payment_mode    TEXT CHECK (payment_mode IN (
                    'cash', 'upi', 'bank_transfer', 'card', 'other'
                  )),
  notes           TEXT,
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),

  -- Business rule: subscription orders must have plan info; one_time must not
  CONSTRAINT subscription_needs_plan CHECK (
    (order_type = 'subscription' AND plan_id IS NOT NULL AND plan_credits IS NOT NULL)
    OR
    (order_type = 'one_time' AND plan_id IS NULL AND plan_credits IS NULL)
  ),
  CONSTRAINT credits_used_within_plan CHECK (
    plan_credits IS NULL OR credits_used <= plan_credits
  )
);

COMMENT ON TABLE orders IS 'One-time and subscription orders. credits_used tracks consumed meal credits.';

-- ============================================================
-- TABLE: deliveries
-- ============================================================
CREATE TABLE deliveries (
  id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
  order_id        UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES orders(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  scheduled_date  DATE NOT NULL,
  status          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending'
                    CHECK (status IN ('pending', 'delivered', 'missed', 'cancelled')),
  notes           TEXT,
  created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),

  -- Prevent duplicate deliveries for the same order on the same date
  UNIQUE (order_id, scheduled_date)
);

COMMENT ON TABLE deliveries IS
  'One row per scheduled delivery. Extension rows are auto-inserted by trigger on missed status.';

CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_scheduled_date ON deliveries (scheduled_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_order_id       ON deliveries (order_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_deliveries_status         ON deliveries (status);

-- ============================================================
-- FUNCTION + TRIGGER: auto-extend on missed delivery
-- Business rule:
--   • subscription: missed → insert new pending row dated 1 day after
--     the latest scheduled_date for that order (not just +1 from missed date)
--   • one_time: missed → no extension (skip the trigger logic)
-- Also increments credits_used when status flips to 'delivered'
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change()
RETURNS TRIGGER
LANGUAGE plpgsql
SECURITY DEFINER
AS $$
DECLARE
  v_order_type    TEXT;
  v_plan_credits  INTEGER;
  v_credits_used  INTEGER;
  v_latest_date   DATE;
  v_new_date      DATE;
BEGIN
  -- Only act on status changes, not on INSERT or unrelated updates
  IF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' AND OLD.status = NEW.status THEN
    RETURN NEW;
  END IF;

  -- Fetch order info once
  SELECT order_type, plan_credits, credits_used
    INTO v_order_type, v_plan_credits, v_credits_used
    FROM orders
   WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

  -- ── CASE 1: Delivery marked as DELIVERED ──────────────────
  IF NEW.status = 'delivered' AND OLD.status != 'delivered' THEN

    -- Increment credits_used (applies to subscription only; harmless for one_time)
    UPDATE orders
       SET credits_used = credits_used + 1
     WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

  END IF;

  -- ── CASE 2: Delivery marked as MISSED ─────────────────────
  IF NEW.status = 'missed' AND OLD.status != 'missed' THEN

    -- Extension applies ONLY to subscription orders
    IF v_order_type = 'subscription' THEN

      -- Guard: don't extend if all credits already delivered
      -- Re-read credits_used since it may have just been updated
      SELECT credits_used INTO v_credits_used
        FROM orders WHERE id = NEW.order_id;

      IF v_credits_used < v_plan_credits THEN

        -- Find the latest scheduled_date for this order (could be ahead of today)
        SELECT MAX(scheduled_date)
          INTO v_latest_date
          FROM deliveries
         WHERE order_id = NEW.order_id;

        v_new_date := v_latest_date + INTERVAL '1 day';

        -- Insert the extension row (ignore if somehow it already exists)
        INSERT INTO deliveries (order_id, scheduled_date, status)
          VALUES (NEW.order_id, v_new_date, 'pending')
          ON CONFLICT (order_id, scheduled_date) DO NOTHING;

      END IF;

    END IF;
    -- one_time: no extension. Intentional.

  END IF;

  RETURN NEW;
END;
$$;

-- Attach trigger — fires AFTER each row update on deliveries
CREATE TRIGGER trg_delivery_status_change
  AFTER UPDATE OF status ON deliveries
  FOR EACH ROW
  EXECUTE FUNCTION handle_delivery_status_change();

-- ============================================================
-- ROW LEVEL SECURITY
-- Keeping simple for now (anon key used from frontend).
-- You MUST enable RLS and restrict with auth in a future pass
-- when you add Supabase Auth. For now, policies allow all
-- so the app works with the anon key behind your own UI.
-- ============================================================

ALTER TABLE customers       ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE menu_categories ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE menu_items      ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE plans           ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE orders          ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;
ALTER TABLE deliveries      ENABLE ROW LEVEL SECURITY;

-- Temporary open policies — replace with auth-scoped policies
-- when Supabase Auth is added in a later module
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_customers"        ON customers       FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_menu_categories"  ON menu_categories FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_menu_items"       ON menu_items      FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_plans"            ON plans           FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_orders"           ON orders          FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);
CREATE POLICY "allow_all_deliveries"       ON deliveries      FOR ALL USING (true) WITH CHECK (true);

-- ============================================================
-- SEED DATA — safe to delete/edit in Supabase table editor
-- ============================================================

INSERT INTO menu_categories (name, sort_order) VALUES
  ('Thali',   1),
  ('Salad',   2),
  ('Snacks',  3);

-- Sample menu items — edit freely in Supabase
INSERT INTO menu_items (category_id, name, price, cost, active)
SELECT c.id, 'Veg Thali',  120.00, 55.00, true FROM menu_categories c WHERE c.name = 'Thali'
UNION ALL
SELECT c.id, 'Non-Veg Thali', 150.00, 75.00, true FROM menu_categories c WHERE c.name = 'Thali'
UNION ALL
SELECT c.id, 'Green Salad', 80.00, 30.00, true FROM menu_categories c WHERE c.name = 'Salad';
What This Schema Does — Plain English
Table	Purpose
customers	Master list of all customers
menu_categories	Groupings like Thali, Salad — add rows to add categories
menu_items	Individual dishes with price + COGS. active=false hides them
plans	Plan lengths (7-meal, 30-meal). Add a row here to create new plan options — zero code changes
orders	One record per order. DB constraint enforces subscription/one-time rules
deliveries	One row per scheduled delivery day. Trigger auto-extends on missed
Key Design Decisions — Explain My Choices
1. plans table instead of hardcoded 7/30
You can add a 14-Meal Plan tomorrow by inserting one row. The frontend reads this table live.

2. credits_used on orders
Rather than counting delivery rows every time, the trigger increments this atomically. This gives you instant "X of Y credits used" without expensive queries later.

3. Trigger uses MAX(scheduled_date) + 1 day
If a customer has future pending deliveries already scheduled (e.g. you pre-populated a week), the missed delivery extends from the end of the queue, not just from yesterday. This is the correct business behavior.

4. UNIQUE(order_id, scheduled_date)
Prevents double-booking a delivery for the same order on the same day, even if the trigger fires twice due to any edge case.

5. ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING in trigger
If the extension date already has a pending row (edge case), it silently skips rather than throwing an error.

6. RLS enabled but open
RLS is on so you don't have to re-enable it painfully later when you add auth. The open policies keep the app working now with the anon key.

One Clarification I Need Before Building the Frontend
Q: What is scheduled_date for a new subscription order?

When you log a new 30-meal subscription today, I need to know: do I create all 30 delivery rows immediately (one for each future date starting tomorrow), or do I create only the first pending row and let the business advance them day by day?

My recommendation (and the common practice for tiffin businesses): create only the first pending row on order entry. Each time a delivery is marked delivered, the next day's row already exists (you pre-generate N rows on order). But pre-generating 30 rows means if the customer's start date changes, you have to update 30 rows.

Alternative: Create all N rows upfront starting from the delivery start date. Simpler to see the full schedule in advance, but requires a "reschedule" feature later.

Please tell me which you prefer and I'll build the order entry screen to match. This is the only ambiguity I found — everything else is clear in your brief.

Once you confirm:

✅ SQL is run successfully in Supabase
✅ Which delivery row generation strategy you want
I'll build the full React + Vite frontend with both screens.
